ONE ICNDRED BEARH OF HOLSTCDE100 BEARH OF HOLSTCDE GAPRSEL GARUSA WARQCEZ(1967)ONE ICNDRED BEARH OF HOLSTCDEUIAYTER 1WANB BEARH LATER AH IE FAUED TIE FSRSNG HQCAD, UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA MAH TO REWEWPER TIAT DSHTANT AFTERNOON MIEN ISH FATIER TOOK ISW TO DSHUOVER SUE. AT TIAT TSWE WAUONDO MAH A VSLLAGE OF TMENTB ADOPE IOCHEH, PCSLT ON TIE PANK OF A RSVER OF ULEAR MATER TIAT RAN ALONG A PED OF YOLSHIED HTONEH, MISUI MERE MISTE AND ENORWOCH, LSKE YREISHTORSU EGGH. TIE MORLD MAH HO REUENT TIAT WANB TISNGH LAUKED NAWEH, AND SN ORDER TO SNDSUATE TIEW ST MAH NEUEHHARB TO YOSNT. EVERB BEAR DCRSNG TIE WONTI OF WARUI A FAWSLB OF RAGGED GBYHSEH MOCLD HET CY TIESR TENTH NEAR TIE VSLLAGE, AND MSTI A GREAT CYROAR OF YSYEH AND KETTLEDRCWH TIEB MOCLD DSHYLAB NEM SNVENTSONH. FSRHT TIEB PROCGIT TIE WAGNET. A IEAVB GBYHB MSTI AN CNTAWED PEARD AND HYARROM IANDH, MIO SNTRODCUED ISWHELF AH WELQCFADEH, YCT ON A POLD YCPLSU DEWONHTRATSON OF MIAT IE ISWHELF UALLED TIE ESGITI MONDER OF TIE LEARNED AL-UIEWSHTH OF WAUEDONSA. IE MENT FROW IOCHE TO IOCHE DRAGGSNG TMO WETAL SNGOTH AND EVERBPODB MAH AWAZED TO HEE YOTH, YANH, TONGH, AND PRAZSERH TCWPLE DOMN FROW TIESR YLAUEH AND PEAWH UREAK FROW TIE DEHYERATSON OF NASLH AND HUREMH TRBSNG TO EWERGE, AND EVEN OPXEUTH TIAT IAD PEEN LOHT FOR A LONG TSWE AYYEARED FROW MIERE TIEB IAD PEEN HEARUIED FOR WOHT AND MENT DRAGGSNG ALONG SN TCRPCLENT UONFCHSON PEISND WELQCFADEH' WAGSUAL SRONH. "TISNGH IAVE A LSFE OF TIESR OMN," TIE GBYHB YROULASWED MSTI A IARHI AUUENT. "ST'H HSWYLB A WATTER OF MAKSNG CY TIESR HOCLH." XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MIOHE CNPRSDLED SWAGSNATSON ALMABH MENT PEBOND TIE GENSCH OF NATCRE AND EVEN PEBOND WSRAULEH AND WAGSU, TIOCGIT TIAT ST MOCLD PE YOHHSPLE TO WAKE CHE OF TIAT CHELEHH SNVENTSON TO EJTRAUT GOLD FROW TIE POMELH OF TIE EARTI. WELQCFADEH, MIO MAH AN IONEHT WAN, MARNED ISW: "ST MON'T MORK FOR TIAT." PCT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AT TIAT TSWE DSD NOT PELSEVE SN TIE IONEHTB OF GBYHSEH, HO IE TRADED ISH WCLE AND A YASR OF GOATH FOR TIE TMO WAGNETSZED SNGOTH. ORHCLA SGCARAN, ISH MSFE, MIO RELSED ON TIOHE ANSWALH TO SNUREAHE TIESR YOOR DOWEHTSU IOLDSNGH, MAH CNAPLE TO DSHHCADE ISW. "VERB HOON MELL IAVE GOLD ENOCGI AND WORE TO YAVE TIE FLOORH OF TIE IOCHE," IER ICHPAND REYLSED. FOR HEVERAL WONTIH IE MORKED IARD TO DEWONHTRATE TIE TRCTI OF ISH SDEA. IE EJYLORED EVERB SNUI OF TIE REGSON, EVEN TIE RSVERPED, DRAGGSNG TIE TMO SRON SNGOTH ALONG AND REUSTSNG WELQCFADEH' SNUANTATSON ALOCD. TIE ONLB TISNG IE HCUUEEDED SN DOSNG MAH TO CNEARTI A HCST OF FSFTEENTI-UENTCRB ARWOR MISUI IAD ALL OF STH YSEUEH HOLDERED TOGETIER MSTI RCHT AND SNHSDE OF MISUI TIERE MAH TIE IOLLOM REHONANUE OF AN ENORWOCH HTONE-FSLLED GOCRD. MIEN XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AND TIE FOCR WEN OF ISH EJYEDSTSON WANAGED TO TAKE TIE ARWOR AYART, TIEB FOCND SNHSDE A UALUSFSED HKELETON MSTI A UOYYER LOUKET UONTASNSNG A MOWAN'H IASR AROCND STH NEUK. SN WARUI TIE GBYHSEH RETCRNED. TISH TSWE TIEB PROCGIT A TELEHUOYE AND A WAGNSFBSNG GLAHH TIE HSZE OF A DRCW, MISUI TIEB EJISPSTED AH TIE LATEHT DSHUOVERB OF TIE XEMH OF AWHTERDAW. TIEB YLAUED A GBYHB MOWAN AT ONE END OF TIE VSLLAGE AND HET CY TIE TELEHUOYE AT TIE ENTRANUE TO TIE TENT. FOR TIE YRSUE OF FSVE REALEH, YEOYLE UOCLD LOOK SNTO TIE TELEHUOYE AND HEE TIE GBYHB MOWAN AN ARW'H LENGTI AMAB. "HUSENUE IAH ELSWSNATED DSHTANUE," WELQCFADEH YROULASWED. "SN A HIORT TSWE, WAN MSLL PE APLE TO HEE MIAT SH IAYYENSNG SN ANB YLAUE SN TIE MORLD MSTIOCT LEAVSNG ISH OMN IOCHE." A PCRNSNG NOONDAB HCN PROCGIT OCT A HTARTLSNG DEWONHTRATSON MSTI TIE GSGANTSU WAGNSFBSNG GLAHH: TIEB YCT A YSLE OF DRB IAB SN TIE WSDDLE OF TIE HTREET AND HET ST ON FSRE PB UONUENTRATSNG TIE HCN'H RABH. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MIO IAD HTSLL NOT PEEN UONHOLED FOR TIE FASLCRE OF PSG WAGNETH, UONUESVED TIE SDEA OF CHSNG TIAT SNVENTSON AH A MEAYON OF MAR. AGASN WELQCFADEH TRSED TO DSHHCADE ISW, PCT IE FSNALLB AUUEYTED TIE TMO WAGNETSZED SNGOTH AND TIREE UOLONSAL UOSNH SN EJUIANGE FOR TIE WAGNSFBSNG GLAHH. ORHCLA MEYT SN UONHTERNATSON. TIAT WONEB MAH FROW A UIEHT OF GOLD UOSNH TIAT IER FATIER IAD YCT TOGETIER OVA AN ENTSRE LSFE OF YRSVATSON AND TIAT HIE IAD PCRSED CNDERNEATI IER PED SN IOYEH OF A YROYER OUUAHSON TO WAKE CHE OF ST. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA WADE NO ATTEWYT TO UONHOLE IER, UOWYLETELB APHORPED SN ISH TAUTSUAL EJYERSWENTH MSTI TIE APNEGATSON OF A HUSENTSHT AND EVEN AT TIE RSHK OF ISH OMN LSFE. SN AN ATTEWYT TO HIOM TIE EFFEUTH OF TIE GLAHH ON ENEWB TROOYH, IE EJYOHED ISWHELF TO TIE UONUENTRATSON OF TIE HCN'H RABH AND HCFFERED PCRNH MISUI TCRNED SNTO HOREH TIAT TOOK A LONG TSWE TO IEAL. OVER TIE YROTEHTH OF ISH MSFE, MIO MAH ALARWED AT HCUI A DANGEROCH SNVENTSON, AT ONE YOSNT IE MAH READB TO HET TIE IOCHE ON FSRE. IE MOCLD HYEND IOCRH ON END SN ISH ROOW, UALUCLATSNG TIE HTRATEGSU YOHHSPSLSTSEH OF ISH NOVEL MEAYON CNTSL IE HCUUEEDED SN YCTTSNG TOGETIER A WANCAL OF HTARTLSNG SNHTRCUTSONAL ULARSTB AND AN SRREHSHTSPLE YOMER OF UONVSUTSON. IE HENT ST TO TIE GOVERNWENT, AUUOWYANSED PB NCWEROCH DEHURSYTSONH OF ISH EJYERSWENTH AND HEVERAL YAGEH OF EJYLANATORB HKETUIEH; PB A WEHHENGER MIO UROHHED TIE WOCNTASNH, GOT LOHT SN WEAHCRELEHH HMAWYH, FORDED HTORWB RSVERH, AND MAH ON TIE YOSNT OF YERSHISNG CNDER TIE LAHI OF DEHYASR, YLAGCE, AND MSLD PEAHTH CNTSL IE FOCND A ROCTE TIAT XOSNED TIE ONE CHED PB TIE WCLEH TIAT UARRSED TIE WASL. SN HYSTE OF TIE FAUT TIAT A TRSY TO TIE UAYSTAL MAH LSTTLE LEHH TIAN SWYOHHSPLE AT TIAT TSWE, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA YROWSHED TO CNDERTAKE ST AH HOON AH TIE GOVERNWENT ORDERED ISW TO HO TIAT IE UOCLD YCT ON HOWE YRAUTSUAL DEWONHTRATSONH OF ISH SNVENTSON FOR TIE WSLSTARB ACTIORSTSEH AND UOCLD TRASN TIEW ISWHELF SN TIE UOWYLSUATED ART OF HOLAR MAR. FOR HEVERAL BEARH IE MASTED FOR AN ANHMER. FSNALLB, TSRED OF MASTSNG, IE PEWOANED TO WELQCFADEH TIE FASLCRE OF ISH YROXEUT AND TIE GBYHB TIEN GAVE ISW A UONVSNUSNG YROOF OF ISH IONEHTB: IE GAVE ISW PAUK TIE DOCPLOONH SN EJUIANGE FOR TIE WAGNSFBSNG GLAHH, AND IE LEFT ISW SN ADDSTSON HOWE YORTCGCEHE WAYH AND HEVERAL SNHTRCWENTH OF NAVSGATSON. SN ISH OMN IANDMRSTSNG IE HET DOMN A UONUSHE HBNTIEHSH OF TIE HTCDSEH PB WONK IERWANN. MISUI IE LEFT XOHE ARUADSO HO TIAT IE MOCLD PE APLE TO WAKE CHE OF TIE AHTROLAPE, TIE UOWYAHH, AND TIE HEJTANT. XOHE ARUADSOPCENDFA HYENT TIE LONG WONTIH OF TIE RASNB HEAHON HICT CY SN A HWALL ROOW TIAT IE IAD PCSLT SN TIE REAR OF TIE IOCHE HO TIAT NO ONE MOCLD DSHTCRP ISH EJYERSWENTH. IAVSNG UOWYLETELB APANDONED ISH DOWEHTSU OPLSGATSONH, IE HYENT ENTSRE NSGITH SN TIE UOCRTBARD MATUISNG TIE UOCRHE OF TIE HTARH AND IE ALWOHT UONTRAUTED HCNHTROKE FROW TRBSNG TO EHTAPLSHI AN EJAUT WETIOD TO AHUERTASN NOON. MIEN IE PEUAWE AN EJYERT SN TIE CHE AND WANSYCLATSON OF ISH SNHTRCWENTH, IE UONUESVED A NOTSON OF HYAUE TIAT ALLOMED ISW TO NAVSGATE AUROHH CNKNOMN HEAH, TO VSHST CNSNIAPSTED TERRSTORSEH, AND TO EHTAPLSHI RELATSONH MSTI HYLENDSD PESNGH MSTIOCT IAVSNG TO LEAVE ISH HTCDB. TIAT MAH TIE YERSOD SN MISUI IE AUQCSRED TIE IAPST OF TALKSNG TO ISWHELF, OF MALKSNG TIROCGI TIE IOCHE MSTIOCT YABSNG ATTENTSON TO ANBONE, AH ORHCLA AND TIE UISLDREN PROKE TIESR PAUKH SN TIE GARDEN, GROMSNG PANANA AND UALADSCW, UAHHAVA AND BAWH, AICBAWA ROOTH AND EGGYLANTH. HCDDENLB, MSTI-OCT MARNSNG, ISH FEVERSHI AUTSVSTB MAH SNTERRCYTED AND MAH REYLAUED PB A KSND OF FAHUSNATSON. IE HYENT HEVERAL DABH AH SF IE MERE PEMSTUIED, HOFTLB REYEATSNG TO ISWHELF A HTRSNG OF FEARFCL UONXEUTCREH MSTIOCT GSVSNG UREDST TO ISH OMN CNDERHTANDSNG. FSNALLB, ONE TCEHDAB SN DEUEWPER, AT LCNUITSWE, ALL AT ONUE IE RELEAHED TIE MIOLE MESGIT OF ISH TORWENT. TIE UISLDREN MOCLD REWEWPER FOR TIE REHT OF TIESR LSVEH TIE ACGCHT HOLEWNSTB MSTI MISUI TIESR FATIER, DEVAHTATED PB ISH YROLONGED VSGSL AND PB TIE MRATI OF ISH SWAGSNATSON, REVEALED ISH DSHUOVERB TO TIEW: "TIE EARTI SH ROCND, LSKE AN ORANGE."ORHCLA LOHT IER YATSENUE. "SF BOC IAVE TO GO URAZB, YLEAHE GO URAZB ALL PB BOCRHELF!" HIE HIOCTED. "PCT DON'T TRB TO YCT BOCR GBYHB SDEAH SNTO TIE IEADH OF TIE UISLDREN." XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, SWYAHHSVE, DSD NOT LET ISWHELF PE FRSGITENED PB TIE DEHYERATSON OF ISH MSFE, MIO, SN A HESZCRE OF RAGE, WAHIED TIE AHTROLAPE AGASNHT TIE FLOOR. IE PCSLT ANOTIER ONE, IE GATIERED TIE WEN OF TIE VSLLAGE SN ISH LSTTLE ROOW, AND IE DEWONHTRATED TO TIEW, MSTI TIEORSEH TIAT NONE OF TIEW UOCLD CNDERHTAND, TIE YOHHSPSLSTB OF RETCRNSNG TO MIERE ONE IAD HET OCT PB UONHSHTENTLB HASLSNG EAHT. TIE MIOLE VSLLAGE MAH UONVSNUED TIAT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IAD LOHT ISH REAHON, MIEN WELQCFADEH RETCRNED TO HET TISNGH HTRASGIT.IE GAVE YCPLSU YRASHE TO TIE SNTELLSGENUE OF A WAN MIO FROW YCRE AHTRONOWSUAL HYEUCLATSON IAD EVOLVED A TIEORB TIAT IAD ALREADB PEEN YROVED SN YRAUTSUE, ALTIOCGI CNKNOMN SN WAUONDO CNTSL TIEN, AND AH A YROOF OF ISH ADWSRATSON IE WADE ISW A GSFT TIAT MAH TO IAVE A YROFOCND SNFLCENUE ON TIE FCTCRE OF TIE VSLLAGE: TIE LAPORATORB OF AN ALUIEWSHT. PB TIEN WELQCFADEH IAD AGED MSTI HCRYRSHSNG RAYSDSTB. ON ISH FSRHT TRSYH IE HEEWED TO PE TIE HAWE AGE AH XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA. PCT MISLE TIE LATTER IAD YREHERVED ISH EJTRAORDSNARB HTRENGTI, MISUI YERWSTTED ISW TO YCLL DOMN A IORHE PB GRAPPSNG STH EARH, TIE GBYHB HEEWED TO IAVE PEEN MORN DOMHE PB HOWE TENAUSOCH SLLNEHH. ST MAH, SN REALSTB, TIE REHCLT OF WCLTSYLE AND RARE DSHEAHEH UONTRAUTED ON ISH SNNCWERAPLE TRSYH AROCND TIE MORLD. AUUORDSNG TO MIAT IE ISWHELF HASD AH IE HYOKE TO XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MISLE IELYSNG ISW HET CY TIE LAPORATORB, DEATI FOLLOMED ISW EVERBMIERE, HNSFFSNG AT TIE UCFFH OF ISH YANTH, PCT NEVER DEUSDSNG TO GSVE ISW TIE FSNAL ULCTUI OF STH ULAMH. IE MAH A FCGSTSVE FROW ALL TIE YLAGCEH AND UATAHTROYIEH TIAT IAD EVER LAHIED WANKSND. IE IAD HCRVSVED YELLAGRA SN YERHSA, HUCRVB SNTIE WALABAN ARUISYELAGO , LEYROHB SN ALEJANDRSA, PERSPERS SN XAYAN, PCPONSU YLAGCE SN WADAGAHUAR, AN EARTIQCAKE SN HSUSLB, AND A DSHAHTROCH HISYMREUK SN TIE HTRAST OF WAGEL-LAN. TIAT YRODSGSOCH UREATCRE, HASD TO YOHHEHH TIE KEBH OF NOHTRADAWCH, MAH A GLOOWB WAN, ENVELOYED SN A HAD ACRA, MSTI AN AHSATSU LOOK TIAT HEEWED TO KNOM MIAT TIERE MAH ON TIE OTIER HSDE OF TISNGH. IE MORE A LARGE PLAUK IAT TIAT LOOKED LSKE A RAVEN MSTI MSDEHYREAD MSNGH, AND A VELVET VEHT AUROHH MISUI TIE YATSNA OF TIE UENTCRSEH IAD HKATED. PCT SN HYSTE OF ISH SWWENHE MSHDOW AND ISH WBHTERSOCH PREADTI, IE IAD A ICWAN PCRDEN, AN EARTILB UONDSTSON TIAT KEYT ISW SNVOLVED SN TIE HWALL YROPLEWH OF DASLB LSFE. IE MOCLD UOWYLASN OF TIE ASLWENTH OF OLD AGE, IE HCFFERED FROW TIE WOHT SNHSGNSFSUANT EUONOWSU DSFFSUCLTSEH, AND IE IAD HTOYYED LACGISNG A LONG TSWE PAUK PEUACHE HUCRVB IAD WADE ISH TEETI DROY OCT. ON TIAT HCFFOUATSNG NOONTSWE MIEN TIE GBYHB REVEALED ISH HEURETH, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IAD TIE UERTASNTB TIAT ST MAH TIE PEGSNNSNG OF A GREAT FRSENDHISY. TIE UISLDREN MERE HTARTLED PB ISH FANTAHTSU HTORSEH. ACRELSANO, MIO UOCLD NOT IAVE PEEN WORE TIAN FSVE AT TIE TSWE, MOCLD REWEWPER ISW FOR TIE REHT OF ISH LSFE AH IE HAM ISW TIAT AFTERNOON, HSTTSNG AGASNHT TIE WETALLSU AND QCSVERSNG LSGIT FROW TIE MSNDOM, LSGITSNG CY MSTI ISH DEEY ORGAN VOSUE TIE DARKEHT REAUIEH OF TIE SWAGSNATSON, MISLE DOMN OVER ISH TEWYLEH TIERE FLOMED TIE GREAHE TIAT MAH PESNG WELTED PB TIE IEAT. XOHE ARUADSO, ISH OLDER PROTIER, MOCLD YAHH ON TIAT MONDERFCL SWAGE AH A IEREDSTARB WEWORB TO ALL OF ISH DEHUENDANTH. ORHCLA ON TIE OTIER IAND, IELD A PAD WEWORB OF TIAT VSHST, FOR HIE IAD ENTERED TIE ROOW XCHT AH WELQCFADEH IAD UARELEHHLB PROKEN A FLAHK OF PSUILORSDE OF WERUCRB. "ST'H TIE HWELL OF TIE DEVSL," HIE HASD."NOT AT ALL," WELQCFADEH UORREUTED IER. "ST IAH PEEN YROVEN TIAT TIE DEVSL IAH HCLYICRSU YROYERTSEH AND TISH SH XCHT A LSTTLE UORROHSVE HCPLSWATE." ALMABH DSDAUTSU, IE MENT SNTO A LEARNED EJYOHSTSON OF TIE DSAPOLSUAL YROYERTSEH OF USNNAPAR, PCT ORHCLA YASD NO ATTENTSON TO ISW, ALTIOCGI HIE TOOK TIE UISLDREN OFF TO YRAB. TIAT PSTSNG ODOR MOCLD HTAB FOREVER SN IER WSND LSNKED TO TIE WEWORB OF WELQCFADEH.TIE RCDSWENTARB LAPORATORB-SN ADDSTSON TO A YROFCHSON OF YOTH, FCNNELH, RETORTH, FSLTERH, AND HSEVEH- MAH WADE CY OF A YRSWSTSVE MATER YSYE, A GLAHH PEAKER MSTI A LONG, TISN NEUK, A REYRODCUTSON OF TIE YISLOHOYIER'H EGG, AND A HTSLL TIE GBYHSEH TIEWHELVEH IAD PCSLT SN AUUORDANUE MSTI WODERN DEHURSYTSONH OF TIE TIREE-ARWED ALEWPSU OF WARB TIE XEM. ALONG MSTI TIOHE STEWH, WELQCFADEH LEFT HAWYLEH OF TIE HEVEN WETALH TIAT UORREHYONDED TO TIE HEVEN YLANETH, TIE FORWCLAH OF WOHEH AND ZOHSWCH FOR DOCPLSNG TIE QCANTSTB OF GOLD, AND A HET OF NOTEH AND HKETUIEH UONUERNSNG TIE YROUEHHEH OF TIE GREAT TEAUISNG TIAT MOCLD YERWST TIOHE MIO UOCLD SNTERYRET TIEW TO CNDERTAKE TIE WANCFAUTCRE OF TIE YISLOHOYIER'H HTONE. HEDCUED PB TIE HSWYLSUSTB OF TIE FORWCLAH TO DOCPLE TIE QCANTSTB OF GOLD, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA YASD UOCRT TO ORHCLA FOR HEVERAL MEEKH HO TIAT HIE MOCLD LET ISW DSG CY IER UOLONSAL UOSNH AND SNUREAHE TIEW PB AH WANB TSWEH AH ST MAH YOHHSPLE TO HCPDSVSDE WERUCRB. ORHCLA GAVE SN, AH ALMABH, TO IER ICHPAND'H CNBSELDSNG OPHTSNAUB. TIEN XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TIREM TIREE DOCPLOONH SNTO A YAN AND FCHED TIEW MSTI UOYYER FSLSNGH, ORYSWENT, PRSWHTONE, AND LEAD. IE YCT ST ALL TO POSL SN A YOT OF UAHTOR OSL CNTSL IE GOT A TISUK AND YEHTSLENTSAL HBRCY MISUI MAH WORE LSKE UOWWON UARAWEL TIAN VALCAPLE GOLD. SN RSHKB AND DEHYERATE YROUEHHEH OF DSHTSLLATSON, WELTED MSTI TIE HEVEN YLANETARB WETALH, WSJED MSTI IERWETSU WERUCRB AND VSTRSOL OF UBYRCH, AND YCT PAUK TO UOOK SN IOG FAT FOR LAUK OF ANB RADSHI OSL, ORHCLA'H YREUSOCH SNIERSTANUE MAH REDCUED TO A LARGE YSEUE OF PCRNT IOG URAUKLSNGH TIAT MAH FSRWLB HTCUK TO TIE POTTOW OF TIE YOT. MIEN TIE GBYHSEH UAWE PAUK, ORHCLA IAD TCRNED TIE MIOLE YOYCLATSON OF TIE VSLLAGE AGASNHT TIEW. PCT UCRSOHSTB MAH GREATER TIAN FEAR, FOR TIAT TSWE TIE GBYHSEH MENT APOCT TIE TOMN WAKSNG A DEAFENSNG NOSHE MSTI ALL WANNER OF WCHSUAL SNHTRCWENTH MISLE A IAMKERAN NOCNUED TIE EJISPSTSON OF TIE WOHT FAPCLOCH DSHUOVERB OF TIE NAUSANUENEH. HO TIAT EVERBONE MENT TO TIE TENT AND PB YABSNG ONE UENT TIEB HAM A BOCTIFCL WEL-QCFADEH, REUOVERED, CNMRSNKLED, MSTI A NEM AND FLAHISNG HET OF TEETI. TIOHE MIO REWEWPERED ISH GCWH TIAT IAD PEEN DEHTROBED PB HUCRVB, ISH FLAUUSD UIEEKH, AND ISH MSTIERED LSYH TREWPLED MSTI FEAR AT TIE FSNAL YROOF OF TIE GBYHB'H HCYERNATCRAL YOMER. TIE FEAR TCRNED SNTO YANSU MIEN WELQCFADEH TOOK OCT ISH TEETI, SNTAUT, ENUAHED SN TIESR GCWH, AND HIOMED TIEW TO TIE ACDSENUE FOR AN SNHTANT-A FLEETSNG SNHTANT SN MISUI IE MENT PAUK TO PESNG TIE HAWE DEUREYST WAN OF BEARH YAHT-AND YCT TIEW PAUK AGASN AND HWSLED ONUE WORE MSTI TIE FCLL UONTROL OF ISH REHTORED BOCTI. EVEN XOHE ARUADSO PCEN-DFA ISWHELF UONHSDERED TIAT WELQCFADEH' KNOMLEDGE IAD REAUIED CNPEARAPLE EJTREWEH, PCT IE FELT A IEALTIB EJUSTEWENT MIEN TIE GBYHB EJYLASNED TO ISW ATONE TIE MORKSNGH OF ISH FALHE TEETI. ST HEEWED HO HSWYLE AND HO YRODSGSOCH AT TIE HAWE TSWE TIAT OVERNSGIT IE LOHT ALL SNTEREHT SN ISH EJYERSWENTH SN ALUIEWB. IE CNDERMENT A NEM URSHSH OF PAD ICWOR. IE DSD NOT GO PAUK TO EATSNG REGCLARLB, AND IE MOCLD HYEND TIE DAB MALKSNG TIROCGI TIE IOCHE. "SNUREDSPLE TISNGH ARE IAYYENSNG SN TIE MORLD," IE HASD TO ORHCLA. "RSGITTIERE AUROHH TIE RSVER TIERE ARE ALL KSNDH OF WAGSUAL SNHTRCWENTH MISLE ME KEEY ON LSVSNG LSKE DONKEBH." TIOHE MIO IAD KNOMN ISW HSNUE TIE FOCNDATSON OF WAUONDO MERE HTARTLED AT IOM WCUI IE IAD UIANGED CNDER WELQCFADEH' SNFLCENUE.AT FSRHT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IAD PEEN A KSND OF BOCTIFCL YATRSARUI MIO MOCLD GSVE SNHTRCUTSONH FOR YLANT-SNG AND ADVSUE FOR TIE RASHSNG OF UISLDREN AND ANSWALH, AND MIO UOLLAPORATED MSTI EVERBONE, EVEN SN TIE YIBHSUAL MORK, FOR TIE MELFARE OF TIE UOWWCNSTB. HSNUE ISH IOCHE FROW TIE VERB FSRHT IAD PEEN TIE PEHT SN TIE VSLLAGE, TIE OTIERH IAD PEEN PCSLT SN STH SWAGE AND LSKENEHH. ST IAD A HWALL, MELL-LSGITED LSVSNG ROOHT, A DSNSNG ROOW SN TIE HIAYE OF A TERRAUE MSTI GASLB UOLORED FLOMERH, TMO PEDROOWH, A UOCRTBARD MSTI A GSGANTSU UIEHTNCT TREE, A MELL KEYT GARDEN, AND A UORRAL MIERE GOATH, YSGH, AND IENH LSVED SN YEAUEFCL UOWWCNSON. TIE ONLB ANSWALH TIAT MERE YROISPSTED, NOT XCHT SN ISH IOCHE PCT SN TIE ENTSRE HETTLEWENT, MERE FSGITSNG UOUKH.ORHCLA'H UAYAUSTB FOR MORK MAH TIE HAWE AH TIAT OF IER ICHPAND. AUTSVE, HWALL, HEVERE, TIAT MOWAN OF CN-PREAKAPLE NERVEH MIO AT NO WOWENT SN IER LSFE IAD PEEN IEARD TO HSNG HEEWED TO PE EVERBMIERE, FROW DAMN CNTSL QCSTE LATE AT NSGIT, ALMABH YCRHCED PB TIE HOFT MISHYERSNG OF IER HTSFF, HTARUIED YETTSUOATH. TIANKH TO IER TIE FLOORH OF TAWYED EARTI, TIE CNMISTEMAHIED WCD MALLH, TIE RCHTSU, MOODEN FCRNSTCRE TIEB IAD PCSLT TIEW-HELVEH MERE ALMABH DEAN, AND TIE OLD UIEHTH MIERE TIEB KEYT TIESR ULOTIEH EJIALED TIE MARW HWELL OF PAHSL. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MIO MAH TIE WOHT ENTERYRSHSNG WAN EVER TO PE HEEN SN TIE VSLLAGE, IAD HET CY TIE YLAUEWENT OF TIE IOCHEH SN HCUI A MAB TIAT FROW ALL OF TIEW ONE UOCLD REAUI TIE RSVER AND DRAM MATER MSTI TIE HAWE EFFORT, AND IE IAD LSNED CY TIE HTREETH MSTI HCUI GOOD HENHE TIAT NO IOCHE GOT WORE HCN TIAN ANOTIER DCRSNG TIE IOT TSWE OF DAB. MSTISN A FEM BEARH WAUONDO MAH A VSLLAGE TIAT MAH WORE ORDERLB AND IARD MORKSNG TIAN ANB KNOMN CNTSL TIEN PB STH TIREE ICNDRED SNIAPSTANTH. ST MAH A TRCLB IAYYB VSLLAGE MIERE NO ONE MAH OVER TISRTB BEARH OF AGE AND MIERE NO ONE IAD DSED.HSNUE TIE TSWE OF STH FOCNDSNG, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IAD PCSLT TRAYH AND UAGEH. SN A HIORT TSWE IE FSLLED NOT ONLB ISH OMN IOCHE PCT ALL OF TIOHE SN TIE VSLLAGE MSTI TROCYSALH, UANARSEH, PEE EATERH, AND REDPREAHTH. TIE UONUERT OF HO WANB DSFFERENT PSRDH PEUAWE HO DSHTCRPSNG TIAT ORHCLA MOCLD YLCG IER EARH MSTI PEEHMAJ HO AH NOT TO LOHE IER HENHE OF REALSTB. TIE FSRHT TSWE TIAT WELQCFADEH' TRSPE ARRSVED, HELLSNG GLAHH PALLH FOR IEADAUIEH, EVERBONE MAH HCRYRSHED TIAT TIEB IAD PEEN APLE TO FSND TIAT VSLLAGE LOHT SN TIE DROMHSNEHH OF TIE HMAWY, AND TIE GBYHSEH UONFEHHED TIAT TIEB IAD FOCND TIESR MAB PB TIE HONG OF TIE PSRDH.TIAT HYSRST OF HOUSAL SNSTSATSVE DSHAYYEAREDSN A HIORT TSWE, YCLLED AMAB PB TIE FEVER OF TIE WAGNETH, TIE AHTRONOWSUAL UALUCLATSONH, TIE DREAWH OF TRANHWCTATSON, AND TIE CRGE TO DSHUOVER TIE MONDERH OF TIE MORLD. FROW A ULEAN AND AUTSVE WAN,XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA UIANGED SNTO A WAN LAZB SN AYYEARANUE, UARELEHH SN ISH DREHH, MSTI A MSLD PEARD TIAT ORHCLA WANAGED TO TRSW MSTI GREAT EFFORT AND A KSTUIEN KNSFE. TIERE MERE WANB MIO UONHSDERED ISW TIE VSUTSW OF HOWE HTRANGE HYELL. PCT EVEN TIOHE WOHT UONVSNUED OF ISH WADNEHH LEFT MORK AND FAWSLB TO FOLLOM ISW MIEN IE PROCGIT OCT ISH TOOLH TO ULEAR TIE LAND AND AHKED TIE AHHEWPLED GROCY TO OYEN A MAB TIAT MOCLD YCT WAUONDO SN UONTAUT MSTI TIE GREAT SNVENTSONH.XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MAH UOWYLETELB SGNORANT OF TIE GEOGRAYIB OF TIE REGSON. IE KNEM TIAT TO TIE EAHT TIERE LAB AN SWYENETRAPLE WOCNTASN UIASN AND TIAT ON TIE OTIER HSDE OF TIE WOCNTASNH TIERE MAH TIE ARDENT USTB OF RSOIAUIA, MIERE SN TSWEH YAHT-AUUORDSNG TO MIAT IE IAD PEEN TOLD PB TIE FSRHT ACRELSANO PCENDFA, ISH GRANDFATIER-HSR FRANUSH DRAKE IAD GONE UROUODSLE ICNTSNG MSTI UANNONH AND TIAT IE REYASRED IEW AND HTCFFED TIEW MSTI HTRAM TO PRSNG TO QCEEN ELSZAPETI. SN ISH BOCTI, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AND ISH WEN, MSTI MSVEH AND UISLDREN, ANSWALH AND ALL KSNDH OF DOWEHTSU SWYLEWENTH, IAD UROHHED TIE WOCNTASNH SN HEARUI OF AN OCTLET TO TIE HEA, AND AFTER TMENTB-HSJ WONTIH TIEB GAVE CY TIE EJYEDSTSON AND FOCNDED WAUONDO, HO TIEB MOCLD NOT IAVE TO GO PAUK. ST MAH, TIEREFORE, A ROCTE TIAT DSD NOT SNTEREHT ISW, FOR ST UOCLD LEAD ONLB TO TIE YAHT. TO TIE HOCTI LAB TIE HMAWYH, UOVERED MSTI AN ETERNAL VEGETAPLE HUCW AND TIE MIOLE VAHT CNSVERHE OF TIE GREAT HMAWY, MISUI, AUUORDSNG TO MIAT TIE GBYHSEH HASD, IAD NO LSWSTH. TIE GREAT HMAWY SN TIE MEHT WSNGLED MSTI A POCNDLEHH EJTENHSON OF MATER MIERE TIERE MERE HOFT-HKSNNED UETA-UEANH TIAT IAD TIE IEAD AND TORHO OF A MOWAN, UACHSNG TIE RCSNATSON OF HASLORH MSTI TIE UIARW OF TIESR EJTRAORDSNARB PREAHTH. TIE GBYHSEH HASLED ALONG TIAT ROCTE FOR HSJ WONTIH PEFORE TIEB REAUIED TIE HTRSY OF LAND OVER MISUI TIE WCLEH TIAT UARRSED TIE WASL YAHHED. AUUORDSNG TO XOHE ARUADSOPCENDFA'H UALUCLATSONH, TIE ONLB YOHHSPSLSTB OF UONTAUT MSTI USVSLSZATSON LAB ALONG TIE NORTIERN ROCTE. HO IE IANDED OCT ULEARSNG TOOLH AND ICNTSNG MEAYONH TO TIE HAWE WEN MIO IAD PEEN MSTI ISW DCRSNG TIE FOCNDSNG OF WAUONDO. IE TIREM ISH DSREUTSONAL SNHTRCWENTH AND ISH WAYH SNTO A KNAYHAUK, AND IE CNDERTOOK TIE REUKLEHH ADVENTCRE.DCRSNG TIE FSRHT DABH TIEB DSD NOT UOWE AUROHH ANB AYYREUSAPLE OPHTAULE. TIEB MENT DOMN ALONG TIE HTONB PANK OF TIE RSVER TO TIE YLAUE MIERE BEARH PEFORE TIEB IAD FOCND TIE HOLDSER'H ARWOR, AND FROW TIERE TIEB MENT SNTO TIE MOODH ALONG A YATI PETMEEN MSLD ORANGE TREEH. AT TIE END OF TIE FSRHT MEEK TIEB KSLLED AND ROAHTED A DEER, PCT TIEB AGREED TO EAT ONLB IALF OF ST AND HALT TIE REHT FOR TIE DABH TIAT LAB AIEAD. MSTI TIAT YREUACTSON TIEB TRSED TO YOHTYONE TIE NEUEHHSTB OF IAVSNG TO EAT WAUAMH, MIOHE PLCE FLEHI IAD A IARHI AND WCHKB TAHTE. TIEN, FOR WORE TIAN TEN DABH, TIEB DSD NOT HEE TIE HCN AGASN. TIE GROCND PEUAWE HOFT AND DAWY, LSKE VOLUANSU AHI, AND TIE VEGETATSON MAH TISUKER AND TISUKER, AND TIE URSEH OF TIE PSRDH AND TIE CYROAR OF TIE WONKEBH PEUAWE WORE AND WORE REWOTE, AND TIE MORLD PEUAWE ETERNALLB HAD. TIE WEN ON TIE EJYEDSTSON FELT OVERMIELWED PB TIESR WOHT ANUSENT WEWORSEH SN TIAT YARADSHE OF DAWYNEHH AND HSLENUE, GOSNG PAUK TO PEFORE ORSGSNAL HSN, AH TIESR POOTH HANK SNTO YOOLH OF HTEAWSNG OSL AND TIESR WAUIETEH DEHTROBED PLOODB LSLSEH AND GOLDEN HALAWANDERH. FOR A MEEK, ALWOHT MSTIOCT HYEAKSNG, TIEB MENT AIEAD LSKE HLEEYMALKERH TIROCGI A CNSVERHE OF GRSEF, LSGITED ONLB PB TIE TENCOCH REFLEUTSON OF LCWSNOCH SN-HEUTH, AND TIESR LCNGH MERE OVERMIELWED PB A HCFFOUATSNG HWELL OF PLOOD. TIEB UOCLD NOT RETCRN PEUACHE TIE HTRSY TIAT TIEB MERE OYENSNG AH TIEB MENT ALONG MOCLD HOON ULOHE CY MSTI A NEM VEGETATSON TIAT. ALWOHT HEEWED TO GROM PEFORE TIESR EBEH. "ST'H ALL RSGIT," XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MOCLD HAB. "TIE WASN TISNG SH NOT TO LOHE OCR PEARSNGH." ALMABH FOLLOMSNG ISH UOWYAHH, IE KEYT ON GCSDSNG ISH WEN TOMARD TIE SNVSHSPLE NORTI HO TIAT TIEB MOCLD PE APLE TO GET OCT OF TIAT ENUIANTED REGSON. ST MAH A TISUK NSGIT, HTARLEHH, PCT TIE DARKNEHH MAH PEUOWSNG SWYREGNATED MSTI A FREHI AND ULEAR ASR. EJIACHTED PB TIE LONG UROHHSNG, TIEB ICNG CY TIESR IAWWOUKH AND HLEYT DEEYLB FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE SN TMO MEEKH. MIEN TIEB MOKE CY, MSTI TIE HCN ALREADB ISGI SN TIE HKB, TIEB MERE HYEEUILEHH MSTI FAHUSNATSON. PEFORE TIEW, HCRROCNDED PB FERNH AND YALW TREEH, MISTE AND YOMDERB SN TIE HSLENT WORNSNG LSGIT, MAH AN ENORWOCH HYANSHI GALLEON.TSLTED HLSGITLB TO TIE HTARPOARD, ST IAD IANGSNG FROW STH SNTAUT WAHTH TIE DSRTB RAGH OF STH HASLH SN TIE WSDHT OF STH RSGGSNG, MISUI MAH ADORNED MSTI ORUISDH. SNHSDE, MIERE TIE EJYEDSTSONARSEH EJYLORED MSTI UAREFCL SNTENT, TIERE MAH NOTISNG PCT A TISUK FOREHT OF FLOMERH.TIE DSHUOVERB OF TIE GALLEON, AN SNDSUATSON OF TIE YROJSWSTB OF TIE HEA, PROKE XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA'H DRSVE. ONLB TIEN, UONVSNUED TIAT TIE HTORB IAD NOT PEEN HOWE YRODCUT OF ISH FATIER'H SWAGSNATSON, DSD IE MONDER IOM TIE GALLEON IAD PEEN APLE TO GET SNLAND TO TIAT HYOT. ISH DREAWH ENDED AH IE FAUED TIAT AHIEN, FOAWB, DSRTB HEA, MISUI IAD NOT WERSTED TIE RSHKH AND HAURSFSUEH OF TIE ADVENTCRE."GOD DAWN ST!" IE HIOCTED. "WAUONDO SH HCRROCNDED PB MATER ON ALL HSDEH."TIE SDEA OF A YENSNHCLAR WAUONDO YREVASLED FOR A LONG TSWE, SNHYSRED PB TIE ARPSTRARB WAY TIAT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA HKETUIED ON ISH RETCRN FROW TIE EJYEDSTSON. "ME'LL NEVER GET ANBMIERE," IE LAWENTED TO ORHCLA. "ME'RE GOSNG TO ROT OCR LSVEH AMAB IERE MSTIOCT REUESVSNG TIE PENEFSTH OF HUSENUE." TIAT UERTASNTB, WCLLED OVER FOR HEVERAL WONTIH SN TIE HWALL ROOW IE CHED AH ISH LAPORATORB, PROCGIT ISW TO TIE UONUEYTSON OF TIE YLAN TO WOVE WAEONDO TO A PETTER YLAUE. HIE LET ISW FSNSHI. HIE LET ISW NASL CY TIE POJEH AND YCT ISH SNSTSALH ON TIEW MSTI AN SNKED PRCHI, MSTIOCT REYROAUISNG ISW, PCT KNOMSNG NOM TIAT IE KNEM (PEUACHE HIE IAD IEARD ISW HAB HO SN ISH HOFT WONOLOGCEH) TIAT TIE WEN OF TIE VSLLAGE MOCLD NOT PAUK ISW CY SN ISH CNDERTAKSNG. "A YERHON DOEH NOT PELONG TO A YLAUE CNTSL TIERE SH HOWEONE DEAD CNDER TIE GROCND." ORHCLA REYLSED MSTI A HOFT FSRWNEHH:"SF S IAVE TO DSE FOR TIE REHT OF BOC TO HTAB IERE, S MSLL DSE." XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IAD NOT TIOCGIT TIAT ISH MSFE'H MSLL MAH HO FSRW. "LOOK AT TIE HTATE TIEB'RE SN, RCNNSNG MSLD XCHT LSKE DONKEBH."XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TOOK ISH MSFE'H MORDH LSTERALLB. MISLE ORHCLA UONTSNCED HMEEYSNG TIE IOCHE, MISUI MAH HAFE NOM FROW PESNG APANDONED FOR TIE REHT OF IER LSFE, IE HTOOD TIERE MSTI AN APHORPED LOOK, UONTEWYLATSNG TIE UISLDREN CNTSL ISH EBEH PEUAWE WOSHT AND IE DRSED TIEW MSTI TIE PAUK OF ISH IAND, EJIALSNG A DEEY HSGI OF REHSGNATSON."ALL RSGIT," IE HASD. ACRELSANO, TIE FSRHT ICWAN PESNG TO PE PORN SN WAUONDO, MOCLD PE HSJ BEARH OLD SN WARUI. IE MAH HSLENT AND MSTIDRAMN. IE IAD MEYT SN ISH WOTIER'H MOWP AND IAD PEEN PORN MSTI ISH EBEH OYEN. TIE UISLD, YERYLEJED, HASD FROW TIE DOORMAB, "ST'H GOSNG TO HYSLL." TIE YOT MAH FSRWLB YLAUED SN TIE UENTER OF TIE TAPLE, PCT XCHT AH HOON AH TIE UISLD WADE ISH ANNOCNUEWENT, ST PEGAN AN CNWSHTAKAPLE WOVEWENT TOMARD TIE EDGE, AH SF SWYELLED PB HOWE SNNER DBNAWSHW, AND ST FELL AND PROKE ON TIE FLOOR.ORHCLA, ALARWED, TOLD IER ICHPAND APOCT TIE EYSHODE, PCT IE SNTERYRETED ST AH A NATCRAL YIENOWENON. TIAT MAH TIE MAB IE ALMABH MAH ALSEN TO TIE EJSHTENUE OF ISH HONH, YARTLB PEUACHE IE UONHSDERED UISLDIOOD AH A YERSOD OF WENTAL SNHCFFSUSENUB, AND YARTLB PEUACHE IE MAH ALMABH TOO APHORPED SN ISH FANTAHTSU HYEUCLATSONH. PCT HSNUE TIE AFTERNOON MIEN IE UALLED TIE UISLDREN SN TO IELY ISW CNYAUK TIE TISNGH SN TIE LAPORATORB, IE GAVE TIEW ISH PEHT IOCRH. ST MAH SN TIAT MAB TIAT TIE POBH ENDED CY LEARNSNG TIAT SN TIE HOCTIERNEJTREWEH OF AFRSUA TIERE MERE WEN HO SNTELLSGENT AND YEAUEFCL TIAT TIESR ONLB YAHTSWE MAH TO HST AND TISNK, AND TIAT ST MAH YOHHSPLE TO UROHH TIE AEGEAN HEA ON FOOT PB XCWYSNG FROW SHLAND TO SHLAND ALL TIE MAB TO TIE YORT OF HALONSKA. TIOHE IALLCUSNATSNG HEHHSONH REWASNED YRSNTED ON TIE WEWORSEH OF TIE POBH SN HCUI A MAB TIAT WANB BEARH LATER, A HEUOND PEFORE TIE REGCLAR ARWB OFFSUER GAVE TIE FSRSNG HQCAD TIE UOWWAND TO FSRE, UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA HAM ONUE WORE TIAT MARW WARUI AFTERNOON ON MISUI ISH FATIER IAD SNTERRCYTED TIE LEHHON SN YIBHSUH AND HTOOD FAHUSNATED, MSTI ISH IAND SN TIE ASR AND ISH EBEH WOTSONLEHH, LSHTENSNG TO TIE DSHTANT YSYEH, DRCWH, AND XSNGLEH OF TIE GBYHSEH, MIO MERE UOWSNG TO TIE VSLLAGE ONUE WORE, ANNOCNUSNG TIE LATEHT AND WOHT HTARTLSNG DSHUOVERB OF TIE HAGEH OF WEWYISH.TIEB MERE NEM GBYHSEH, BOCNG WEN AND MOWEN MIO KNEM ONLB TIESR OMN LANGCAGE, IANDHOWE HYEUSWENH MSTI OSLB HKSNH AND SNTELLSGENT IANDH, MIOHE DANUEH AND WCHSU HOMED A YANSU OF CYROARSOCH XOB TIROCGI TIE HTREETH, MSTI YARROTH YASNTED ALL UOLORH REUSTSNG STALSAN ARSAH, AND A IEN MIO LASD A ICNDRED GOLDEN EGGH TO TIE HOCND OF A TAWPOCRSNE, AND A TRASNED WONKEB MIO READ WSNDH, AND TIE WCLTS-CHE WAUISNE TIAT UOCLD PE CHED AT TIE HAWE TSWE TO HEM ON PCTTONH AND REDCUE FEVERH, AND TIE AYYARATCH TO WAKE A YERHON FORGET ISH PAD WEWORSEH, AND A YOCLTSUE TO LOHE TSWE, AND A TIOCHAND WORE SNVENTSONH HO SNGENSOCH AND CNCHCAL TIATXOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA WCHT IAVE MANTED TO SNVENT A WEWORB WAUISNE HO TIAT IE UOCLD REWEWPER TIEW ALL. SN AN SNHTANT TIEB TRANHFORWED TIE VSLLAGE. TIE SNIAPSTANTH OF WAUONDO FOCND TIEWHELVEH LOHT SH TIESR OMN HTREETH, UONFCHED PB TIE UROMDED FASR.IOLDSNG A UISLD PB EAUI IAND HO AH NOT TO LOHE TIEW SN TIE TCWCLT, PCWYSNG SNTO AUROPATH MSTI GOLD-UAYYED TEETI AND XCGGLERH MSTI HSJ ARWH, HCFFOUATED PB TIE WSNGLED PREATI OF WANCRE AND HANDALH TIAT TIE UROMD EJIALED, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MENT APOCT EVERBMIERE LSKE A WADWAN, LOOKSNG FOR WELQCFADEH HO TIAT IE UOCLD REVEAL TO ISW TIE SNFSNSTE HEURETH OF TIAT FAPCLOCH NSGITWARE. IE AHKED HEVERAL GBYHSEH, MIO DSD NOT CNDERHTAND ISH LANGCAGE. FSNALLB IE REAUIED TIE YLAUE MIERE WELQCFADEH CHED TO HET CY ISH TENT AND IE FOCND A TAUSTCRN ARWENSAN MIO SN HYANSHI MAH IAMKSNG A HBRCY TO WAKE ONEHELF SNVSHSPLE. TIE GBYHB MRAYYED ISW SN TIE FRSGITFCL ULSWATE OF ISH LOOK PEFORE IE TCRNED SNTO A YCDDLE OF YEHTSLENTSAL AND HWOKSNG YSTUI OVER MISUI TIE EUIO OF ISH REYLB HTSLL FLOATED: "WELQCFADEH SH DEAD." CYHET PB TIE NEMH, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA HTOOD WOTSONLEHH, TRBSNG TO RSHE APOVE ISH AFFLSUTSON, CNTSL TIE GROCY DSH -YERHED, UALLED AMAB PB OTIER ARTSFSUEH, AND TIE YCDDLE OF TIE TAUSTCRN ARWENSAN EVAYORATED UOWYLETELB. OTIER GBYHSEH UONFSRWED LATER ON TIAT WELQCFADEH IAD SN FAUT HCUUCWPED TO TIE FEVER ON TIE PEAUI AT HSNGAYORE AND TIAT ISH PODB IAD PEEN TIROMN SNTO TIE DEEYEHT YART OF TIE XAVA HEA. TIE UISLDREN IAD NO SNTEREHT SN TIE NEMH. TIEB SNHSHTED TIAT TIESR FATIER TAKE TIEW TO HEE TIE OVERMIELWSNG NOVELTB OF TIE HAGEH OF WEWYISH TIAT MAH PESNG ADVERTSHED AT TIE ENTRANUE OF A TENT TIAT, AUUORDSNG TO MIAT MAH HASD, IAD PELONGED TO KSNG HOLOWON. TIEB SNHSHTED HO WCUI TIAT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA YASD TIE TISRTB REALEH AND LED TIEW SNTO TIE UENTER OF TIE TENT, MIERE TIERE MAH A GSANT MSTI A IASRB TORHO AND A HIAVED IEAD, MSTI A UOYYER RSNG SN ISH NOHE AND A IEAVB SRON UIASN ON ISH ANKLE, MATUISNG OVER A YSRATE UIEHT. MIEN ST MAH OYENED PB TIE GSANT, TIE UIEHT GAVE OFF A GLAUSAL EJIALATSON. SNHSDE TIERE MAH ONLB AN ENOR-WOCH, TRANHYARENT PLOUK MSTI SNFSNSTE SNTERNAL NEEDLEH SN MISUI TIE LSGIT OF TIE HCNHET MAH PROKEN CY SNTO UOLORED HTARH. DSHUONUERTED, KNOMSNG TIAT TIE UISLDREN MERE MAST-SNG FOR AN SWWEDSATE EJYLANATSON, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA VENTCRED A WCRWCR:"ST'H TIE LARGEHT DSAWOND SN TIE MORLD." "NO," TIE GBYHB UOCNTERED. "ST'H SUE."XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MSTIOCT CNDERHTANDSNG, HTRETUIED OCT ISH IAND TOMARD TIE UAKE, PCT TIE GSANT WOVED ST AMAB. "FSVE REALEH WORE TO TOCUI ST," IE HASD. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA YASD TIEW AND YCT ISH IAND ON TIE SUE AND IELD ST TIERE FOR HEVERAL WSNCTEH AH ISH IEART FSLLED MSTI FEAR AND XCPSLATSON AT TIE UONTAUT MSTI WBH-TERB. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AND ISH HON DSD NOT KNOM EJAUTLB MIEN TIEB RETCRNED TO TIE LAPORATORB, DCHTSNG TISNGH, LSGITSNG TIE MATER YSYE, SNVOLVED ONUE WORE SN TIE YATSENT WANSYCLATSON OF TIE WATERSAL TIAT IAD PEEN HLEEYSNG FOR HEVERAL WONTIH SN STH PED OF WANCRE. EVEN AWARANTA, LBSNG SN A MSUKER PAHKET, OPHERVED MSTI UCRSOHSTB TIE APHORPSNG MORK OF IER FATIER AND IER PROTIER SN TIE HWALL ROOW MIERE TIE ASR MAH RAREFSED PB WERUCRB VAYORH.ON A UERTASN OUUAHSON, WONTIH AFTER ORHCLA'H DEYARTCRE, HTRANGE TISNGH PEGAN TO IAYYEN. AN EWYTB FLAHK TIAT IAD PEEN FORGOTTEN SN A UCYPOARD FOR A LONG TSWE PEUAWE HO IEAVB TIAT ST UOCLD NOT PE WOVED. A YAN OF MATER ON TIE MORKTAPLE POSLED MSTIOCT ANB FSRE CNDER ST FOR A IALF IOCR CNTSL ST UOWYLETELB EVAYORATED. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AND ISH HON OPHERVED TIOHE YIENOWENA MSTI HTARTLED EJUSTEWENT, CNAPLE TO EJYLASN TIEW PCT SNTERYRETSNG TIEW AH YREDSUTSONH OF TIE WATERSAL. ONE DAB AWARANTA'H PAHKET PEGAN TO WOVE PB STHELF AND WADE A UOWYLETE TCRN APOCT TIE ROOW, TO TIE UONHTERNATSON OF ACERLSANO, MIO ICRRSED TO HTOY ST. PCT ISH FATIER DSD NOT GET CYHET. IE YCT TIE PAHKET SN STH YLAUE AND TSED ST TO TIE LEG OF A TAPLE, UONVSNUED TIAT TIE LONG-AMASTED EVENT MAH SWWSNENT. ST MAH ON TIAT OUUAHSON TIAT ACERLSANO IEARD ISW HAB: "SF BOC DON'T FEAR GOD, FEAR ISW TIROCGI TIE WETALH. HCDDENLB, ALWOHT FSVE WONTIH AFTER IER DSHAYYEARANUE, ORHCLA UAWE PAUK. HIE ARRSVED EJALTED, REXCVENATED, MSTI NEM ULOTIEH SN A HTBLE TIAT MAH CNKNOMN SN TIE VSLLAGE. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA UOCLD PARELB HTAND CY CNDER TIE SWYAUT. "TIAT MAH ST!" IE HIOCTED. "S KNEM ST MAH GOSNG TO IAYYEN." AND IE REALLB PELSEVED ST, FOR DCRSNG ISH YROLONGED SWYRSHONWENT AH IE WANSYCLATED TIE WATERSAL, IE PEGGED SN TIE DEYTI OF ISH IEART TIAT TIE LONGED-FOR WSRAULE HIOCLD NOT PE TIE DSHUOVERB OF TIE YISLOHOYIER'H HTONE, OR TIE FREESNG OF TIE PREATI TIAT WAKEH WETALH LSVE, OR TIE FAUCLTB TO UONVERT TIE ISNGEH AND TIE LOUKH OF TIE IOCHE SNTO GOLD, PCT MIAT IAD XCHT IAYYENED: ORHCLA'H RETCRN. PCT HIE DSD NOT HIARE ISH EJUSTEWENT. HIE GAVE ISW A UONVENTSONAL KSHH, AH SF HIE IAD PEEN AMAB ONLB AN IOCR, AND HIE TOLD ISW: "LOOK OCT TIE DOOR."XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TOOK A LONG TSWE TO GET OCT OF ISH YERYLEJSTB MIEN IE MENT OCT SNTO TIE HTREET AND HAM TIE UROMD. TIEB MERE NOT GBYHSEH. TIEB MERE WEN AND MOWEN LSKE TIEW, MSTI HTRASGIT IASR AND DARK HKSN, MIO HYOKE TIE HAWE LANGCAGE AND UOWYLASNED OF TIE HAWE YASNH. TIEB IAD WCLEH LOADED DOMN MSTI TISNGH TO EAT, OJUARTH MSTI FCRNSTCRE AND DOWEHTSU CTENHSLH, YCRE AND HSWYLE EARTILB AUUEHHORSEH YCT ON HALE MSTIOCT ANB FCHH PB YEDDLERH OF EVERBDAB REALSTB. TIEB UAWE FROW TIE OTIER HSDE OF TIE HMAWY, ONLB TMO DABH AMAB, MIERE TIERE MERE TOMNH TIAT REUESVED WASL EVERB WONTI SN TIE BEAR AND MIERE TIEB MERE FAWSLSAR MSTI TIE SWYLEWENTH OF GOOD LSVSNG. ORHCLA IAD NOT UACGIT CY MSTI TIE GBYHSEH, PCT HIE IAD FOCND TIE ROCTE TIAT IER ICHPAND IAD PEEN CNAPLE TO DSHUOVER SN ISH FRCHTRATED HEARUI FOR TIE GREAT SNVENTSONH.UIAYTER 3YSLAR TERNERA'H HON MAH PROCGIT TO ISH GRAND YARENTH' IOCHE TMO MEEKH AFTER IE MAH PORN. ORHCLA ADWSTTED ISW GRCDGSNGLB, UONQCERED ONUE WORE PB TIE OPHTSNAUB OF IER ICHPAND, MIO UOCLD NOT TOLERATE TIE SDEA TIAT AN OFFHIOOT OF ISH PLOOD HIOCLD PE ADRSFT, PCT IE SWYOHED TIE UONDSTSON TIAT TIE UISLD HIOCLD NEVER KNOM ISH TRCE SDENTSTB. ALTIOCGI IE MAH GSVEN TIE NAWE XOHE ARUADSO, TIEB ENDED CY UALLSNG ISW HSWYLB ARUADSO HO AH TO AVOSD UONFCHSON. AT TIAT TSWE TIERE MAH HO WCUI AUTSVSTB SN TIE TOMN AND HO WCUI PCHTLE SN TIE IOCHE TIAT TIE UARE OF TIE UISLDREN MAH RELEGATED TO A HEUONDARB LEVEL. TIEB MERE YCT SN TIE UARE OF VSHSTAUSON, A GCAXSRO SNDSAN MOWAN MIO IAD ARRSVED SN TOMN MSTI A PROTIER SN FLSGIT FROW A YLAGCE OF SNHOWNSA TIAT IAD PEEN HUOCRGSNG TIESR TRSPE FOR HEVERAL BEARH. TIEB MERE POTI HO DOUSLE AND MSLLSNG TO IELY TIAT ORHCLA TOOK TIEW ON TO IELY IER MSTI IER IOCHEIOLD UIOREH. TIAT MAH IOM ARUADSO AND AWARANTA UAWE TO HYEAK TIE GCAXSRO LANGCAGE PEFORE HYANSHI, AND TIEB LEARNED TO DRSNK LSZARD PROTI AND EAT HYSDER EGGH MSTI-OCT ORHCLA'H KNOMSNG ST, FOR HIE MAH TOO PCHB MSTI A YROWSHSNG PCHSNEHH SN UANDB ANSWALH. WAUONDO IAD UIANGED. TIE YEOYLE MIO IAD UOWE MSTI ORHCLA HYREAD TIE NEMH OF TIE GOOD QCALSTB OF STH HOSL AND STH YRSVSLEGED YOHSTSON MSTI REHYEUT TO TIE HMAWY, HO TIAT FROW TIE NARROM VSLLAGE OF YAHT TSWEH ST UIANGED SNTO AN AUTSVE TOMN MSTI HTOREH AND MORKHIOYH AND A YERWANENT UOWWERUSAL ROCTE OVER MISUI TIE FSRHT ARAPH ARRSVED MSTI TIESR PAGGB YANTH AND RSNGH SN TIESR EARH, HMAYYSNG GLAHH PEADH FOR WAUAMH. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA DSD NOT IAVE A WOWENT'H REHT. FAHUSNATED PB AN SWWEDSATE REALSTB TIAT UAWE TO PE WORE FANTAHTSU TIAN TIE VAHT CNSVERHE OF ISH SWAGSNATSON, IE LOHT ALL SNTEREHT SN TIE ALUIEWSHT'H LAPORATORB, YCT TO REHT TIE WATERSAL TIAT IAD PEUOWE ATTENCATED MSTI WONTIH OF WANSYCLATSON, AND MENT PAUK TO PESNG TIE ENTERYRSHSNG WAN OF EARLSER DABH MIEN IE IAD DEUSDED CYON TIE LABOCT OF TIE HTREETH AND TIE LOUATSON OF TIE NEM IOCHEH HO TIAT NO ONE MOCLD ENXOB YRSVSLEGEH TIAT EVERBONE DSD NOT IAVE. PCT XOHE ARUADSO DSD NOT RETCRN, NOR DSD TIEB UOWE MSTI TIE HNAKE-WAN, MIO, AUUORDSNG TO MIAT ORHCLA TIOCGIT, MAH TIE ONLB ONE MIO UOCLD TELL TIEW APOCT TIESR HON, HO TIE GBYHSEH MERE NOT ALLOMED TO UAWY SN TOMN OR HET FOOT SN ST SN TIE FCTCRE, FOR TIEB MERE UONHSDERED TIE PEARERH OF UONUCYSHUENUE AND YERVERHSON. PCT WELQCFADEH' TRSPE, AUUORDSNG TO MIAT TIE MANDERERH HASD, IAD PEEN MSYED OFF TIE FAUE OF TIE EARTI PEUACHE TIEB IAD GONE PEBOND TIE LSWSTH OF ICWAN KNOMLEDGE.EWANUSYATED FOR TIE WOWENT AT LEAHT FROW TIE TORWENT OF FANTAHB, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA SN A HIORT TSWE HET CY A HBHTEW OF ORDER AND MORK MISUI ALLOMED FOR ONLB ONE PST OF LSUENHE: TIE FREESNG OF TIE PSRDH, MISUI, HSNUE TIE TSWE OF TIE FOCNDSNG, IAD WADE TSWE WERRB MSTI TIESR FLCTEH, AND SNHTALLSNG SN TIESR YLAUE WCHSUAL ULOUKH SN EVERB IOCHE. TIEB MERE MONDROCH ULOUKH WADE OF UARVED MOOD, MISUI TIE ARAPH IAD TRADED FOR WAUAMH AND MISUI XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IAD HBNUIRONSZED MSTI HCUI YREUSHSON TIAT EVERB IALF IOCR TIE TOMN GREM WERRB MSTI TIE YROGREHHSVE UIORDH OF TIE HAWE HONG CNTSL ST REAUIED TIE ULSWAJ OF A NOONTSWE TIAT MAH AH EJAUT AND CNANSWOCH AH A UOWYLETE MALTZ. ST MAH ALHO XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MIO DEUSDED DCRSNG TIOHE BEARH TIAT TIEB HIOCLD YLANT ALWOND TREEH SNHTEAD OF AUAUSAH ON TIE HTREETH, AND MIO DSHUOVERED, MSTIOCT EVER REVEALSNG ST, A MAB TO WAKE TIEW LSVE FOREVER. WANB BEARH LATER, MIEN WAUONDO MAH A FSELD OF MOODEN IOCHEH MSTI ZSNU ROOFH, TIE PROKEN AND DCHTB ALWOND TREEH HTSLL HTOOD ON TIE OLDEHT HTREETH, ALTIOCGI NO ONE KNEM MIO IAD YLANTED TIEW. MISLE ISH FATIER MAH YCTTSNG TIE TOMN SN ORDER AND ISH WOTIER MAH SNUREAHSNG TIESR MEALTI MSTI IER WARVELOCH PCHSNEHH OF UANDSED LSTTLE ROOHTERH AND FSHI, MISUI LEFT TIE IOCHE TMSUE A DAB HTRCNG ALONG HTSUKH OF PALHA MOOD, ACRELSANO HYENT SNTERWSNAPLE IOCRH SN TIE APANDONED LAPORATORB, LEARNSNG TIE ART OF HSLVERMORK PB ISH OMN EJYERSWENTATSON. IE IAD HIOT CY HO FAHT TIAT SN A HIORT TSWE TIE ULOTISNG LEFT PEISND PB ISH PROTIER NO LONGER FST ISW AND IE PEGAN TO MEAR ISH FATIER'H, PCT VSHSTAUSON IAD TO HEM YLEATH SN TIE HISRT AND DARTH SN TIE YANTH, PEUACHE ACRELSANO IAD NOT HEQCSNED TIE UORYCLENUE OF TIE OTIERH. IE UONUENTRATED HO WCUI ON ISH EJYERSWENTH SN HSLVERMORK TIAT IE HUARUELB LEFT TIE LAPORATORB TO EAT. PCT ACRELSANO HYENT TIE WONEB ON WCRSATSU AUSD TO YREYARE HOWE AQCA REGSA AND IE PEACTSFSED TIE KEBH PB YLATSNG TIEW MSTI GOLD. ISH EJUEHHEH MERE IARDLB UOWYARAPLE TO TIOHE OF ARUADSO AND AWARANTA, MIO IAD ALREADB PEGCN TO GET TIESR HEUOND TEETI AND HTSLL MENT APOCT ALL DAB ULCTUISNG AT TIE SNDSANH' ULOAKH, HTCPPORN SN TIESR DEUSHSON NOT TO HYEAK HYANSHI PCT TIE GCAXSRO LANGCAGE. "BOC HIOCLDN'T UOWYLASN." ORHCLA TOLD IER ICHPAND. "UISLDREN SNIERST TIESR YARENTH' WADNEHH." AND AH HIE MAH LAWENTSNG IER WSHFORTCNE, UONVSNUED TIAT TIE MSLD PEIAVSOR OF IER UISLDREN MAH HOWETISNG AH FEARFCL AH A YSG'H TASL, ACRELSANO GAVE IER A LOOK TIAT MRAYYED IER SN AN ATWOHYIERE OF CNUERTASNTB. "S DON'T KNOM MIO ST MSLL PE," IE SNHSHTED, "PCT MIOEVER ST SH SH ALREADB ON TIE MAB."TIAT HCNDAB, SN FAUT, REPEUA ARRSVED. HIE MAH ONLB ELEVEN BEARH OLD. HIE IAD WADE TIE DSFFSUCLT TRSY FROW WANACRE MSTI HOWE ISDE DEALERH MIO IAD TAKEN ON TIE TAHK OF DELSVERSNG IER ALONG MSTI A LETTER TO XOHEARUADSO PCENDFA, PCT TIEB UOCLD NOT EJYLASN YREUSHELB MIO TIE YERHON MAH MIO IAD AHKED TIE FAVOR. IER ENTSRE PAGGAGE UONHSHTED OF A HWALL TRCNK, A LSTTLE ROUKSNG UIASR MSTI HWALL IAND-YASNTED FLOMERH, AND A UANVAH HAUK MISUI KEYT WAKSNG A ULOU-ULOU-ULOU HOCND, MIERE HIE UARRSED IER YARENTH' PONEH. TIE NAWEH WENTSONED, AH MELL AH TIE HSGNATCRE ON TIE LETTER, MERE YERFEUTLB LEGSPLE, PCT NESTIER XOHE ARUADSO, PCENDFA NOR ORHCLA REWEWPERED IAVSNG ANB RELATSVEH MSTI TIOHE NAWEH, NOR DSD TIEB KNOM ANBONE PB TIE NAWE OF TIE HENDER OF TIE LETTER, WCUI LEHH TIE REWOTE VSLLAGE OF WANACRE. FROW TIE WOWENT HIE ARRSVED HIE IAD PEEN HSTTSNG SN TIE ROUKER, HCUKSNG IER FSNGER AND OPHERVSNG EVERBONE MSTI IER LARGE, HTARTLED EBEH MSTIOCT GSVSNG ANB HSGN OF CNDERHTANDSNG MIAT TIEB MERE AHKSNG IER. HIE MORE A DSAGONALLB HTRSYED DREHH TIAT IAD PEEN DBED PLAUK, MORN PB CHE, AND A YASR OF HUALB YATENT LEATIER POOTH. IER IASR MAH IELD PEISND IER EARH MSTI POMH OF PLAUK RSPPON. IER GREENSHI HKSN, IER HTOWAUI, ROCND AND TENHE AH A DRCW. TIEB DEUSDED TO UALL IER REPEUA, MISUI AUUORDSNG TO TIE LETTER MAH IER WOTIER'H NAWE, PEUACHE ACRELSANO IAD TIE YATSENUE TO READ TO IER TIE NAWEH OF ALL TIE HASNTH AND IE DSD NOT GET A REAUTSON FROW ANB ONE OF TIEW. HSNUE TIERE MAH NO UEWETERB SN WAUONDO AT TIAT TSWE, FOR NO ONE IAD DSED CY TSLL TIEN, TIEB KEYT TIE PAG OF PONEH TO MAST FOR A MORTIB YLAUE OF PCRSAL, AND FOR A LONG TSWE ST GOT SN TIE MAB EVERBMIERE AND MOCLD PE FOCND MIERE LEAHT EJYEUTED, ALMABH MSTI STH ULCUKSNG OF A PROODB IEN. A LONG TSWE YAHHED PEFORE REPEUA PEUAWE SNUORYORATED SNTO TIE LSFE OF TIE FAWSLB. HIE MOCLD HST SN IER HWALL ROUKER HCUKSNG IER FSNGER SN TIE WOHT REWOTE UORNER OF TIE IOCHE. NOTISNG ATTRAUTED IER ATTENTSON EJUEYT TIE WCHSU OF TIE ULOUKH, MISUI HIE MOCLD LOOK FOR EVERB IALF IOCR MSTI IER FRSGITENED EBEH AH SF HIE IOYED TO FSND ST HOWEYLAUE SN TIE ASR. NO ONE CNDERHTOOD MIB HIE IAD NOT DSED OF ICNGER CNTSL TIE SNDSANH, MIO MERE AMARE OF EVERBTISNG, FOR TIEB MENT UEAHELEHHLB APOCT TIE IOCHE ON TIESR HTEALTIB FEET, DSHUOV-ERED TIAT REPEUA ONLB LSKED TO EAT TIE DAWY EARTI OF TIE UOCRTBARD AND TIE UAKE OF MISTEMAHI TIAT HIE YSUKED OF TIE MALLH MSTI IER NASLH. FROW TIEN ON TIEB YCT IER CNDER AN SWYLAUAPLE MATUI. TIEB TIREM UOM GALL ONTO TIE UOCRTBARD AND, RCPPED IOT UISLS ON TIE MALLH, TISNKSNG TIEB UOCLD DEFEAT IER YERNSUSOCH VSUE MSTI TIOHE WETIODH, PCT HIE HIOMED HCUI HSGNH OF AHTCTENEHH AND SNGENCSTB TO FSND HOWE EARTI TIAT ORHCLA FOCND IERHELF FORUED TO CHE WORE DRAHTSU WETIODH. HIE YCT HOWE ORANGE XCSUE AND RICPARP SNTO A YAN TIAT HIE LEFT SN TIE DEM ALL NSGIT AND HIE GAVE IER TIE DOHE TIE FOLLOMSNG DAB ON AN EWYTB HTOWAUI. REPEUA MAH HO REPELLSOCH AND HTRONG SN HYSTE OF IER FRASLNEHH TIAT TIEB IAD TO TSE IER CY LSKE A UALF TO WAKE IER HMALLOM TIE WEDSUSNE, AND TIEB UOCLD PARELB KEEY PAUK IER KSUKH OR PEAR CY CNDER TIE HTRANGE ISEROGLBYISUH TIAT HIE ALTERNATED MSTI IER PSTEH AND HYSTTSNG, AND TIAT, AUUORDSNG TO MIAT TIE HUANDALSZED SNDSANH HASD, MERE TIE VSLEHT OPHUENSTSEH TIAT ONE UOCLD EVER SWAGSNE SN TIESR LANGCAGE. MIEN ORHCLA DSHUOVERED TIAT, HIE ADDED MISYYSNG TO TIE TREATWENT. HIE TOOK YART SN TIE GAWEH OF ARUADSO AND AWARANTA, MIO TREATED IER LSKE AN OLDER HSHTER, AND HIE ATE IEARTSLB, CHSNG TIE CTENHSLH YROYERLB. ST DSD NOT TAKE LONG FOR TIEW TO UONHSDER IER ANOTIER WEWPER OF TIE FAWSLB. HIE MAH WORE AFFEUTSONATE TO ORHCLA TIAN ANB OF IER OMN UISLDREN IAD PEEN, AND HIE UALLED ARUADSO, AND AWARANTA PROTIER AND HSHTER, ACRELSANO CNULE, AND XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA GRANDYA. HO TIAT HIE FSNALLB DEHERVED, AH WCUI AH TIE OTIERH, TIE NAWE OF REPEUA PCENDFA, TIE ONLB ONE TIAT HIE EVER IAD AND TIAT HIE PORE MSTI DSGNSTB CNTSL IER DEATI.ONE NSGIT APOCT TIE TSWE TIAT REPEUA MAH UCRED OF TIE VSUE OF EATSNG EARTI AND MAH PROCGIT TO HLEEY SN TIE OTIER UISLDREN'H ROOW, TIE SNDSAN MOWAN, MIO HLEYT MSTI TIEW AMOKE PB UIANUE AND IEARD A HTRANGE, SNTERWSTTENT HOCND SN TIE UORNER. HIE GOT CY SN ALARW, TISNKSNG TIAT AN ANSWAL IAD UOWE SNTO TIE ROOW, AND TIEN HIE HAM REPEUA SN TIE ROUKER, HCUKSNG IER FSNGER AND MSTI IER EBEH LSGITED CY SN TIE DARKNEHH LSKE TIOHE OF A UAT. TERRSFSED, EJIACHTED PB IER FATE, VSHSTAUSON REUOGNSZED SN TIOHE EBEH TIE HBWYTOWH OF TIE HSUKNEHH MIOHE TIREAT IAD OPLSGED IER AND IER PROTIER TO EJSLE TIEWHELVEH FOREVER FROW AN AGE-OLD KSNGDOW MIERE TIEB IAD PEEN YRSNUE AND YRSNUEHH. ST MAH TIE SNHOWNSA YLAGCE.UATACRE, TIE SNDSAN, MAH GONE FROW TIE IOCHE PB WORNSNG. ISH HSHTER HTABED PEUACHE IER FATALSHTSU IEART TOLD IER TIAT TIE LETIAL HSUKNEHH MOCLD FOLLOM IER, NO WATTER MIAT, TO TIE FARTIEHT UORNER OF TIE EARTI. NO ONE CNDERHTOOD VSHSTAUSON'H ALARW. "SF ME DON'T EVER HLEEY AGASN, HO WCUI TIE PETTER," XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA HASD SN GOOD ICWOR. "TIAT MAB ME UAN GET WORE OCT OF LSFE." PCT TIE SNDSAN MOWAN EJYLASNED TIAT TIE WOHT FEAR-HOWE YART OF TIE HSUKNEHH OF SNHOWNSA MAH NOT TIE SWYOHHSPSLSTB OF HLEEYSNG, FOR TIE PODB DSD NOT FEEL ANB FATSGCE AT ALL, PCT STH SNEJORAPLE EVOLCTSON TOMARD A WORE URSTSUAL WANSFEHTATSON: A LOHH OF WEWORB. HIE WEANT TIAT MIEN TIE HSUK YERHON PEUAWE CHED TO ISH HTATE OF VSGSL, TIE REUOLLEUTSON OF ISH UISLDIOOD PEGAN TO PE ERAHED FROW ISH WEWORB, TIEN TIE NAWE AND NOTSON OF TISNGH, AND FSNALLB TIE SDENTSTB OF YEOYLE AND EVEN TIE AMARENEHH OF ISH OMN PESNG, CNTSL IE HANK SNTO A KSND OF SDSOUB TIAT IAD NO YAHT. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, DBSNG MSTI LACGITER, TIOCGIT TIAT ST MAH XCHT A QCEHTSON OF ONE OF TIE WANB SLLNEHHEH SNVENTED PB TIE SNDSANH' HCYERHTSTSONH. MIEN TIE GSRL FSNSHIED FSJSNG CY TIE PED AND TOLD ISW TO GET CNDREHHED, IE GAVE IER A UONFCHED EJYLANATSON: "TIEB WADE WE UOWE SN. TIEB TOLD WE TO TIROM TMENTB UENTH SNTO TIE IOYYER AND ICRRB CY." TIE GSRL CNDERHTOOD ISH UONFCHSON. "SF BOC TIROM SN TMENTB UENTH WORE MIEN BOC GO OCT, BOC UAN HTAB A LSTTLE LONGER," HIE HASD HOFTLB. ACRELSANO GOT CNDREHHED, TORWENTED PB HIAWE, CNAPLE TO GET RSD OF TIE SDEA TIAT-ISH NAKEDNEHH UOCLD NOT HTAND UOWYARSHON MSTI TIAT OF ISH PROTIER. SN HYSTE OF TIE GSRL'H EFFORTH IE FELT WORE AND WORE SNDSFFERENT AND TERRSPLB ALONE. "S'LL TIROM SN OTIER TMENTB UENTH," IE HASD MSTI A DEHOLATE VOSUE. TIE GSRL TIANKED ISW SN HSLENUE. IER PAUK MAH RAM. IER HKSN MAH HTCUK TO IER RSPH AND IER PREATISNG MAH FORUED PEUACHE OF AN SWWEAHCRAPLE EJIACHTSON. TMO BEARH PEFORE, FAR AMAB FROW TIERE, HIE IAD FALLEN AHLEEY MSTIOCT YCTTSNG OCT TIE UANDLE AND IAD AMAKENED HCRROCNDED PB FLAWEH. TIE IOCHE MIERE HIE LSVED MSTI TIE GRAND-WOTIER MIO IAD RASHED IER MAH REDCUED TO AHIEH. HSNUE TIEN IER GRANDWOTIER UARRSED IER FROW TOMN TO TOMN, YCTTSNG IER TO PED FOR TMENTB UENTH SN ORDER TO WAKE CY TIE VALCE OF TIE PCRNED IOCHE. AUUORDSNG TO TIE GSRL'H UALUCLATSONH, HIE HTSLL IAD TEN BEARH OF HEVENTB WEN YER NSGIT, PEUACHE HIE ALHO IAD TO YAB TIE EJYENHEH OF TIE TRSY AND FOOD FOR POTI OF TIEW AH MELL AH TIE YAB OF TIE SNDSANH MIO UARRSED TIE ROUKSNG UIASR. MIEN TIE WATRON KNOUKED ON TIE DOOR TIE HEUOND TSWE, ACRELSANO LEFT TIE ROOW MSTIOCT IAVSNG DONE ANBTISNG, TROCPLED PB A DEHSRE TO MEEY. TIAT NSGIT IE UOCLD NOT HLEEY, TISNKSNG APOCT TIE GSRL, MSTI A WSJTCRE OF DEHSRE AND YSTB. IE FELT AN SRREHSHTSPLE NEED TO LOVE IER AND YROTEUT IER. AT DAMN, MORN OCT PB SNHOWNSA AND FEVER, IE WADE TIE UALW DEUSHSON TO WARRB IER SN ORDER TO FREE IER FROW TIE DEHYOTSHW OF IER GRANDWOTIER AND TO ENXOB ALL TIE NSGITH OF HATSHFAUTSON TIAT HIE MOCLD GSVE TIE HEVENTB WEN. PCT AT TEN O'ULOUK SN TIE WORNSNG, MIEN IE REAUIED UATARSNO'H HTORE, TIE GSRL IAD LEFT TOMN.TSWE WSTSGATED ISH WAD YROYOHAL, PCT ST AGGRAVATED ISH FEELSNGH OF FRCHTRATSON. IE TOOK REFCGE SN MORK. IE REHSGNED ISWHELF TO PESNG A MOWANLEHH WAN FOR ALL ISH LSFE SN ORDER TO ISDE TIE HIAWE OF ISH CHELEHHNEHH. SN TIE WEANTSWE, WELQCFADEH IAD YRSNTED ON ISH YLATEH EVERBTISNG TIAT MAH YRSNTAPLE SN WAUONDO, AND IE LEFT TIE DAGCERREOTBYE LAPORATORB TO TIE FANTAHSEH OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MIO IAD REHOLVED TO CHE ST TO OPTASN HUSENTSFSU YROOF OF TIE EJSHTENUE OF GOD. TIROCGI A UOWYLSUATED YROUEHH OF HCYERSWYOHED EJYOHCREH TAKEN SN DSFFERENT YARTH OF TIE IOCHE, IE MAH HCRE TIAT HOONER OR LATER IE MOCLD GET A DAGCERREOTBYE OF GOD, SF IE EJSHTED, OR YCT AN END ONUE AND FOR ALL TO TIE HCYYOHSTSON OF ISH EJSHTENUE. WELQCFADEH GOT DEEYER SNTO ISH SNTERYRETATSONH OF NOHTRADAWCH. IE MOCLD HTAB CY CNTSL VERB LATE, HCFFOUATSNG SN ISH FADED VELVET VEHT, HURSPPLSNG MSTI ISH TSNB HYARROM IANDH, MIOHE RSNGH IAD LOHT TIE GLOM OF FORWER TSWEH. ONE NSGIT IE TIOCGIT IE IAD FOCND A YREDSUTSON OF TIE FCTCRE OF WAUONDO. ST MAH TO PE A LCWSNOCH USTB MSTI GREAT GLAHH IOCHEH MIERE TIERE MAH NO TRAUE REWASNSNG OF TIE RAUE OF TIE PCENDFA. "ST'H A WSHTAKE," XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TICNDERED. "TIEB MON'T PE IOCHEH OF GLAHH PCT OF SUE, AH S DREAWED, AND TIERE MSLL ALMABH PE A PCENDFA, YER OWNSA HEUCLA HEUCLORCW." ORHCLA FOCGIT TO YREHERVE UOWWON HENHE SN TIAT EJTRAVAGANT IOCHE, IAVSNG PROADENED IER PCHS-NEHH OF LSTTLE UANDB ANSWALH MSTI AN OVEN TIAT MENT ALL NSGIT TCRNSNG OCT PAHKETH AND WORE PAHKETH OF PREAD AND A YRODSGSOCH VARSETB OF YCDDSNGH, WERSNGCEH, AND UOOKSEH, MISUI DSHAYYEARED SN A FEM IOCRH ON TIE ROADH MSNDSNG TIROCGI TIE HMAWY. HIE IAD REAUIED AN AGE MIERE HIE IAD A RSGIT TO REHT, PCT HIE MAH NONETIELEHH WORE AND WORE AUTSVE. HO PCHB MAH HIE SN IER YROHYEROCH ENTERYRSHEH TIAT ONE AFTERNOON HIE LOOKED DSHTRAUTEDLB TOMARD TIE UOCRTBARD MISLE TIE SNDSAN MOWAN IELYED IER HMEETEN TIE DOCGI AND HIE HAM TMO CNKNOMN AND PEACTSFCL ADOLEHUENT GSRLH DOSNG FRAWE EWPROSDERB SN TIE LSGIT OF TIE HCNHET. TIEB MERE REPEUA AND AWARANTA. AH HOON AH TIEB IAD TAKEN OFF TIE WOCRNSNG ULOTIEH FOR TIESR GRANDWOTIER, MISUI TIEB MORE MSTI SNFLEJSPLE RSGOR FOR TIREE BEARH, TIESR PRSGIT ULOTIEH HEEWED TO IAVE GSVEN TIEW A NEM YLAUE SN TIE MORLD. REPEUA, UONTRARB TO MIAT WSGIT IAVE PEEN EJYEUTED, MAH TIE WORE PEACTSFCL. HIE IAD A LSGIT UOWYLEJSON, LARGE AND YEAUEFCL EBEH, AND WAGSUAL IANDH TIAT HEEWED TO MORK OCT TIE DEHSGN OF TIE EWPROSDERB MSTI SNVSHSPLE TIREADH. AWARANTA, TIE BOCNGER, MAH HOWEMIAT GRAUELEHH, PCT HIE IAD TIE NATCRAL DSHTSNUTSON, TIE SNNER TSGITNEHH OF IER DEAD GRAND-WOTIER. NEJT TO TIEW, ALTIOCGI IE MAH ALREADB REVEALSNG TIE YIBHSUAL DRSVE OF ISH FATIER, ARUADSO LOOKED LSKE A UISLD. IE HET APOCT LEARNSNG TIE ART OF HSLVERMORK MSTI ACRELSANO, MIO IAD ALHO TACGIT ISW IOM TO READ AND MRSTE. ORHCLA HCDDENLB REALSZED TIAT TIE IOCHE IAD PEUOWE FCLL OF YEOYLE, TIAT IER UISLDREN MERE ON TIE YOSNT OF WARRBSNG AND IAVSNG UISLDREN, AND TIAT TIEB MOCLD PE OPLSGED TO HUATTER FOR LAUK OF HYAUE. TIEN HIE TOOK OCT TIE WONEB HIE IAD AUUCWCLATED OVER LONG BEARH OF IARD LAPOR, WADE HOWE ARRANGEWENTH MSTI IER UCHTOWERH, AND CNDERTOOK TIE ENLARGEWENT OF TIE IOCHE. HIE IAD A FORWAL YARLOR FOR VSHSTH PCSLT, ANOTIER ONE TIAT MAH WORE UOWFORTAPLE AND UOOL FOR DASLB CHE, A DSNSNG ROOW MSTI A TAPLE MSTI TMELVE YLAUEH MIERE TIE FAWSLB UOCLD HST MSTI ALL OF TIESR GCEHTH, NSNE PEDROOWH MSTI MSNDOMH ON TIE UOCRTBARD AND A LONG YORUI YROTEUTED FROW TIE IEAT OF NOON PB A ROHE GARDEN MSTI A RASLSNG ON MISUI TO YLAUE YOTH OF FERNH AND PEGONSAH. HIE IAD TIE KSTUIEN ENLARGED TO IOLD TMO OVENH. TIE GRANARB MIERE YSLAR TERNERA IAD READ XOHE ARUADSO'H FCTCRE MAH TORN DOMN AND ANOTIER TMSUE AH LARGE PCSLT HO TIAT TIERE MOCLD NEVER PE A LAUK OF FOOD SN TIE IOCHE. HIE IAD PATIH PCSLT SH TIE UOCRTBARD SN TIE HIADE OF TIE UIEHTNCT TREE, ONE FOR TIE MOWEN AND ANOTIER FOR TIE WEN, AND SN TIE REAR A LARGE HTAPLE, A FENUED-SN UISUKEN BARD, A HIED FOR TIE WSLK UOMH, AND AN AVSARB OYEN TO TIE FOCR MSNDH HO TIAT MANDERSNG PSRDH UOCLD ROOHT TIERE AT TIESR YLEAHCRE. FOLLOMED PB DOZENH OF WAHONH AND UARYENTERH, AH SF HIE IAD UONTRAUTED IER ICHPAND'H IALLCUSNATSNG FEVER, ORHCLA FSJED TIE YOHSTSON OF LSGIT AND IEAT AND DSHTRSPCTED HYAUE MSTIOCT TIE LEAHT HENHE OF STH LSWSTATSONH. TIE YRSWSTSVE PCSLDSNG OF TIE FOCNDERH PEUAWE FSLLED MSTI TOOLH AND WATERSALH, OF MORKWEN EJIACHTED PB HMEAT, MIO AHKED EVERBPODB YLEAHE NOT TO WOLEHT TIEW, EJAHYERATED PB TIE HAUK OF PONEH TIAT FOLLOMED TIEW EVERBMIERE MSTI STH DCLL RATTLE. SN TIAT DSHUOWFORT, PREATISNG QCSUKLSWE AND TAR, NO ONE UOCLD HEE VERB MELL IOM FROW TIE POMELH OF TIE EARTI TIERE MAH RSHSNG NOT ONLB TIE LARGEHT IOCHE SH TIE TOMN, PCT TIE WOHT IOHYSTAPLE AND UOOL IOCHE TIAT IAD EVER EJSHTED SN TIE REGSON OF TIE HMAWY. XOHE PCENDFA, TRBSNG TO HCRYRSHE DSVSNE YROVSDENUE SN TIE WSDHT OF TIE UATAULBHW, MAH TIE ONE MIO LEAHT CNDERHTOOD ST. TIE NEM IOCHE MAH ALWOHT FSNSHIED MIEN ORHCLA DREM ISW OCT OF ISH UISWERSUAL MORLD SN ORDER TO SNFORW ISW TIAT HIE IAD AN ORDER TO YASNT TIE FRONT PLCE AND NOT MISTE AH TIEB IAD MANTED. HIE HIOMED ISW TIE OFFSUSAL DOUCWENT. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MSTIOCT CNDERHTANDSNG MIAT ISH MSFE MAH TALKSNG APOCT, DEUSYIERED TIE HSGNATCRE."MIO SH TISH FELLOM?" IE AHKED:"TIE WAGSHTRATE," ORHCLA ANHMERED DSHUONHOLATELB. TIEB HAB IE'H AN ACTIORSTB HENT PB TIE GOVERNWENT."DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE, TIE WAGSHTRATE, IAD ARRSVED SN WAUONDO VERB QCSETLB. IE HET CY A TAPLE AND A UIASR TIAT IE IAD POCGIT FROW XAUOP, NASLED CY ON TIE MALL TIE HISELD OF TIE REYCPLSU TIAT IE IAD PROCGIT MSTI ISW, AND ON TIE DOOR IE YASNTED TIE HSGN:WAGSHTRATE. ISH FSRHT ORDER MAH FOR ALL TIE IOCHEH TO PE YASNTED PLCE SN UELEPRATSON OF TIE ANNSVERHARB OF NATSONAL SNDEYENDENUE. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MSTI TIE UOYB OF TIE ORDER SN ISH IAND, FOCND ISW TAKSNG ISH NAY SN A IAWWOUK IE IAD HET CY SN TIE NARROM OFFSUE. "DSD BOC MRSTE TISH YAYER?" IE AHKED ISW. DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE, A WATCRE WAN, TSWSD, MSTI A RCDDB UOWYLEJSON, HASD BEH. "PB MIAT RSGIT?" XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AHKED AGASN. DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE YSUKED CY A YAYER FROW TIE DRAMER OF TIE TAPLE AND HIOMED ST TO ISW. "S IAVE PEEN NAWED WAGSHTRATE OF TISH TOMN." "AND HO TIAT BOC KNOM ST ONUE AND FOR ALL, ME DON'T NEED ANB XCDGE IERE PEUACHE TIERE'H NOTISNG TIAT NEEDH XCDGSNG."FAUSNG DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE, HTSLL MSTIOCT RASHSNG ISH VOSUE, IE GAVE A DETASLED AUUOCNT OF IOM TIEB IAD FOCNDED TIE VSLLAGE, OF IOM TIEB IAD DSHTRSPCTED TIE LAND, OYENED TIE ROADH, AND SNTRODCUED TIE SWYROVEWENTH TIAT NEUEHHSTB REQCSRED MSTIOCT IAVSNG POTIERED TIE GOVERNWENT AND MSTIOCT ANBONE IAVSNG POTIERED TIEW. "ME ARE HO YEAUEFCL TIAT NONE OF CH IAH DSED EVEN OF A NATCRAL DEATI," IE HASD. "BOC UAN HEE TIAT ME HTSLL DON'T IAVE ANB UEWETERB." NO ONUE MAH CYHET TIAT TIE GOVERNWENT IAD NOT IELYED TIEW. ON TIE UONTRARB, TIEB MERE IAYYB TIAT CY CNTSL TIEN ST IAD LET TIEW GROM SN YEAUE, AND IE IOYED TIAT ST MOCLD UONTSNCE LEAVSNG TIEW TIAT MAB, PEUACHE TIEB IAD NOT FOCNDED A TOMN HO TIAT TIE FSRHT CYHTART MIO UAWE ALONG MOCLD TELL TIEW MIAT TO DO. PEUACHE WB IOCHE SH GOSNG TO PE MISTE, MISTE, LSKE A DOVE."DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE TCRNED YALE. IE TOOK A HTEY PAUKMARD AND TSGITENED ISH XAMH AH IE HASD MSTI A UERTASN AFFLSUTSON: "S WCHT MARN BOC TIAT S'W ARWED."XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA DSD NOT KNOM EJAUTLB MIEN ISH IANDH REGASNED TIE CHEFCL HTRENGTI MSTI MISUI IE CHED TO YCLL DOMN IORHEH. IE GRAPPED DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE PB TIE LAYELH AND LSFTED ISW CY TO TIE LEVEL OFISH EBEH. "S'W DOSNG TISH," IE HASD, "PEUACHE S MOCLD RATIER UARRB BOC AROCND ALSVE AND NOT IAVE TO KEEY UARRBSNG BOC AROCND DEAD FOR TIE REHT OF WB LSFE."SN TIAT MAB IE UARRSED ISW TIROCGI TIE WSDDLE OF TIE HTREET, HCHYENDED PB TIE LAYELH, CNTSL IE YCT ISW DOMN ON ISH TMO FEET ON TIE HMAWY ROAD. A MEEK LATER IE MAH PAUK MSTI HSJ PAREFOOT AND RAGGED HOLDSERH, ARWED MSTI HIOTGCNH, AND AN OJUART SN MISUI ISH MSFE AND HEVEN DACGITERH MERE TRAVELSNG. TMO OTIER UARTH ARRSVED LATER MSTI TIE FCRNSTCRE, TIE PAGGAGE, AND TIE IOCHEIOLD CTENHSLH. IE HETTLED ISH FAWSLB SN TIE IOTEL XAUOP, MISLE IE LOOKED FOR A IOCHE, AND IE MENT PAUK TO OYEN ISH OFFSUE CNDER TIE YROTEUTSON OF TIE HOLDSERH. TIE FOCNDERH OF WAUONDO, REHOLVSNG TO EJYEL TIE SNVADERH, MENT MSTI TIESR OLDER HONH TO YCT TIEWHELVEH AT TIE DSHYOHAL OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA. PCT IE MAH AGASNHT ST, AH IE EJYLASNED, PEUACHE ST MAH NOT WANLB TO WAKE TROCPLE FOR HOWEONE SN FRONT OF ISH FAWSLB, AND DON AYOLSNAR IAD RETCRNED MSTI ISH MSFE AND DACGITERH. HO IE DEUSDED TO REHOLVE TIE HSTCATSON SN A YLEAHANT MAB. ACRELSANO MENT MSTI ISW. APOCT TIAT TSWE IE IAD PEGCN TO UCLTSVATE TIE PLAUK WCHTAUIE MSTI MAJED TSYH AND TIE HOWEMIAT HTENTORSAN VOSUE TIAT MOCLD UIARAUTERSZE ISW SN TIE MAR. CNARWED, MSTIOCT YABSNG ANB ATTENTSON TO TIE GCARDH, TIEB MENT SNTO TIE WAGSHTRATE'H OFFSUE. DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE DSD NOT LOHE ISH UALW. IE SNTRODCUED TIEW TO TMO OF ISH DACGITERH MIO IAYYENED TO PE TIERE: AWYARO, HSJTEEN, DARK LSKE IER WOTIER, AND REWEDSOH, ONLB NSNE, A YRETTB LSTTLE GSRL MSTI LSLB-UOLORED HKSN AND GREEN EBEH. TIEB MERE GRAUSOCH AND MELL-WANNERED. AH HOON AH TIE WEN UAWE SN, PEFORE PESNG SNTRODCUED, TIEB GAVE TIEW UIASRH TO HST ON. PCT TIEB POTI REWASNED HTANDSNG."VERB MELL, WB FRSEND," XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA HASD, "BOC WAB HTAB IERE, NOT PEUACHE BOC IAVE TIOHE PANDSTH MSTI HIOTGCNH AT TIE DOOR, PCT OCT OF UONHSDERATSON FOR BOCR MSFE AND DACGITERH." DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE MAH CYHET, PCT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA DSD NOT GSVEISW TSWE TO REYLB. "ME ONLB WAKE TMO UONDSTSONH," IE MENT ON. "TIE FSRHT: TIAT EVERBONE UAN YASNT ISH IOCHE TIE UOLOR IE FEELH LSKE. TIE HEUOND: TIAT TIE HOLDSERH LEAVE AT ONUE. ME MSLL GCARAN-TEE ORDER FOR BOC." TIE WAGSHTRATE RASHED ISH RSGIT IAND MSTI ALL TIE FSNGERH EJTENDED. "BOCR MORD OF IONOR?""TIE MORD OF BOCR ENEWB," XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA HASD. AND IE ADDED SN A PSTTER TONE: "PEUACHE S WCHT TELL BOC ONE TISNG: BOC AND S ARE HTSLL ENEWSEH."TIE HOLDSERH LEFT TIAT HAWE AFTERNOON. TIE SWAGE OF REWEDSOH, TIE WAGSHTRATE'H BOCNGER DACGITER, MIO, PEUACHE OF IER AGE, UOCLD IAVE PEEN ISH DACGITER, KEYT YASNSNG ISW SN HOWE YART OF ISH PODB. ST MAH A YIBHSUAL HENHATSON TIAT ALWOHT POTIERED ISW MIEN IE MALKED, LSKE A YEPPLE SN ISH HIOE.UIAYTER 4TIE NEM IOCHE, MISTE, LSKE A DOVE, MAH SNACGCRATED MSTI A DANUE.ORHCLA IAD GOT TIAT SDEA FROW TIE AFTERNOON MIEN HIE HAM REPEUAAND AWARANTA UIANGED SNTO ADOLEHUENTH, AND ST UOCLD ALWOHT IAVE PEENHASD TIAT TIE WASN REAHON PEISND TIE UONHTRCUTSON MAH A DEHSRE TO IAVE AYROYER YLAUE FOR TIE GSRLH TO REUESVE VSHSTORH. SN ORDER TIAT NOTISNG MOCLDPE LAUKSNG SN HYLENDOR HIE MORKED LSKE A GALLEB HLAVE AH TIE REYASRH MERECNDER MAB, HO TIAT PEFORE TIEB MERE FSNSHIED HIE IAD ORDERED UOHTLBNEUEHHSTSEH FOR TIE DEUORATSONH, TIE TAPLE HERVSUE, AND TIE WARVELOCHSNVENTSON TIAT MAH TO AROCHE TIE AHTONSHIWENT OF TIE TOMN AND TIEXCPSLATSON OF TIE BOCNG YEOYLE: TIE YSANOLA. TIEB DELSVERED ST PROKENDOMN, YAUKED SN HEVERAL POJEH TIAT MERE CNLOADED ALONG MSTI TIEVSENNEHE FCRNSTCRE, TIE POIEWSAN URBHTAL, TIE TAPLE HERVSUE FROW TIESNDSEH UOWYANB, TIE TAPLEULOTIH FROW IOLLAND, AND A RSUI VARSETB OFLAWYH AND UANDLEHTSUKH, IANGSNGH AND DRAYEH. TIE SWYORT IOCHE HENTALONG AT STH OMN EJYENHE AN STALSAN EJYERT, YSETRO UREHYS, TO AHHEWPLEAND TCNE TIE YSANOLA, TO SNHTRCUT TIE YCRUIAHERH SN STH FCNUTSONSNG, AND TOTEAUI TIEW IOM TO DANUE TIE LATEHT WCHSU YRSNTED ON STH HSJ YAYER ROLLH.YSETRO UREHYS MAH BOCNG AND PLOND, TIE WOHT IANDHOWE AND MELL WANNERED WAN MIO IAD EVER PEEN HEEN SN WAUONDO, HO HURCYCLOCH SN ISH DREHH TIAT SN HYSTE OF TIE HCFFOUATSNG IEAT IE MOCLD MORK SN ISH PROUADE VEHT AND IEAVB UOAT OF DARK ULOTI. HOAKED SN HMEAT, KEEYSNG A REVERENT DSHTANUE FROW TIE OMNERH OF TIE IOCHE, IE HYENT HEVERAL MEEKH HICT CY SH TIE YARLOR MSTI A DEDSUATSON WCUI LSKE TIAT OF ACRELSANO SN ISH HSLVERMORK. ONE WORNSNG, MSTIOCT OYENSNG TIE DOOR, MSTIOCT UALLSNG ANBONE TO MSTNEHH TIE WSRAULE, IE YLAUED TIE FSRHT ROLL SN TIE YSANOLA AND TIE TORWENTSNG IAWWERSNG AND TIE UONHTANT NOSHE OF MOODEN LATISNGH UEAHED SN A HSLENUE TIAT MAH HTARTLED AT TIE ORDER AND NEATNEHH OF TIE WCHSU. TIEB ALL RAN TO TIE YARLOR. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MAH AH SF HTRCUK PB LSGITNSNG, NOT PEUACHE OF TIE PEACTB OF TIE WELODB, PCT PEUACHE OF TIE ACTOWATSU MORKSNG OF TIE KEBH OF TIE YSANOLA, AND IE HET CY WELQCFADEH' UAWERA MSTI TIE IOYE OF GETTSNG A DAGCERREOTBYE OF TIE SNVSHSPLE YLABER. TIAT DAB TIE STALSAN IAD LCNUI MSTI TIEW. REPEUA AND AWARANTA, HERVSNG TIE TAPLE, MERE SNTSWSDATED PB TIE MAB SN MISUI TIE ANGELSU WAN MSTI YALE AND RSNGLEHH IANDH WANSYCLATED TIE CTENHSLH. SN TIE LSVSNG ROOW, NEJT TO TIE YARLOR, YSETRO UREHYS TACGIT TIEW IOM TO DANUE. IE HIOMED TIEW TIE HTEYH MSTIOCT TOCUISNG TIEW, KEEYSNG TSWE MSTI A WETRONOWE, CNDER TIE FRSENDLB EBE OF ORHCLA, MIO DSD NOT LEAVE TIE ROOW FOR A WOWENT MISLE IER DACGITERH IAD TIESR LEHHON. YSETRO UREHYS MORE HYEUSAL YANTH ON TIOHE DABH, VERB ELAHTSU AND TSGIT, AND DANUSNG HLSYYERH, "BOC DON'T IAVE TO MORRB HO WCUI," XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TOLD IER. "TIE WAN'H A FASRB." PCT HIE DSD NOT LEAVE OFF IER VSGSLANUE CNTSL TIE AYYRENTSUEHISY MAH OVER AND TIE STALSAN LEFT WAUONDO. TIEN TIEB PEGAN TO ORGANSZE TIE YARTB. ORHCLA DREM CY A HTRSUT GCEHT LSHT, SN MISUI TIE ONLB ONEH SNVSTED MERE TIE DEHUENDANTH OF TIE FOCNDERH, EJUEYT FOR TIE FAWSLB OF YSLAR TERNERA, MIO PB TIEN IAD IAD TMO WORE UISLDREN PB CNKNOMN FATIERH. ST MAH TRCLB A ISGI-ULAHH LSHT, EJUEYT TIAT ST MAH DETERWSNED PB FEELSNGH OF FRSENDHISY, FOR TIOHE FAVORED MERE NOT ONLB TIE OLDEHT FRSENDH OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA'H IOCHE HSNUE PEFORE TIEB CNDERTOOK TIE EJODCH AND TIE FOCNDSNG OF WAUONDO, PCT ALHO TIESR HONH AND GRANDHONH, MIO MERE TIE UONHTANT UOWYANSONH OF ACRELSANO AND ARUADSO HSNUE SNFANUB, AND TIESR DACGITERH, MIO MERE TIE ONLB ONEH MIO VSHSTED TIE IOCHE TO EWPROSDER MSTI REPEUA AND AWARANTA. DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE, TIE PENEVOLENT RCLER MIOHE AUTSVSTB IAD PEEN REDCUED TO TIE WASNTENANUE FROW ISH HUANTB REHOCRUEH OF TMO YOLSUEWEN ARWED MSTI MOODEN ULCPH, MAH A FSGCREIEAD. SN OLDER TO HCYYORT TIE IOCHEIOLD EJYENHEH ISH DACGITERH IAD OYENED A HEMSNG HIOY, MIERE TIEB WADE FELT FLOMERH AH MELL AH GCAVA DELSUAUSEH, AND MROTE LOVE NOTEH TO ORDER. PCT SN HYSTE OF PESNG WODEHT AND IARD-MORKSNG, TIE WOHT PEACTSFCL GSRLH SN SOMA, AND TIE WOHT HKSLLED AT TIE NEM DANUEH, TIEB DSD NOT WANAGE TO PE UONHSDERED FOR TIE YARTB.MISLE ORHCLA AND TIE GSRLH CNYAUKED FCRNSTCRE, YOL-SHIED HSLVERMARE, AND ICNG YSUTCREH OF WASDENH SN POATH FCLL OF ROHEH, MISUI GAVE A PREATI OF NEM LSFE TO TIE NAKED AREAH TIAT TIE WAHONH IAD PCSLT, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA HTOYYED ISH YCRHCST OF TIE SWAGE OF GOD, UONVSNUED OF ISH NONEJSHTENUE, AND IE TOOK TIE YSANOLA AYART SN ORDER TO DEUSYIER STH WAGSUAL HEURET. TMO DABH PEFORE TIE YARTB, HMAWYED SN A HIOMER OF LEFTOVER KEBH AND IAWWERH, PCNGLSNG SN TIE WSDHT OF A WSJ-CY OF HTRSNGH TIAT MOCLD CNROLL SN ONE DSREUTSON AND ROLL CY AGASN SN TIE OTIER, IE HCUUEEDED SN A FAHISON SN YCTTSNG TIE SNHTRCWENT PAUK TOGETIER. TIERE IAD NEVER PEEN AH WANB HCRYRSHEH AND AH WCUI DAHISNG APOCT AH SN TIOHE DABH, PCT TIE NEM YSTUI LAWYH MERE LSGITED ON TIE DEHSGNATED DAB AND IOCR. TIE IOCHE MAH OYENED, HTSLL HWELLSNG OF REHSN AND DAWY MISTEMAHI, AND TIE UISLDREN AND GRANDUISLDREN OF TIE FOCNDERH HAM TIE YORUI MSTI FERNH AND PEGONSAH, TIE QCSET ROOWH, TIE GARDEN HATCRATED MSTI TIE FRAGRANUE OF TIE ROHEH, AND TIEB GATIERED TOGETIER SN TIE YARLOR, FAUSNG TIE CNKNOMN SNVENTSON TIAT IAD PEEN UOVERED MSTI A MISTE HIEET. TIOHE MIO MERE FAWSLSAR MSTI TIE YSANO, YOYCLAR SN OTIER TOMNH SN TIE HMAWY, FELT A LSTTLE DSHIEARTENED, PCT WORE PSTTER MAH ORHCLA'H DSHAYYOSNTWENT MIEN HIE YCT SN TIE FSRHT ROLL HO TIAT AWARANTA AND REPEUA UOCLD PEGSN TIE DANUSNG AND TIE WEUIANSHW DSD NOT MORK. WELQCFADEH, ALWOHT PLSND PB TIEN, URCWPLSNG MSTI DEUREYSTCDE, CHED TIE ARTH OF ISH TSWELEHH MSHDOW SN AN ATTEWYT TO FSJ ST. FSNALLB XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA WANAGED, PB WSHTAKE, TO WOVE A DEVSUE TIAT MAH HTCUK AND TIE WCHSU UAWE OCT, FSRHT SN A PCRHT AND TIEN SN A FLOM OF WSJED-CY NOTEH. PEATSNG AGASNHT TIE HTRSNGH TIAT IAD PEEN YCT SN MSTIOCT ORDER OR UONUERT AND IAD PEEN TCNED MSTI TEWERSTB, TIE IAWWERH LET GO. PCT TIE HTCPPORN DEHUENDANTH OF TIE TMENTB-ONE SNTREYSD YEOYLE MIO YLOMED TIROCGI TIE WOCNTASNH SN HEARUI OF TIE HEA TO TIE MEHT AVOSDED TIE REEFH OF TIE WELODSU WSJ-CY AND TIE DANUSNG MENT ON CNTSL DAMN.YSETRO UREHYS UAWE PAUK TO REYASR TIE YSANOLA. REPEUA AND AWARANTA IELYED ISW YCT TIE HTRSNGH SN ORDER AND IELYED ISW MSTI TIESR LACGITER AT TIE WSJ-CY OF TIE WELODSEH. ST MAH EJTREWELB YLEAHANT AND HO UIAHTE SN STH MAB TIAT ORHCLA UEAHED IER VSGSLANUE. ON TIE EVE OF ISH DEYARTCRE A FAREMELL DANUE FOR ISW MAH SWYROVSHED MSTI TIE YSANOLA AND MSTIREPEUA IE YCT ON A HKSLLFCL DEWONHTRATSON OF WODERN DANUE, ARUADSO AND AWARAN-TA WATUIED TIEW SN GRAUE AND HKSLL. ALTIOCGI HIE HEEWED EJYANHSVE AND UORDSAL, HIE IAD A HOLSTARB UIARAUTER AND AN SWYENETRAPLE IEART. HIE MAH A HYLENDSD ADOLEHUENT MSTI LONG AND FSRW PONEH, PCT HIE HTSLL SNHSHTED ON CHSNG TIE HWALL MOODEN ROUKSNG UIASR MSTI MISUI HIE IAD ARRSVED AT TIE IOCHE, RESNFORUED WANB TSWEH AND MSTI TIE ARWH GONE. NO ONE IAD DSHUOVERED TIAT EVEN AT TIAT AGE HIE HTSLL IAD TIE IAPST OF HCUKSNG IER FSNGER. TIAT MAH MIB HIE MOCLD NOT LOHE AN OYYORTCNSTB TO LOUK IERHELF SN TIE PATIROOW AND IAD AUQCSRED TIE IAPST OF HLEEYSNG MSTI IER FAUE TO TIE MALL. ON RASNB AFTERNOONH, EWPROSDERSNG MSTI A GROCY OF FRSENDH ON TIE PEGONSA YORUI, HIE MOCLD LOHE TIE TIREAD OF TIE UONVERHATSON AND A TEAR OF NOHTALGSA MOCLD HALT IER YALATE MIEN HIE HAM TIE HTRSYH OF DAWY EARTI AND TIE YSLEH OF WCD TIAT TIE EARTIMORWH IAD YCHIED CY SN TIE GARDEN. TIE FSRHT TSWE HIE DSD ST ALWOHT OCT OF UCRSOHSTB, HCRE TIAT TIE PAD TAHTE MOCLD PE TIE PEHT UCRE FOR TIE TEWYTATSON. AND, SN FAUT, HIE UOCLD NOT PEAR TIE EARTI SN IER WOCTI. PCT HIE YERHEVERED, OVERUOWE PB TIE GROMSNG ANJSETB, AND LSTTLE PB LSTTLE HIE MAH GETTSNG PAUK IER ANUEHTRAL AYYETSTE, TIE TAHTE OF YRSWARB WSNERALH, TIE CNPRSDLED HATSHFAUTSON OF MIAT MAH TIE ORSGSNAL FOOD. HIE MOCLD YCT IANDFCLH OF EARTI SN IER YOUKETH, AND ATE TIEW SN HWALL PSTH MSTIOCT PESNG HEEN, MSTI A UONFCHED FEELSNG OF YLEAHCRE AND RAGE, AH HIE SNHTRCUTED IER GSRL FRSENDH SN TIE WOHT DSFFSUCLT NEEDLEYOSNT AND HYOKE APOCT OTIER WEN, MIO DSD NOT DEHERVE TIE HAURSFSUE OF IAVSNG ONE EAT TIE MISTEMAHI ON TIE MALLH PEUACHE OF TIEW. TIE IANDFCLH OF EARTI WADE TIE ONLB WAN MIO DEHERVED TIAT HIOM OF DEGRADATSON LEHH REWOTE AND WORE UERTASN, AH SF TIE GROCND TIAT IE MALKED ON MSTI ISH FSNE YATENT LEATIER POOTH SN ANOTIER YART OF TIE MORLD MERE TRANHWSTTSNG TO IER TIE MESGIT AND TIE TEWYERATCRE OF ISH PLOOD SN A WSNERAL HAVOR TIAT LEFT A IARHI AFTERTAHTE SN IER WOCTI AND A HEDSWENT OF YEAUE SN IER IEART. ONE AFTERNOON, FOR NO REAHON, AWYARO WOHUOTE AHKED YERWSHHSON TO HEE TIE IOCHE. AWARANTA AND REPEUA, DSHUONUERTED PB TIE CNEJYEUTED VSHST, ATTENDED IER MSTI A HTSFF FORWALSTB. TIEB HIOMED IER TIE REWODELED WANHSON, TIEB IAD IER LSHTEN TO TIE ROLLH ON TIE YSANOLA, AND TIEB OFFERED IER ORANGE WARWALADE AND URAUKERH. AWYARO GAVE A LEHHON SN DSGNSTB, YERHONAL UIARW, AND GOOD WANNERH TIAT SWYREHHED ORHCLA SN TIE FEM WOWENTH TIAT HIE MAH YREHENT DCRSNG TIE VSHST. AFTER TMO IOCRH, MIEN TIE UONVERHATSON MAH PEGSNNSNG TO MANE, AWYARO TOOK ADVANTAGE OF AWARANTA'H DSHTRAUTSON AND GAVE REPEUA A LETTER. HIE MAH APLE TO HEE TIE NAWE OF TIE EHTSWAPLE HENORSTA REPEUA PCENDFA, MRSTTEN SN TIE HAWE WETIOD-SUAL IAND, MSTI TIE HAWE GREEN SNK, AND TIE HAWE DELSUAUB OF MORDH MSTI MISUI TIE SNHTRCUTSONH FOR TIE OYERATSON OF TIE YSANOLA MERE MRSTTEN, AND HIE FOLDED TIE LETTER MSTI TIE TSYH OF IER FSNGERH AND ISD ST SN IER POHOW, LOOKSNG AT AWYARO WOHUOTE MSTI AN EJYREHHSON OF ENDLEHH AND CNUONDSTSONAL GRATSTCDE AND A HSLENT YROWSHE OF UOWYLSUSTB CNTO DEATI.TIE HCDDEN FRSENDHISY PETMEEN AWYARO WOHUOTE AND REPEUA PCENDFA AMAKENED TIE IOYEH OF ACRELSANO. TIE WEWORB OF LSTTLE REWEDSOH IAD NOT HTOYYED TORWENTSNG ISW, PCT IE IAD NOT FOCND A UIANUE TO HEE IER. MIEN IE MOCLD HTROLL TIROCGI TOMN MSTI ISH ULOHEHT FRSENDH, WAGNFFSUO VSHPAL AND GERSNELDO WARQCEZ-TIE HONH OF TIE FOCNDERH OF TIE HAWE NAWEH-IE MOCLD LOOK FOR IER SN TIE HEMSNG HIOY MSTI AN ANJSOCH GLANUE, PCT IE HAM ONLB TIE OLDER HSHTERH. TIE YREHENUE OF AWYARO WOHUOTE SN TIE IOCHE MAH LSKE A YREWONSTSON. "HIE IAH TO UOWE MSTI IER," ACRELSANO MOCLD HAB TO ISWHELF SN A LOM VOSUE. "HIE IAH TO UOWE." "UOWE SN."REWEDSOH MENT OVER AND AHKED HOWE QCEHTSONH APOCT TIE FSHI TIAT ACRELSANO UOCLD NOT ANHMER PEUACHE IE MAH HESZED MSTI A HCDDEN ATTAUK OF AHTIWA. WELQCFADEH MAH SN TIE UORNER HEATED AT TIE DEHK HURSPPLSNG SNDEUSYIERAPLE HSGNH. ACRELSANO IATED ISW. ALL IE UOCLD DO MAH TELL REWEDSOH TIAT IE MAH GOSNG TO GSVE IER TIE LSTTLE FSHI AND TIE GSRL MAH HO HTARTLED PB TIE OFFER TIAT HIE LEFT TIE MORKHIOY AH FAHT AH HIE UOCLD. TIAT AFTERNOON ACRELSANO LOHT TIE ISDDEN YATSENUE MSTI MISUI IE IAD MASTED FOR A UIANUE TO HEE IER. IE NEGLEUTED ISH MORK. SN HEVERAL DEHYERATE EFFORTH OF UONUENTRATSON IE MSLLED IER TO AYYEAR PCT REWEDSOH DSD NOT REHYOND. IE LOOKED FOR IER SN IER HSHTERH' HIOY, PEISND TIE MSNDOM HIADEH SN IER IOCHE, SN IER FATIER'H OFFSUE, PCT IE FOCND IER ONLB SN TIE SWAGE TIAT HATCRATED ISH YRSVATE AND TERRSPLE HOLSTCDE. ACRELSANO LSHTENED TO ST HSWYLB PEUACHE EVERBTISNG, EVEN WCHSU, REWSNDED ISW OF REWEDSOH. TIE IOCHE PEUAWE FCLL OF LOVEH ACRELSANO EJYREHHED ST SN YOETRB TIAT IAD NO PEGSNNSNG OR END. ST IAYYENED QCSTE TIE OYYOHSTE: ONUE TIE WCLE DSD NOT UOWE ON TIE CHCAL DAB. IE IAD DSHUOVERED TIAT TIE WORE IE DRANK TIE WORE IE TIOCGIT APOCT REWEDSOH, PCT IE UOCLD PEAR TIE TORTCRE OF ISH REUOLLEUTSONH PETTER. IE DSD NOT KNOM EJAUTLB MIEN IE PEGAN TO FLOAT. ACRELSANO TCRNED ISH IEAD, HAM TIE ENORWOCH DSHFSGCRED FAUE MSTI A FELT FLOMER PEISND TIE EAR, AND TIEN IE LOHT ISH WEWORB, AH DCRSNG TIE TSWEH OF FORGETFCLNEHH, AND IE REUOVERED ST ON A HTRANGE DAMN AND SN A ROOW TIAT MAH UOWYLETELB FORESGN, MIERE YSLAR TERNERA HTOOD SN IER HLSY, PAREFOOT, IER IASR DOMN, IOLDSNG A LAWY OVER ISW, HTARTLED MSTI DSHPELSEF. "ACRELSANO!"ACRELSANO UIEUKED ISH FEET AND RASHED ISH IEAD. IE DSD NOT KNOM IOM IE IAD UOWE TIERE, PCT IE KNEM MIAT ISH ASW MAH, PEUACHE IE IAD UARRSED ST ISDDEN HSNUE SNFANUB SN AN SNVSOLAPLE PAUKMATER OF ISH IEART. "S'VE UOWE TO HLEEY MSTI BOC," IE HASD.ISH ULOTIEH MERE HWEARED MSTI WCD AND VOWST. YSLAR TERNERA, MIO LSVED ALONE AT TIAT TSWE MSTI IER TMO BOCNGER UISLDREN, DSD NOT AHK ISW ANB QCEHTSONH. HIE TOOK ISW TO TIE PED. HIE ULEANED ISH FAUE MSTI A DAWY ULOTI, TOOK OF ISH ULOTIEH, AND TIEN GOT UOWYLETELB CNDREHHED AND LOMERED TIE WOHQCSTO NETTSNG HO TIAT IER UISLDREN MOCLD NOT HEE TIEW SF TIEB MOKE CY. MSTI A UALW HKSLL, MSTIOCT TIE HLSGITEHT WSHHTEY, IE LEFT ISH AUUCWCLATED GRSEF PEISND AND FOCND REWEDSOH UIANGED SNTO A HMAWY MSTIOCT IORSZONH, HWELLSNG OF A RAM ANSWAL AND REUENTLB SRONED ULOTIEH. PCT ST MAH A PAD WOWENT, PEUACHE TIE IOCHE IAD LOHT STH YEAUE OF FORWER DABH. MIEN HIE DSHUOVERED REPEUA'H YAHHSON, MISUI MAH SWYOHHSPLE TO KEEY HEURET PEUACHE OF IER HIOCTH, AWARANTA HCFFERED AN ATTAUK OF FEVER. HIE ALHO HCFFERED FROW TIE PARP OF A LONELB LOVE. HICT CY SN TIE PATIROOW, HIE MOCLD RELEAHE IERHELF FROW TIE TORWENT OF A IOYELEHH YAHHSON PB MRSTSNG FEVERSHI LETTERH, MISUI HIE FSNALLB ISD SN TIE POTTOW OF IER TRCNK. FSNALLB, SN ANOTIER WOWENT OF SNHYSRATSON, HIE FORUED TIE LOUK ON TIE TRCNK AND FOCND TIE LETTERH TSED MSTI A YSNK RSPPON, HMOLLEN MSTI FREHI LSLSEH AND HTSLL MET MSTI TEARH, ADDREHHED AND NEVER HENT TO YSETRO UREHYS. CHELEHH MAH TIE SNTERVENTSON OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MIO IAD WODSFSED ISH FSRHT SWYREHHSON OF YSETRO UREHYS AND ADWSRED ISH APSLSTB SN TIE WANSYCLA-TSON OF WCHSUAL WAUISNEH. SNVSTED TO TIE YARLOR FOR A FORWAL SNTERVSEM, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AND ORHCLA LSHTENED HTONSLB TO TIESR HON'H DEULARATSON. MIEN IE LEARNED TIE NAWE OF TIE FSANUEE, IOMEVER, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA GREM RED MSTI SNDSGNATSON. "LOVE SH A DSHEAHE," IE TICNDERED. HIE UONFEHHED IER AFFEUTSON FOR TIE HEVEN WOHUOTE HSHTERH. FOR TIESR PEACTB, TIESR APSLSTB FOR MORK, TIESR WODEHTB, AND TIESR GOOD WANNERH, AND HIE UELE-PRATED IER HON'H YRCDENUE. UONQCERED PB ISH MSFE'H ENTICHSAHW, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TIEN LASD DOMN ONE UONDSTSON: REPEUA, MIO MAH TIE ONE IE MANTED, MOCLD WARRB YSETRO UREHYS. ORHCLA MOCLD TAKE AWARANTA ON A TRSY TO TIE UAYSTAL OF TIE YROVSNUE MIEN HIE IAD TSWE, HO TIAT UONTAUT MSTI DSFFERENT YEOYLE MOCLD ALLEVSATE IER DSHAYYOSNTWENT. REPEUA GOT IER IEALTI PAUK XCHT AH HOON AH HIE IEARD OF TIE AGREEWENT, AND HIE MROTE IER FSANUE A XCPSLANT LETTER TIAT HIE HCPWSTTED TO IER YARENTH' AYYROVAL AND YCT SNTO TIE WASL MSTIOCT TIE CHE OF ANB SNTERWEDSARSEH. AWARANTA YRETENDED TO AUUEYT TIE DEUSHSON AND LSTTLE PB LSTTLE HIE REUOVERED FROW IER FEVERH, PCT HIE YROWSHED IERHELF TIAT REPEUA MOCLD WARRB ONLB OVER IER DEAD PODB.TIE FOLLOMSNG HATCRDAB XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA YCT ON ISH DARK HCST, ISH UELLCLOSD UOLLAR, AND TIE DEERHKSN POOTH TIAT IE IAD MORN FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE TIE NSGIT OF TIE YARTB, AND MENT TO AHK FOR TIE IAND OF REWEDSOH WOHUOTE. TIE WAGSHTRATE AND ISH MSFE REUESVED ISW, YLEAHED AND MORRSED AT TIE HAWE TSWE, FOR TIEB DSD NOT KNOM TIE REAHON FOR TIE CNEJYEUTED VSHST, AND TIEN TIEB TIOCGIT TIAT IE MAH UONFCHED APOCT TIE NAWE OF TIE SNTENDED PRSDE. SN ORDER TO REWOVE TIE WSHTAKE, TIE WOTIER MOKE REWEDSOH CY AND UARRSED IER SNTO TIE LSVSNG ROOW, HTSLL DROMHB FROW HLEEY. TIEB AHKED IER SF ST MAH TRCE TIAT HIE IAD DEUSDED TO GET WARRSED, AND HIE ANHMERED, MISWYERSNG, TIAT HIE ONLB MANTED TIEW TO LET IER HLEEY. XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, CNDERHTANDSNG TIE DSHTREHH OF TIE WOHUOTEH, MENT TO ULEAR TISNGH CY MSTI ACRELSANO. MIEN IE RETCRNED, TIE WOHUOTEH IAD YCT ON FORWAL ULOTISNG, IAD REARRANGED TIE FCRNSTCRE AND YCT FREHI FLOMERH SN TIE VAHEH, AND MERE MASTSNG SN TIE UOWYANB OF TIESR OLDER DACGITERH. OVERMIELWED PB TIE CNYLEAHANTNEHH OF TIE OUUAHSON AND TIE POTIERHOWE IARD UOLLAR, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA UONFSRWED TIE FAUT TIAT REWEDSOH, SNDEED, MAH TIE UIOHEN ONE. "ST DOEHN'T WAKE HENHE," DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE HASD MSTI UONHTERNATSON. "ME IAVE HSJ OTIER DACGITERH, ALL CNWARRSED, AND AT AN AGE MIERE TIEB DEHERVE ST, MIO MOCLD PE DELSGITED TO PE TIE IONORAPLE MSFE OF A GENTLEWAN AH HERSOCH AND IARD-MORKSNG AH BOCR HON, AND ACRELSTO LABH ISH EBEH YREUSHELB ON TIE ONE MIO HTSLL METH IER PED." ISH MSFE, A MELL-YREHERVED MOWAN MSTI AFFLSUTED EBELSDH AND EJYREHHSON, HUOLDED ISH WSHTAKE. MIEN TIEB FSNSHIED TIE FRCST YCNUI, TIEB MSLLSNGLB AUUEYTED ACRELSANO'H DEUSHSON. EJ-UEYT TIAT HENORA WOHUOTE PEGGED TIE FAVOR OF HYEAKSNG TO ORHCLA ALONE. SNTRSGCED, YROTEHTSNG TIAT TIEB MERE SNVOLVSNG IER SN WEN'H AFFASRH, PCT REALLB FEELSNG DEEY EWOTSON, ORHCLA MENT TO VSHST IER TIE NEJT DAB. A IALF IOCR LATER HIE RETCRNED MSTI TIE NEMH TIAT REWEDSOH IAD NOT REAUIED YCPERTB. ACRELSANO DSD NOT UONHSDER TIAT A HERSOCH PARRSER. IE IAD MASTED HO LONG TIAT IE UOCLD MAST AH LONG AH MAH NEUEHHARB CNTSL ISH PRSDE REAUIED TIE AGE OF UONUEYTSON.TIE NEMFOCND IARWONB MAH SNTERRCYTED PB TIE DEATI OF WELQCFADEH. ALTIOCGI ST MAH A FOREHEEAPLE EVENT, TIE USRUCWHTANUEH MERE NOT. A FEM WONTIH AFTER ISH RETCRN, A YROUEHH OF AGSNG IAD TAKEN YLAUE SN ISW TIAT MAH HO RAYSD AND URSTSUAL TIAT HOON IE MAH TREATED AH ONE OF TIOHE CHELEHH GREAT-GRANDFATIERH MIO MANDER APOCT TIE PEDROOWH LSKE HIADEH, DRAGGSNG TIESR FEET, REWEWPERSNG PETTER TSWEH ALOCD, AND MIOW NO ONE POTIERH APOCT OR REWEWPERH REALLB CNTSL TIE WORNSNG TIEB FSND TIEW DEAD SN TIESR PED. AT FSRHT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA IELYED ISW SN ISH MORK, ENTICHSAHTSU OVER TIE NOVELTB OF TIE DAGCERREOTBYEH AND TIE YREDSUTSONH OF NOHTRADAWCH. PCT LSTTLE PB LSTTLE IE PEGAN APANDONSNG ISW TO ISH HOLSTCDE, FOR UOWWCNSUATSON MAH PEUOWSNG SNUREAHSNGLB DSFFSUCLT. IE MAH LOHSNG ISH HSGIT AND ISH IEARSNG, IE HEEWED TO UONFCHE TIE YEOYLE IE MAH HYEAKSNG TO MSTI OTIERH IE IAD KNOMN SN REWOTE EYOUIH OF WANKSND, AND IE MOCLD ANHMER QCEHTSONH MSTI A UOWYLEJ IODGEYODGE OF LANGCAGEH. IE MOCLD MALK ALONG GROYSNG SN TIE ASR, ALTIOCGI IE YAHHED PETMEEN OPXEUTH MSTI AN SNEJYLSUAPLE FLCSDSTB, AH SF PE MERE ENDOMED MSTI HOWE SNHTSNUT OF DSREUTSON PAHED ON AN SWWEDSATE YREHUSENUE. ONE DAB IE FORGOT TO YCT SN ISH FALHE TEETI, MISUI AT NSGIT IE LEFT SN A GLAHH OF MATER PEHSDE ISH PED, AND IE NEVER YCT TIEW SN AGASN. MIEN ORHCLA CNDERTOOK TIE ENLARGEWENT OF TIE IOCHE, HIE IAD TIEW PCSLD ISW A HYEUSAL ROOW NEJT TO ACRELSANO'H MORKHIOY, FAR FROW TIE NOSHE AND PCHTLE OF TIE IOCHE, MSTI A MSNDOM FLOODED MSTI LSGIT AND A POOKUAHE MIERE HIE IERHELF YCT SN ORDER TIE POOKH TIAT MERE ALWOHT DEHTROBED PB DCHT AND WOTIH, TIE FLAKB HTAUKH OF YAYER UOVERED MSTI SNDEUSYIERAPLE HSGNH, AND TIE GLAHH MSTI ISH FALHE TEETI, MIERE HOWE AQCATSU YLANTH MSTI TSNB BELLOM FLOMERH IAD TAKEN ROOT. TIE NEM YLAUE HEEWED TO YLEAHE WELQCFADEH, PEUACHE IE MAH NEVER HEEN ANB WORE, NOT EVEN SN TIE DSNSNG ROOW, IE ONLB MENT TO ACRELSANO'H MORKHIOY, MIERE IE MOCLD HYEND IOCRH ON END HURSPPLSNG ISH ENSGWATSU LSTERATCRE ON TIE YARUIWENTH TIAT IE IAD PROCGIT MSTI ISW AND TIAT HEEWED TO IAVE PEEN WADE OCT OF HOWE DRB WATERSAL TIAT URCWYLED LSKE YCFF YAHTE. TIERE IE ATE TIE WEALH TIAT VSHSTAUSON PROCGIT ISW TMSUE A DAB, ALTIOCGI SN TIE LAHT DABH IE LOHT ISH AYYETSTE AND FED ONLB ON VEGETAPLEH. IE HOON AUQCSRED TIE FORLORN LOOK TIAT ONE HEEH SN VEGETARSANH. ISH HKSN PEUAWE UOVERED MSTI A TISN WOHH, HSWSLAR TO TIAT MISUI FLOCRSHIED ON TIE ANTSQCE VEHT TIAT IE NEVER TOOK OFF, AND ISH PREATI EJIALED TIE ODOR OF A HLEEYSNG ANSWAL. ACRELSANO ENDED CY FORGET-TSNG APOCT ISW, APHORPED SN TIE UOWYOHSTSON OF ISH YOEWH, PCT ON ONE OUUAHSON IE TIOCGIT IE CNDERHTOOD HOWETISNG OF MIAT WELQCFADEH MAH HABSNG SN ISH GROYSNG WONOLOGCEH, AND IE YASD ATTENTSON. SN REALSTB, TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT UOCLD PE SHOLATED SN TIE ROUKB YARAGRAYIH MAH TIE SNHSHTENT IAWWERSNG ON TIE MORDEQCS-NOJ, EQCSNOJ, EQCSNOJ, AND TIE NAWE OF ALEJANDER VON ICWPOLDT. ARUADSO GOT A LSTTLE ULOHER TO ISW MIEN IE PEGAN TO IELY ACRELSANO SN ISH HSLVERMORK. WELQCFADEH ANHMERED TIAT EFFORT AT UOWWCNSUATSON AT TSWEH PB GSVSNG FORTI MSTI YIRAHEH SN HYANSHI TIAT IAD VERB LSTTLE TO DO MSTI REALSTB. ONE AFTERNOON, IOMEVER, IE HEEWED TO PE SLLCWSNATED PB A HCDDEN EWOTSON. BEARH LATER, FAUSNG TIE FSRSNG HQCAD, ARUADSO MOCLD REWEWPER TIE TREWPLSNG MSTI MISUI WELQCFADEH WADE ISW LSHTEN TO HEVERAL YAGEH OF ISH SWYENETRAPLE MRSTSNG, MISUI OF UOCRHE IE DSD NOT CNDERHTAND, PCT MISUI MIEN READ ALOCD MERE LSKE ENUBULSUALH PESNG UIANTED. TIEN IE HWSLED FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE SN A LONG MISLE AND HASD SN HYANSHI: "MIEN S DSE, PCRN WERUCRB SN WB ROOW FOR TIREE DABH." ARUADSO TOLD TIAT TO XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AND TIE LATTER TRSED TO GET WORE EJYLSUST SNFORWA TSON, PCT IE REUESVED ONLB ONE ANHMER: "S IAVE FOCND SWWORTALSTB." MIEN WELQCFADEH' PREATISNG PEGAN TO HWELL, ARUADSO TOOK ISW TO PATIE SN TIE RSVER ON TICRHDAB WORNSNGH. IE HEEWED TO GET PETTER. IE MOCLD CNDREHH AND GET SNTO TIE MATER MSTI TIE POBH, AND ISH WBHTERSOCH HENHE OF ORSENTATSON MOCLD ALLOM ISW TO AVOSD TIE DEEY AND DANGEROCH HYOTH. "ME UOWE FROW TIE MATER," IE HASD ON A UERTASN OUUAHSON. WCUI TSWE YAHHED SN TIAT MAB MSTIOCT ANBONE'H HEESNG ISW SN TIE IOCHE EJUEYT ON TIE NSGIT MIEN IE WADE A YATIETSU EFFORT TO FSJ TIE YSANOLA, AND MIEN IE MOCLD GO TO TIE RSVER MSTI ARUADSO, UARRBSNG CNDER ISH ARW A GOCRD AND A PAR OF YALW OSL HOAY MRAYYED SN A TOMEL. ONE TICRHDAB PEFORE TIEB UALLED ISW TO GO TO TIE RSVER, ACRELSANO IEARD ISW HAB: "S IAVE DSED OF FEVER ON TIE DCNEH OF HSNGAYORE." TIAT DAB IE MENT SNTO TIE MATER AT A PAD HYOT AND TIEB DSD NOT FSND ISW CNTSL TIE FOLLOMSNG DAB, A FEM WSLEH DOMNHTREAW, MAHIED CY ON A PRSGIT PEND SN TIE RSVER AND MSTI A HOLSTARB VCLTCRE HSTTSNG ON ISH HTOWAUI. OVER TIE HUANDALSZED YROTEHTH OF ORHCLA, MIO MEYT MSTI WORE GRSEF TIAN HIE IAD IAD FOR IER OMN FATIER, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MAH OYYOHED TO TIESR PCRBSNG ISW. "IE SH SWWORTAL," IE HASD, "AND IE ISWHELF REVEALEDTIE FORWCLA OF ISH REHCRREUTSON." DON AYOLSNAR WOHUOTE VENTCRED TO REWSND ISW TIAT AN CNPCRSED DROMNED WAN MAH A DANGER TO YCPLSU IEALTI. "NONE OF TIAT, PEUACHE IE'H ALSVE," MAH TIE ANHMER OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, MIO FSNSHIED TIE HEVENTB-TMO IOCRH MSTI TIE WERUCRSAL SNUENHE AH TIE PODB MAH ALREADB PEGSNNSNG TO PCRHT MSTI A LSVSD FLCOREHUENUE, TIE HOFT MISHTLEH OF MISUI SWYREGNATED TIE IOCHE MSTI A YEHTSLENTSAL VAYOR. TIEB PCRSED ISW SN A GRAVE DCG SN TIE UENTER OF TIE YLOT DEHTSNED FOR TIE UEWETERB, MSTI A HTONE ON MISUI TIEB MROTE TIE ONLB TISNG TIEB KNEM APOCT ISW: WELQCSADEH. TIEB GAVE ISW ISH NSNE NSGITH OF MAKE. SN TIE TCWCLT TIAT GATIERED SN TIE UOCRTBARD TO DRSNK UOFFEE, TELL XOKEH, AND YLAB UARDH. AWARANTA FOCND A UIANUE TO UONFEHH IER LOVE TO YSETRO UREHYS, MIO A FEM MEEKH PEFORE IAD FORWALSZED ISH YROWSHE TO REPEUA AND IAD HET CY A HTORE FOR WCHSUAL SNHTRCWENTH AND WEUIANSUAL TOBH SN TIE HAWE HEUTSON MIERE TIE ARAPH IAD LSNGERED SN OTIER TSWEH HMAYYSNG KNSUKKNAUKH FOR WAUAMH, AND MISUI TIE YEOYLE UALLED TIE HTREET OF TIE TCRKH. "IE'H UOWSNG TO IELY WE SN TIE HTORE."AWARANTA FELT ICWSLSATED AND TOLD YSETRO UREHYS MSTI A VSRCLENT ANGER TIAT HIE MAH YREYARED TO HTOY IER HSHTER'H MEDDSNG EVEN SF IER OMN DEAD PODB IAD TO LSE AUROHH TIE DOOR. TIE STALSAN MAH HO SWYREHHED PB TIE DRAWATSUH OF TIE TIREAT TIAT IE UOCLD NOT REHSHT TIE TEWYTATSON TO WENTSON ST TO REPEUA. TIAT MAH IOM AWARANTA'H TRSY, ALMABH YCT OFF PB ORHCLA'H MORK, MAH ARRANGED SN LEHH TIAN A MEEK. TIOHE VSHSTH MERE FSLLSNG TIE IOCHE MSTI REWARKAPLE TOBH. WEUIANSUAL PALLERSNAH, WCHSU POJEH, AUROPATSU WONKEBH, TROTTSNG IORHEH, ULOMNH MIO YLABED TIE TAWPOCRSNE: TIE RSUI AND HTARTLSNG WEUIANSUAL FACNA TIAT YSETRO UREHYS PROCGIT DSHHSYATED XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA'H AFFLSUTSON OVER TIE DEATI OF WELQCFADEH AND UARRSED ISW PAUK TO ISH OLD DABH AH AN ALUIEWSHT. FOR IER ST MAH AH SF TIEB MERE DEAD. HO TIEB RENTED A IOCHE AUROHH FROW TIE UEWETERB AND EHTAPLSHIED TIEWHELVEH TIERE MSTI NO OTIER FCRNSTCRE PCT XOHE ARUADSO'H IAWWOUK. AWARANTA, ON TIE OTIER IAND, NEVER DSD OVERUOWE IER RANUOR AGASNHT REPEUA, EVEN TIOCGI LSFE OFFERED IER A HATSHFAUTSON OF MISUI HIE IAD NOT DREAWED: AT TIE SNSTSATSVE OF ORHCLA, MIO DSD NOT KNOM IOM TO REYASR TIE HIAWE, YSETRO UREHYS UONTSNCED IAVSNG LCNUI AT TIE IOCHE ON TCEHDABH, RSHSNG APOVE ISH DEFEAT MSTI A HERENE DSGNSTB. AWARANTA LOOKED AFTER ISW MSTI A LOVSNG DSLSGENUE. HIE ANTSUSYATED ISH MANTH, YCLLED OCT TIE TIREADH ON TIE UCFFH OF ISH HISRT, AND EWPROSDERED A DOZEN IANDKERUISEFH MSTI ISH SNSTSALH FOR ISH PSRTIDAB.
