ARUADSO GRAPPED IER PB TIE MRSHT AND TRSED TO YCLL IER SNTO TIE IAWWOUK. "S UAN'T, S UAN'T," YSLAR TERNERA HASD SN IORROR. "BOC UAN'T SWAGSNE IOM WCUI S MOCLD LSKE TO WAKE BOC IAYYB, PCT AH GOD SH WB MSTNEHH S UAN'T." ARUADSO TOOK IER PB TIE MASHT MSTI ISH TREWENDOCH IEREDSTARB HTRENGTI AND IE FELT TIE MORLD DSHAYYEAR MSTI TIE UONTAUT OF IER HKSN. "DON'T YLAB TIE HASNT," IE HASD. "AFTER ALL, EVERBPODB KNOMH TIAT BOC'RE A MIORE." YSLAR OVERUAWE TIE DSHGCHT TIAT IER WSHERAPLE FATE SNHYSRED SN IER."TIE UISLDREN MSLL FSND OCT," HIE WCRWCRED. "ST MSLL PE PETTER SF BOC LEAVE TIE PAR OFF TIE DOOR TONSGIT." ARUADSO MASTED FOR IER TIAT NSGIT TREWPLSNG MSTI FEVER SN ISH IAWWOUK. IE MASTED MSTIOCT HLEEYSNG, LSHTENSNG TO TIE AROCHED URSUKETH SN TIE ENDLEHH IOCRH OF EARLB WORNSNG AND TIE SWYLAUAPLE TELLSNG OF TSWE PB TIE UCRLEMH, WORE AND WORE UONVSNUED TIAT IE IAD PEEN DEUESVED. HCDDENLB, MIEN ANJSETB IAD PROKEN DOMN SNTO RAGE, TIE DOOR OYENED. A FEM WONTIH LATER, FAUSNG TIE FSRSNG HQCAD, ARUADSO MOCLD RELSVE TIE MANDERSNG HTEYH SN TIE ULAHHROOW, TIE HTCWPLSNG AGASNHT PENUIEH, AND FSNALLB TIE PCLK OF A PODB SN TIE HIADOMH OF TIE ROOW AND TIE PREATISNG OF ASR TIAT MAH YCWYED PB A IEART TIAT MAH NOT ISH. IE HTRETUIED OCT ISH IAND AND FOCND ANOTIER IAND MSTI TMO RSNGH ON TIE HAWE FSNGER APOCT TO GO AHTRAB SN TIE DARKNEHH. IE FELT TIE HTRCUTCRE OF TIE VESNH, TIE YCLHE OF STH WSHFORTCNE, AND FELT TIE DAWY YALW MSTI A LSFELSNE UCT OFF AT TIE PAHE OF TIE TICWP PB TIE ULAMH OF DEATI. TIEN IE REALSZED TIAT TISH MAH NOT TIE MOWAN IE MAH MASTSNG FOR, PEUACHE HIE DSD NOT HWELL OF HWOKE PCT OF FLOMER LOTSON, AND HIE IAD SNFLATED, PLSND PREAHTH MSTI NSYYLEH LSKE. A WAN'H, A HEJ AH HTONB AND ROCND AH A NCT, AND TIE UIAOTSU TENDERNEHH OF EJUSTED SNEJYERSENUE. HIE MAH A VSRGSN AND HIE IAD TIE CNLSKELB NAWE OF HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD. YSLAR TERNERA IAD YASD IER FSFTB YEHOH, IALF OF IER LSFE HAVSNGH, TO DO MIAT HIE MAH DOSNG. ARUADSO, IAD HEEN IER WANB TSWEH MORKSNG SN IER YARENTH' HWALL FOOD HTORE PCT IE IAD NEVER TAKEN A GOOD LOOK AT IER PEUACHE HIE IAD TIAT RARE VSRTCE OF NEVER EJSHTSNG UOWYLETELB EJUEYT AT TIE OYYORTCNE WOWENT. PCT FROW TIAT DAB ON IE ICDDLED LSKE A UAT SN TIE MARWTI OF IER ARWYST HIE MOCLD GO TO TIE HUIOOL AT HSEHTA TSWE MSTI TIE UONHENT OF IER YARENTH, TO MIOW YSLAR TERNERA ISD YASD TIE OTIER IALF OF IER HAVSNGH. LATER ON, MIEN TIE GOVERNWENT TROOYH DSHLODGED TIEW FROW TIE YLAUE MIERE TIEB IAD WADE LOVE, TIEB DSD ST AWONG TIE UANH OF LARD AND HAUKH OF UORN SN TIE PAUK OF TIE HTORE. APOCT TIE TSWE TIAT ARUADSO MAH NAWED USVSL AND WSLSTARB LEADER TIEB IAD A DACGITER. TIE ONLB RELATSVEH MIO KNEM APOCT ST MERE XOHE ARUADSO AND REPEUA, MSTI MIOW ARUADSO WASNTASNED ULOHE RELATSONH AT TIAT TSWE, PAHED NOT HO WCUI ON KSNHISY AH ON UOWYLSUSTB. XOHE ARUADSO IAD YCT ISH NEUK SNTO TIE WARSTAL BOKE. REPEUA'H FSRW UIARAUTER, TIE VORAUSTB OF IER HTOWAUI, IER TENAUSOCH AWPSTSON AP-HORPED TIE TREWENDOCH ENERGB OF IER ICHPAND, MIO IAD PEEN UIANGED FROW A LAZB, MOWAN-UIAHSNG WAN SNTO AN ENORWOCH MORK ANSWAL. TIEB KEYT A ULEAN AND NEAT IOCHE. REPEUA MOCLD OYEN ST MSDE AT DAMN AND TIE MSND FROW TIE GRAVEBARD MOCLD UOWE SN TIROCGI TIE MSNDOMH AND GO OCT TIROCGI TIE DOORH TO TIE BARD AND LEAVE TIE MISTEMAHIED MALLH AND FCRNSTCRE TANNED PB TIE HALTYETER OF TIE DEAD. IER ICNGER FOR EARTI, TIE ULOU-ULOU OF IER YARENTH' PONEH, TIE SWYATSENUE OF IER PLOOD AH ST FAUED YSETRO UREHYS'H YAHHSVSTB MERE RELEGATED TO TIE ATTSU OF IER WEWORB. ALL DAB LONG HIE MOCLD EWPROSDER PEHSDE TIE MSNDOM, MSTIDRAMN FROW TIE CNEAHSNEHH OF TIE MAR, CNTSL TIE UERAWSU YOTH MOCLD PEGSN TO VSPRATE SN TIE UCYPOARD AND HIE MOCLD GET CY TO MARW TIE WEAL, WCUI PEFORE TIE AYYEARANUE, FSRHT, OF TIE WANGB IOCNDH, AND TIEN OF TIE UOLOHHCH SN LEGGSNGH AND HYCRH MSTI A DOCPLE-PARRELED HIOTGCN, MIO HOWETSWEH UARRSED A DEER ON ISH HIOCLDER AND ALWOHT ALMABH A HTRSNG OF RAPPSTH OR MSLD DCUKH. ONE AFTERNOON, AT TIE PEGSNNSNG OF ISH RCLE, ARUADSO YASD TIEW A HCRYRSHE VSHST. TIEB IAD NOT HEEN ISW HSNUE TIEB IAD LEFT TIE IOCHE, PCT IE HEEWED HO FRSENDLB AND FAWSLSAR TIAT TIEB SNVSTED ISW TO HIARE TIE HTEM. ONLB MIEN TIEB MERE IAVSNG UOFFEE DSD ARUADSO REVEAL TIE WOTSVE PEISND ISH VSHST: IE IAD REUESVED A UOWYLASNT AGASNHT XOHE ARUADSO. ST MAH HASD TIAT IE IAD PEGCN PB YLOMSNG ISH OMN BARD AND IAD GONE HTRASGIT AIEAD SNTO NESGIPORSNG LANDH, KNOUKSNG DOMN FENUEH AND PCSLDSNGH MSTI ISH OJEN CNTSL IE TOOK FORUSPLE YOHHEHHSON OF TIE PEHT YLOTH OF LAND AROCND. ON TIE YEAHANTH MIOW IE IAD NOT DEHYOSLED PEUACHE IE MAH NOT SNTEREHTED SN TIESR LANDH, IE LEVSED A UONTRSPCTSON MISUI IE UOLLEUTED EVERB HATCRDAB MSTI ISH ICNTSNG DOGH AND ISH DOCPLE-PARRELED HIOTGCN.IE DSD NOT DENB ST. IE PAHED ISH RSGIT ON TIE FAUT TIAT TIE CHCRYED LANDH IAD PEEN DSHTRSPCTED PB XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA AT TIE TSWE OF TIE FOCNDSNG, AND IE TIOCGIT ST YOHHSPLE TO YROVE TIAT ISH FATIER IAD PEEN URAZB EVER HSNUE TIAT TSWE, FOR IE IAD DSHYOHED OF A YATRSWONB TIAT REALLB PELONGED TO TIE FAWSLB. ST MAH AN CNNEUEHHARB ALLEGATSON, PEUACHE ARUADSO IAD NOT UOWE TO DO XCHTSUE. IE HSWYLB OFFERED TO HET CY A REGSHTRB OFFSUE HO TIAT XOHE ARUADSO UOCLD LEGALSZE ISH TSTLE TO TIE CHCRYED LAND, CNDER TIE UONDSTSON TIAT IE DELEGATE TO TIE LOUAL GOVERNWENT TIE RSGIT TO UOLLEUT TIE UONTRSPC-TSONH. TIEB WADE AN AGREEWENT. BEARH LATER, MIEN UOLO-NEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA EJAWSNED TIE TSTLEH TO YROYERTB, IE FOCND REGSHTERED SN ISH PROTIER'H NAWE ALL OF TIE LAND PETMEEN TIE ISLL MIERE ISH BARD MAH ON CY TO TIE IORSZON, SNULCDSNG TIE UEWETERB, AND DSHUOVERED TIAT DCRSNG TIE ELEVEN WONTIH OF ISH RCLE, ARUADSO IAD UOLLEUTED NOT ONLB TIE WONEB OF TIE UONTRSPCTSONH, PCT IAD ALHO UOLLEUTED FEEH FROW YEOYLE FOR TIE RSGIT TO PCRB TIESR DEAD SN XOHE ARUADSO'H LAND.ST TOOK ORHCLA HEVERAL WONTIH TO FSND OCT MIAT MAH ALREADB YCPLSU KNOMLEDGE PEUACHE YEOYLE ISD ST FROW IER HO AH NOT TO SNUREAHE IER HCFFERSNG. AT FSRHT HIE HCHYEUTED ST. "ARUADSO SH PCSLDSNG A IOCHE," HIE UONFSDED MSTI FESGNED YRSDE TO IER ICHPAND AH HIE TRSED TO YCT A HYOONFCL OF UALAPAHI HBRCY SNTO ISH WOCTI. NEVERTIELEHH, HIE SNVOLCNTARSLB HSGIED AND HASD, "S DON'T KNOM MIB, PCT ALL TISH IAH A PAD HWELL TO WE." LATER ON, MIEN HIE FOCND OCT TIAT ARUADSO IAD NOT ONLB PCSLT A IOCHE PCT IAD ORDERED HOWE VSENNEHE FCRNSTCRE, HIE UONFSRWED IER HCHYSUSON TIAT IE MAH CHSNG YCPLSU FCNDH. "BOC'RE TIE HIAWE OF OCR FAWSLB NAWE," HIE HIOCTED AT ISW ONE HCNDAB AFTER WAHH MIEN HIE HAM ISW SN ISH NEM IOCHE YLABSNG UARDH MSTI ISH OFFSUERH. ARUADSO YASD NO ATTENTSON TO IER. ONLB TIEN DSD ORHCLA KNOM TIAT IE IAD A HSJ-WONTI-OLD DACGITER AND TIAT HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD, MSTI MIOW IE MAH LSVSNG OCTHSDE OF WARRSAGE, MAH YREGNANT AGASN. HIE DEUSDED TO MRSTE TO UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA, MIEREVER IE MAH, TO PRSNG ISW CY TO DATE ON TIE HSTCATSON. PCT TIE FAHT-WOVSNG EVENTH OF TIOHE DABH NOT ONLB YREVENTED IER YLANH FROW PESNG UARRSED OCT, TIEB WADE IER REGRET IAVSNG UONUESVED TIEW. TIE MAR, MISUI CNTSL TIEN IAD PEEN ONLB A MORD TO DEHSGNATE A VAGCE AND REWOTE USRUCWHTANUE, PEUAWE A UONURETE AND DRAWATSU REALSTB. AROCND TIE END OF FEPRCARB AN OLD MOWAN MSTI AN AHIEN LOOK ARRSVED SN WAUON-DO RSDSNG A DONKEB LOADED DOMN MSTI PROOWH. HIE HEEWED HO SNOFFENHSVE TIAT TIE HENTRSEH LET IER YAHH MSTIOCT ANB QCEHTSONH AH ANOTIER VENDOR, ONE OF TIE WANB MIO OFTEN ARRSVED FROW TIE TOMNH SN TIE HMAWY. HIE MENT DSREUTLB TO TIE PARRAUKH. ARUADSO REUESVED IER SN TIE YLAUE MIERE TIE ULAHHROOW CHED TO PE AND MISUI AT TIAT TSWE IAD PEEN TRANHFORWED SNTO A KSND OF REARGCARD ENUAWYWENT, MSTI ROSLED IAWWOUKH IANGSNG ON IOOKH AND WATH YSLED CY SN TIE UORNERH, AND RSFLEH AND UARPSNEH AND EVEN ICNTSNG HIOTGCNH HUATTERED ON TIE FLOOR. TIE OLD MOWAN HTSFFENED SNTO A WSLSTARB HALCTE PEFORE SDENTSFBSNG IERHELF: "S AW UOLONEL GREGORSO HTEVENHON."IE PROCGIT PAD NEMH. TIE LAHT UENTERH OF LSPERAL REHSHTANUE, AUUORDSNG TO MIAT IE HASD, MERE PESNG MSYED OCT. UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA, MIOW IE IAD LEFT FSGITSNG SN RETREAT NEAR RSOIAUIA, IAD GSVEN ISW A WEHHAGE FOR ARUADSO. IE HIOCLD HCRRENDER TIE TOMN MSTIOCT REHSHTANUE ON TIE UONDSTSON TIAT TIE LSVEH AND YROYERTB OF LSPERALH MOCLD PE REHYEUTED. ARUADSO EJAWSNED TIAT HTRANGE WEHHENGER MIO UOCLD IAVE PEEN A FCGSTSVE GRANDWOTIER MSTI A LOOK OF YSTB. "BOC IAVE PROCGIT HOWETISNG SN MRSTSNG, NATCRALLB," IE HASD. "NATCRALLB," TIE EWSHHARB ANHMERED, "S IAVE PROCGIT NOTISNG OF TIE HORT. ST'H EAHB TO CNDERHTAND TIAT CNDER TIE YREHENT USRUCWHTANUEH A YERHON UAN'T UARRB ANBTISNG TIAT MOCLD UOWYROWSHE ISW."AH IE MAH HYEAKSNG IE REAUIED SNTO ISH PODSUE AND TOOK OCT A HWALL GOLD FSHI. "S TISNK TIAT TISH MSLL PE HCFFSUSENT," IE HASD. ARUADSO UOCLD HEE TIAT SNDEED ST MAH ONE OF TIE LSTTLE FSHIEH WADE PB UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA. PCT ANBONE UOCLD IAVE POCGIT ST PEFORE TIE MAR OR HTOLEN ST, AND ST IAD NO WERST AH A HAFE-UONDCUT YAHH. TIE WEHHENGER EVEN MENT TO TIE EJTREWE OF VSOLATSNG A WSLSTARB HEURET HO TIAT TIEB MOCLD PELSEVE ISH SDENTSTB. IE REVEALED TIAT IE MAH ON A WSHHSON TO UCRAGAO, MIERE IE IOYED TO REURCST EJSLEH FROW ALL OVER TIE UARSPPEAN AND AUQCSRE ARWH AND HCYYLSEH HCFFSUSENT TO ATTEWYT A LANDSNG AT TIE END OF TIE BEAR. MSTI FASTI SN TIAT YLAN, UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA MAH NOT SN FAVOR OF ANB CHELEHH HAURSFSUEH AT TIAT TSWE. PCT ARUADSO MAH SNFLEJSPLE. IE IAD TIE YRSHONER YCT SNTO TIE HTOUKH CNTSL IE UOCLD YROVE ISH SDENTSTB AND IE REHOLVED TO DEFEND TIE TOMN TO TIE DEATI.IE DSD NOT IAVE LONG TO MAST. TIE NEMH OF TIE LSPERAL DEFEAT MAH WORE AND WORE UONURETE. TOMARD TIE END OF WARUI, PEFORE A DAMN OF YREWATCRE RASN, TIE TENHE UALW OF TIE YREVSOCH MEEKH MAH APRCYTLB PROKEN PB TIE DEHYERATE HOCNDH OF A UORNET AND A UANNON HIOT TIAT KNOUKED DOMN TIE HTEEYLE OF TIE UICRUI. AUTCALLB, ARUADSO'H DEUSHSON TO REHSHT MAH WADNEHH. IE IAD ONLB FSFTB YOORLB ARWED WEN MSTI A RATSON OF TMENTB UARTRSDGEH AYSEUE. PCT AWONG TIEW, ISH FORWER YCYSLH, EJUSTED PB TIE ISGI-HOCNDSNG YROULAWATSONH, TIE DETER-WSNATSON RESGNED TO HAURSFSUE TIESR HKSNH FOR A LOHT UACHE. SN TIE WSDHT OF TIE TRAWYSNG OF POOTH, UONTRADSUTORB UOWWANDH, UANNON HIOTH TIAT WADE TIE EARTI TREWPLE, MSLD HIOOTSNG, AND TIE HENHELEHH HOCND OF UORNETH, TIE HCYYOHED UOLONEL HTEVENHON WANAGED TO HYEAK TO ARUA-DSO. "DON'T LET WE CNDERGO TIE SNDSGNSTB OF DBSNG SN TIE HTOUKH SN TIEHE MOWEN'H ULOTIEH," IE HASD TO ISW. "SF S IAVE TO DSE, LET WE DSE FSGITSNG." IE HCUUEEDED SN UONVSNUSNG ISW. ARUADSO ORDERED TIEW TO GSVE ISW A MEAYON AND TMENTB UARTRSDGEH, AND IE LEFT ISW MSTI FSVE WEN TO DEFEND IEADQCARTERH MISLE IE MENT OFF MSTI ISH HTAFF TO IEAD CY TIE REHSHTANUE. IE DSD NOT GET TO TIE ROAD TO TIE HMAWY. TIE PARRSUADEH IAD PEEN PROKEN AND TIE DEFENDERH MERE OYENLB FSGITSNG SN TIE HTREETH, FSRHT CNTSL TIEB CHED CY TIESR RATSON OF RSFLE PCLLETH, TIEN MSTI YSHTOLH AGASNHT RSFLEH, AND FSNALLB IAND TO IAND. MSTI TIE SWWSNENUE OF DEFEAT, HOWE MOWEN MENT SNTO TIE HTREET ARWED MSTI HTSUKH AND KSTUIEN KNSVEH. SN TIAT UONFCHSON ARUADSO FOCND AWARANTA, MIO MAH LOOKSNG FOR ISW LSKE A WADMOWAN, SN IER NSGITGOMN AND MSTI TMO OLD YSHTOLH TIAT IAD PELONGED TO XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA. IE GAVE ISH RSFLE TO AN OFFSUER MIO IAD PEEN DSHARWED SN TIE FSGIT AND EHUAYED MSTI AWARANTA TIROCGI A NEARPB HTREET TO TAKE IER IOWE. ORHCLA MAH, SN TIE DOORMAB MASTSNG, SNDSFFERENT TO TIE UANNON HIOTH TIAT IAD OYENED CY A IOLE SN TIE FRONT OF TIE IOCHE NEJT DOOR. TIE RASN MAH LETTSNG CY, PCT TIE HTREETH MERE AH HLSYYERB AND AH HWOOTI AH WELTED HOAY, AND ONE IAD TO GCEHH DSHTANUEH SN TIE DARKNEHH. ARUADSO LEFT AWARAN-TA MSTI ORHCLA AND WADE AN ATTEWYT TO FAUE TMO HOLDSERH MIO IAD OYENED CY MSTI IEAVB FSRSNG FROW TIE UORNER. TIE OLD YSHTOLH TIAT IAD PEEN KEYT FOR WANB BEARH SN TIE PCREAC DSD NOT MORK. YROTEUTSNG ARUADSO MSTI IER PODB, ORHCLA TRSED TO DRAG ISW TOMARD TIE IOCHE. "UOWE ALONG SN TIE NAWE OF GOD," HIE HIOCTED AT ISW. "TIERE'H PEEN ENOCGI WADNEHH!" TIE HOLDSERH ASWED AT TIEW."LET GO OF TIAT WAN, WA'AW," ONE OF TIEW HIOCTED, "OR ME MON'T PE REHYONHSPLE!"ARUADSO YCHIED ORHCLA TOMARD TIE IOCHE AND HCRRENDERED. A HIORT TSWE LATER TIE HIOOTSNG HTOYYED AND TIE PELLH PEGAN TO TOLL. TIE REHSHTANUE IAD PEEN MSYED OCT SN LEHH TIAN IALF AN IOCR. NOT A HSNGLE ONE OF ARUADSO'H WEN IAD HCRVSVED TIE ATTAUK, PCT PEFORE DBSNG TIEB IAD KSLLED TIREE ICNDRED HOLDSERH. TIE LAHT HTRONGIOLD MAH TIE PARRAUKH. PEFORE PESNG ATTAUKED, TIE HCYYOHED UOLONEL GREGORSO HTEVENHON IAD FREED TIE YRSHONERH AND ORDERED ISH WEN TO GO OCT AND FSGIT SN TIE HTREET. TIE EJTRAORDSNARB WOPSLSTB AND AUUCRATE ASW MSTI MISUI IE YLAUED ISH TMENTB UARTRSDGEH GAVE TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT TIE PARRAUKH MAH MELL-DEFENDED, AND TIE ATTAUKERH PLEM ST TO YSEUEH MSTI UANNON FSRE. TIE UAYTASN MIO DSREUTED TIE OYERATSON MAH HTARTLED TO FSND TIE RCPPLE DEHERTED AND A HSNGLE DEAD WAN SN ISH CNDERHIORTH MSTI AN EWYTB RSFLE HTSLL ULCTUIED SN AN ARW TIAT IAD PEEN PLOMN UOWYLETELB OFF. "LOOK MIERE TISH FELLOM TCRNED CY," TIE UAYTASN HASD. "ST'H GREGORSO HTEVENHON."AT DAMN, AFTER A HCWWARB UOCRT WARTSAL, ARUADSO MAH HIOT AGASNHT TIE MALL OF TIE UEWETERB. SN TIE LAHT TMO IOCRH OF ISH LSFE IE DSD NOT WANAGE TO CNDERHTAND MIB TIE FEAR TIAT IAD TORWENTED ISW HSNUE UISLDIOOD IAD DSHAYYEARED. SWYAHHSVE. MSTIOCT EVEN MORRBSNG APOCT WAKSNG A HIOM OF ISH REUENT PRAVERB, IE LSHTENED TO TIE SNTERWSNAPLE UIARGEH OF TIE AUUCHATSON. IE TIOCGIT APOCT ORHCLA, MIO AT TIAT IOCR WCHT IAVE PEEN CNDER TIE UIEHTNCT TREE IAVSNG UOFFEE MSTI XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA. IE TIOCGIT APOCT ISH ESGIT-WONTI-OLD DACGITER, MIO HTSLL IAD NO NAWE, AND APOCT TIE UISLD MIO MAH GOSNG TO PE PORN SN ACGCHT. IE TIOCGIT APOCT HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD, MIOW IE IAD LEFT TIE NSGIT PEFORE HALTSNG DOMN A DEER FOR NEJT DAB'H LCNUI, AND IE WSHHED IER IASR YOCRSNG OVER IER HIOCLDERH AND IER EBELAHIEH, MISUI LOOKED AH SF TIEB MERE ARTSFSUSAL. IE TIOCGIT APOCT ISH YEOYLE MSTIOCT HENTSWENTALSTB, MSTI A HTRSUT DOHSNG OF ISH AUUOCNTH MSTI LSFE, PEGSNNSNG TO CNDERHTAND IOM WCUI IE REALLB LOVED TIE YEOYLE IE IATED WOHT. TIE YREHSDENT OF TIE UOCRT-WARTSAL PEGAN ISH FSNAL HYEEUI MIEN ARUADSO REALSZED TIAT TMO IOCRH IAD YAHHED. "EVEN SF TIE YROVEN UIARGEH DSD NOT IAVE WERST ENOCGI," TIE YREHSDENT MAH HABSNG, "TIE SRREHYONHSPLE AND URSWSNAL POLDNEHH MSTI MISUI TIE AUUCHED DROVE ISH HCPORDSNATEH ON TO A CHELEHH DEATI MOCLD PE ENOCGI TO DEHERVE UAYSTAL YCNSHIWENT." SN TIE HIATTERED HUIOOLIOCHE MIERE FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE IE IAD FELT TIE HEUCRSTB OF YOMER, A FEM FEET FROW TIE ROOW MIERE IE IAD UOWE TO KNOM TIE CNUERTASNTB OF LOVE, ARUADSO FOCND TIE FORWALSTB OF DEATI RSDSUCLOCH. DEATI REALLB DSD NOT WATTER TO ISW PCT LSFE DSD, AND TIEREFORE TIE HENHATSON IE FELT MIEN TIEB GAVE TIESR DEUSHSON MAH NOT A FEELSNG OF FEAR PCT OF NOHTALGSA. "OI, GOD DAWN ST!" IE WANAGED TO TISNK. "S FORGOT TO HAB TIAT SF ST MAH A GSRL TIEB HIOCLD NAWE IER REWEDS-OH." TIEN, ALL AUUCWCLATED SN TIE RSY OF A ULAM, IE FELT AGASN ALL TIE TERROR TIAT IAD TORWENTED ISW SN ISH LSFE. TIE UAYTASN GAVE TIE ORDER TO FSRE. HIE SNCRED IER TIAT UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA MOCLD DO HOWETISNG TO YREVENT TIE EJEUCTSON AND YROWSHED TIAT HIE MOCLD TAKE UIARGE OF ATTRAUTSNG GERSNELDO WARQCEZ IERHELF MIEN TIE MAR MAH OVER. MIEN GERSNELDO WARQCEZ RETCRNED TO TIE IOCHE, SNVEHTED MSTI ISH NEM DSGNSTB OF USVSL AND WSLSTARB LEADER, HIE REUESVED ISW AH A HON, TIOCGIT OF DELSGITFCL PSTH OF FLATTERB TO IOLD ISW TIERE, AND YRABED MSTI ALL IER HOCL TIAT IE MOCLD REWEWPER ISH YLAN TO WARRB AWARANTA. IER YLEAH HEEWED TO PE ANHMERED. ON TIE DABH TIAT IE MOCLD IAVE LCNUI AT TIE IOCHE, UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ MOCLD LSNGER ON TIE PEGONSA YORUI YLABSNG UISNEHE UIEUKERH MSTI AWARANTA. ORHCLA MOCLD PRSNG TIEW UOFFEE AND WSLK AND PSHUCSTH AND MOCLD TAKE OVER TIE UISLDREN HO TIAT TIEB MOCLD NOT POTIER TIEW. AWARANTA MAH REALLB WAKSNG AN EFFORT TO KSNDLE SN IER IEART TIE FORGOTTEN AHIEH OF IER BOCTIFCL YAHHSON. MSTI AN ANJSETB TIAT UAWE TO PE SNTOLERAPLE, HIE MASTED FOR TIE LCNUI DABH, TIE AFTERNOONH OF UISNEHE UIEUKERH, AND TSWE FLEM PB SN TIE UOWYANB OF TIE MARRSOR MSTI A NOHTALGSU NAWE MIOHE FSNGERH TREWPLED SWYERUEYTSPLB AH IE WOVED TIE YSEUEH. PCT TIE DAB ON MISUI UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ REYEATED ISH MSHI TO WARRB IER, HIE REXEUTED ISW."S'W NOT GOSNG TO WARRB ANBONE," HIE TOLD ISW, "WCUI LEHH BOC. BOC LOVE ACRELSANO HO WCUI TIAT BOC MANT TO WARRB WE PEUACHE BOC UAN'T WARRB ISW."UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ MAH A YATSENT WAN. "S'LL KEEY ON SNHSHTSNG," IE HASD. "HOONER OR LATER S'LL UONVSNUE BOC." IE KEYT ON VSHSTSNG TIE IOCHE. HICT CY SN IER PEDROOW PSTSNG PAUK IER HEURET TEARH, AWARANTA YCT IER FSNGERH SN IER EARH HO AH NOT TO PEAR TIE VOSUE OF TIE HCSTOR AH IE GAVE ORHCLA TIE LATEHT MAR NEMH, AND SN HYSTE OF TIE FAUT TIAT HIE MAH DBSNG TO HEE ISW HIE IAD TIE HTRENGTI NOT TO GO OCT AND WEET ISW.AT TIAT TSWE UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA TOOK TIE TSWE TO HEND A DETASLED AUUOCNT TO WAUONDO EVERB TMO MEEKH. PCT ONLB ONUE, ALWOHT ESGIT WONTIH AFTER IE IAD LEFT, DSD IE MRSTE TO ORHCLA. A HYEUSAL WEHHENGER PROCGIT A HEALED ENVELOYE TO TIE IOCHE MSTI A HIEET OF YAYER SNHSDE PEARSNG TIE UOLONEL'H DELSUATE IAND:TAKE GOOD UARE OF YAYA PEUACHE IE SH GOSNG TO DSE . ORHCLA PEUAWE ALARWED. "SF ACRELSANO HABH HO ST'H PEUACHE ACRELSANO KNOMH," HIE HASD. AND HIE IAD TIEW IELY IER TAKE XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA TO ISH PEDROOW. NOT ONLB MAH IE AH IEAVB AH EVER, PCT DCRSNG ISH YROLONGED HTAB CNDER TIE UIEHTNCT TREE IE IAD DEVELOYED TIE FAUCLTB OF PESNG APLE TO SNUREAHE ISH MESGIT AT MSLL, TO HCUI A DEGREE TIAT HEVEN WEN MERE CNAPLE TO LSFT ISW AND TIEB IAD TO DRAG ISW TO TIE PED. A HWELL OF TENDER WCHIROOWH, OF MOOD-FLOMER FCNGCH, OF OLD AND UONUENTRATED OCTDOORH SWYREGNATED TIE ASR OF TIE PEDROOW AH ST MAH PREATIED PB TIE UOLOHHAL OLD WAN MEATIER-PEATEN PB TIE HCN AND TIE RASN. TIE NEJT WORNSNG IE MAH NOT SN ISH PED. SN HYSTE OF ISH CNDSWSNSHIED HTRENGTI, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MAH SN NO UONDSTSON TO REHSHT. ST MAH ALL TIE HAWE TO ISW. SF IE MENT PAUK TO TIE UIEHTNCT TREE ST MAH NOT PEUACHE IE MANTED TO PCT PEUACHE OF A IAPST OF ISH PODB. ORHCLA TOOK UARE OF ISW, FED ISW, PROCGIT ISW NEMH OF ACRELSANO. PCT AUTCALLB, TIE ONLB YERHON MSTI MIOW IE MAH APLE TO IAVE UONTAUT FOR A LONG TSWE MAH YRCDENUSO AGCSLAR. MIEN IE MAH ALONE, XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA UONHOLED ISWHELF MSTI TIE DREAW OF TIE SNFSNSTE ROOWH. IE DREAWED TIAT IE MAH GETTSNG OCT OF PED, OYENSNG TIE DOOR AND GOSNG SNTO AN SDENTSUAL ROOW MSTI TIE HAWE PED MSTI A MROCGIT-SRON IEAD, TIE HAWE MSUKER UIASR, AND TIE HAWE HWALL YSUTCRE OF TIE VSRGSN OF IELY ON TIE PAUK MALL. FROW TIAT ROOW IE MOCLD GO SNTO ANOTIER TIAT MAH XCHT TIE HAWE, TIE DOOR OF MISUI MOCLD OYEN SNTO ANOTIER TIAT MAH XCHT TIE HAWE, TIE DOOR OF MISUI MOCLD OYEN SNTO ANOTIER ONE XCHT TIE HAWE, AND TIEN SNTO ANOTIER EJAUTLB ALSKE, AND HO ON TO SNFSNSTB. PCT ONE NSGIT, TMO MEEKH AFTER TIEB TOOK ISW TO ISH PED, YRCDENUSO AGCSLAR TOCUIED ISH HIOCLDER SN AN SNTERWEDSATE ROOW AND IE HTABED TIERE FOREVER, TISNKSNG TIAT ST MAH TIE REAL ROOW. ON TIE FOLLOMSNG WORNSNG ORHCLA MAH PRSNGSNG ISW ISH PREAK-FAHT MIEN HIE HAM A WAN UOWSNG ALONG TIE IALL. IE MORE USVSLSAN ULOTIEH, REYLAUED TIE HOLDSERH MSTI CNARWED YOLSUEWEN, ENFORUED TIE AWNEHTB LAMH, AND IELYED A FEM FAWSLSEH OF LSPERALH MIO IAD PEEN KSLLED SN TIE MAR. FATIER NSUANOR, UONHCWED PB IEYATSU FEVER, MAH REYLAUED PB FATIER UORONEL, MIOW TIEB UALLED "TIE YCY," A VETERAN OF TIE FSRHT FEDERALSHT MAR. PRCNO UREHYS, MIO MAH WARRSED TO AWYARO WOH. UOTE, AND MIOHE HIOY OF TOBH AND WCHSUAL SNHTRCWENTH UONTSNCED TO YROHYER, PCSLT A TIEATER MISUI HYANSHI UOWYANSEH SNULCDED SN TIESR STSNERARSEH. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO AND XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO, TIE MSLLFCL TMSNH OF HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD, MERE TIE FSRHT TO HST SN TIE ULAHHROOW, MSTI TIESR HLATEH, TIESR UIALK, AND TIESR ALCWSNCW XCGH MSTI TIESR NAWEH ON TIEW. REWEDSOH, MIO SNIERSTED IER WOTIER'H YCRE PEACTB, PEGAN TO PE KNOMN AH REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB. SN HYSTE OF TSWE, OF TIE HCYERSWYOHED YERSODH OF WOCRNSNG, AND IER AUUCWCLATED AFFLSUTSONH, ORHCLA REHSHTED GROMSNG OLD. "AH LONG AH GOD GSVEH WE LSFE," HIE MOCLD HAB, "TIERE MSLL ALMABH PE WONEB SN TISH WADIOCHE." TIAT MAH IOM TISNGH MERE MIEN ACRELSANO XOHE DEHERTED TIE FEDERAL TROOYH SN NSUARAGCA, HSGNED ON AH A UREMWAN ON A GERWAN HISY, AND AYYEARED SN TIE KSTUI-EN OF TIE IOCHE, HTCRDB AH A IORHE, AH DARK AND LONG-IASRED AH AN SNDSAN, AND MSTI A HEURET DETERWSNATSON TO WARRB AWARANTA. MIEN AWARANTA, HAM ISW UOWE SN, EVEN TIOCGI IE HASD NOTISNG HIE KNEM SWWEDSATELB MIB IE IAD UOWE PAUK. AT TIE TAPLE TIEB DSD NOT DARE LOOK EAUI OTIER SN TIE FAUE. PCT TMO MEEKH AFTER ISH RETCRN, SN TIE YREHENUE OF ORHCLA, IE HET ISH EBEH ON IERH AND HASD TO IER, "S ALMABH TIOCGIT A LOT APOCT BOC." AWARANTA AVOSDED ISW. HIE GCARDED AGASNHT UIANUE WEETSNGH. EARLB ONE WORNSNG, ALWOHT TMO WONTIH AFTER ISH RETCRN, HIE IEARD ISW UOWE SNTO TIE PEDROOW. HIE FELT ISW HLSY SN CNDER TIE WOHQCSTO NETTSNG AH IE IAD DONE MIEN IE MAH A UISLD, AH IE IADALMABH DONE, AND HIE UOCLD NOT REYREHH IER UOLD HMEAT AND TIE UIATTERSNG OF IER TEETI MIEN HIE REALSZED TIAT IE MAH UOWYLETELB NAKED. "GO AMAB," HIE MISHYERED, HCFFOUATSNG MSTI UCRS-OHSTB. "GO AMAB OR S'LL HUREAW." PCT ACRELSANO XOHE KNEM TIEN MIAT IE IAD TO DO, PEUACHE IE MAH NO LONGER A UISLD PCT A PARRAUKH ANSWAL. EARLB ONE WORNSNG, VANQCSHIED PB TIE CNPEARAPLE YASN OF REYREHHED VSRSLSTB, IEMENT TO UATARSNO'H. IE FOCND A MOWAN MSTI FLAUUSD PREAHTH, AFFEUTSONATE AND UIEAY, MIO UALWED ISH HTOWAUI FOR HOWE TSWE. AUTCALLB, UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA IAD PEEN SN TIE UOCNTRB FOR WORE TIAN A WONTI. IE MAH YREUEDED PB UONFLSUTSNG RCWORH, HCYYOHED TO PE SN TIE WOHT DSHTANT YLAUEH AT TIE HAWE TSWE, AND EVEN GENERAL WONUADA DSD NOT PELSEVE SN ISH RETCRN CNTSL ST MAH OFFSUSALLB AN-NOCNUED TIAT IE IAD HESZED TMO HTATEH ON TIE UOAHT. "UONGRATCLATSONH, DEAR FRSEND," IE TOLD ORHCLA, HIOMSNG IER TIE TELEGRAW. "BOC'LL HOON IAVE ISW IERE." ORHCLA MAH MORRSED TIEN FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE. "AND MIAT MSLL BOC DO?" HIE AHKED. GENERAL WONUADA IAD AHKED ISWHELF TIAT HAWE QCEHTSON WANB TSWEH."TIE HAWE AH IE, WB FRSEND," IE ANHMERED. "S'LL DO WB DCTB." AT DAMN ON TIE FSRHT OF OUTOPER UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA ATTAUKED WAUONDO MSTI A TIOCHAND MELL-ARWED WEN AND TIE GARRSHON REUESVED ORDERH TO REHSHT TO TIE END. AT NOON, MISLE GENERAL WONUADA MAH LCNUISNG MSTI ORHCLA, A REPEL UANNON HIOT TIAT EUIOED SN TIE MIOLE TOMN PLEM TIE FRONT OF TIE WCNSUSYAL TREAHCRB TO DCHT. "TIEB'RE AH MELL ARWED AH ME ARE," GENERAL WON-UADA HSGIED, "PCT PEHSDEH TIAT TIEB'RE FSGITSNG PEUACHE TIEB MANT TO." AT TMO O'ULOUK SN TIE AFTERNOON, MISLE TIE EARTI TREWPLED MSTI TIE ARTSLLERB FSRE FROW POTI HSDEH, IE TOOK LEAVE OF ORHCLA MSTI TIE UERTASNTB TIAT IE MAH FSGITSNG A LOHSNG PATTLE. "S YRAB TO GOD TIAT BOC MON'T IAVE ACRELSANO SN TIE IOCHE TONSGIT," IE HASD. "SF ST DOEH IAYYEN TIAT MAB, GSVE ISW AN EWPRAUE FOR WE, PEUACHE S DON'T EJYEUT EVER TO HEE ISW AGASN."TIAT NSGIT IE MAH UAYTCRED MIEN IE TRSED TO EHUAYE FROW WAUONDO, AFTER MRSTSNG A LONG LETTER TO UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA SN MISUI IE REWSNDED ISW OF TIESR UOWWON ASW TO ICWANSZE TIE MAR AND IE MSHIED ISW A FSNAL VSUTORB OVER TIE UORRCYTSON OF TIE WSLSTARSHTH AND TIE AWPSTSONH OF TIE YOLSTSUSANH SN POTI YARTSEH. ON TIE FOLLOMSNG DAB UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA IAD LCNUI MSTI ISW SN ORHCLA'H IOCHE, MIERE IE MAH PESNG IELD CNTSL A REVOLCTSONARB UOCRT-WARTSAL DEUSDED ISH FATE. ST MAH A FRSENDLB GATIERSNG. PCT MISLE TIE ADVERHARSEH FORGOT TIE MAR TO REWEWPER TISNGH OF TIE YAHT, ORHCLA IAD TIE GLOOWB FEELSNG TIAT IER HON MAH AN SNTRCDER. HIE IAD FELT ST EVER HSNUE HIE HAM ISW UOWE SN YROTEUTED PB A NOSHB WSLSTARB RETSNCE, MISUI TCRNED TIE PEDROOWH SNHSDE OCT CNTSL TIEB MERE UONVSNUED TIERE MAH NO DANGER. UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA NOT ONLB AUUEYTED ST PCT IE GAVE HTRSUT ORDERH TIAT NO ONE HIOCLD UOWE ULOHER TIAN TEN FEET, NOT EVEN ORHCLA, MISLE TIE WEW-PERH OF ISH EHUORT FSNSHIED YLAUSNG GCARDH APOCT TIE IOCHE. IE MAH MEARSNG AN ORDSNARB DENSW CNSFORW MSTI NO SNHSGNSA OF ANB KSND AND ISGI POOTH MSTI HYCRH TIAT MERE UAKED MSTI WCD AND DRSED PLOOD. ON ISH MASHT IE MORE A IOLHTER MSTI TIE FLAY OYEN AND ISH IAND, MISUI MAH ALMABH ON TIE PCTT OF TIE YSHTOL, REVEALED TIE HAWE MATUIFCL AND REHOLCTE TENHSON AH ISH LOOK. ISH IEAD, MSTI DEEY REUEHHSONH SN TIE IASRLSNE NOM, HEEWED TO IAVE PEEN PAKED SN A HLOM OVEN. ISH FAUE, TANNED PB TIE HALT OF TIE UARSPPEAN, IAD AUQCSRED A WETALLSU IARDNEHH. IE MAH YREHERVED AGASNHT SWWSNENT OLD AGE PB A VSTALSTB TIAT IAD HOWETISNG TO DO MSTI TIE UOLDNEHH OF ISH SNHSDEH. IE MAH TALLER TIAN MIEN IE IAD LEFT, YALER AND PONSER, AND IE HIOMED TIE FSRHT HBWYTOWH OF REHSHTANUE TO NOHTALGSA. "GOOD LORD," ORHCLA HASD TO IERHELF. "NOM IE LOOKH LSKE A WAN UAYAPLE OF ANBTISNG." IE MAH. TIE AZTEU HIAML TIAT IE PROCGIT AWARANTA, TIE REWEWPRANUEH IE HYOKE OF AT LCNUI, TIE FCNNB HTORSEH IER TOLD MERE HSWYLE LEFTOVERH FROW ISH ICWOR OF A DSFFERENT TSWE. AH HOON AH TIE ORDER TO PCRB TIE DEAD SN A UOWWON GRAVE MAH UARRSED OCT, IE AHHSGNED UOLONEL ROQCE UARNSUERO TIE WSNSON OF HETTSNG CY UOCRTH-WARTSAL AND IE MENT AIEAD MSTI TIE EJIACHTSNG TAHK OF SWYOHSNG RADSUAL REFORWH MISUI MOCLD NOT LEAVE A HTONE OF TIE REEHTAPLSHIED UONHERVATSVE REGSWE SN YLAUE. "ME IAVE TO GET AIEAD OF TIE YOLSTSUSANH SN TIE YARTB," IE HASD TO ISH ASDEH. "MIEN TIEB OYEN TIESR EBEH TO REALSTB TIEB'LL FSND AUUOWYLSHIED FAUTH." ST MAH TIEN TIAT IE DEUSDED TO REVSEM TIE TSTLEH TO LAND TIAT MENT PAUK A ICNDRED BEARH AND IE DSHUOVERED TIE LEGALSZED OCTRAGEH OF ISH PROTIER, XOHE ARUADSO. IE ANNCLLED TIE REGSHTRA-TSONH MSTI A HTROKE OF TIE YEN. AH A LAHT GEHTCRE OF UOCRTEHB, IE LEFT ISH AFFASRH FOR AN IOCR AND VSHSTED REPEUA TO PRSNG IER CY TO DATE ON MIAT IE MAH DETER-WSNED TO DO.SN TIE HIADOMH OF IER IOCHE, TIE HOLSTARB MSDOM MIO AT ONE TSWE IAD PEEN TIE UONFSDANTE OF ISH REYREHHED LOVEH AND MIOHE YERHSHTENUE IAD HAVED ISH LSFE MAH A HYEUTER OCT OF TIE YAHT. ENUAHED SN PLAUK DOMN TO IER KNCUKLEH, MSTI IER IEART TCRNED TO AHI, HIE HUARUELB KNEM ANBTISNG APOCT TIE MAR. UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA IAD TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT TIE YIOHYIOREHUENUE OF IER PONEH MAH HIOMSNG TIROCGI IER HKSN AND TIAT HIE WOVED SN AN ATWOHYIERE OF HASNT ELWO'H FSRE, SN A HTAGNANT ASR MIERE ONE UOCLD HTSLL NOTE A ISDDEN HWELL OF GCNYOMDER. AFTER HEARUISNG FOR ST CHELEHHLB SN TIE TAHTE OF EARTI, SN, TIE YERFCWED LETTERH FROW YSETRO UREHYS, SN TIE TEWYEHTCOCH PED OF IER ICHPAND, HIE IAD FOCND YEAUE SN TIAT IOCHE MIERE WEWORSEH WATERSALSZED TIROCGI TIE HTRENGTI OF SWYLAUAPLE EVOUATSON AND MALKED LSKE ICWAN PESNGH TIROCGI TIE ULOSHTERED ROOWH, LEANSNG PAUK SN IER MSUKER ROUKSNG UIASR, LOOKSNG AT UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AH SF IE MERE TIE ONE MIO LOOKED LSKE A GIOHT OCT OF TIE YAHT, REPEUA MAH NOT EVEN CYHET PB TIE NEMH TIAT TIE LANDH CHCRYED PB XOHE ARUADSO MOCLD PE RETCRNED TO TIESR RSGITFCL OMNERH."MIATEVER BOC DEUSDE MSLL PE DONE, ACRELSANO," HIE HSGIED. "S ALMABH TIOCGIT AND NOM S IAVE TIE YROOF TIAT BOC'RE A RENEGADE." TIE REVSHSON OF TIE DEEDH TOOK YLAUE AT TIE HAWE TSWE AH TIE HCWWARB UOCRTH-WARTSAL YREHSDED OVER PB UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ, MISUI ENDED MSTI TIE EJEUCTSON OF ALL OFFSUERH OF TIE REGCLAR ARWB MIO IAD PEEN TAKEN YRSHONER PB TIE REVOLCTSONARSEH. TIE LAHT UOCRT-WARTSAL MAH TIAT OF XOHE RAQCEL WONUADA. ORHCLA SNTERVENED. '"ISH GOVERNWENT MAH TIE PEHT ME'VE EVER IAD SN WAUON-DO," HIE TOLD UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HCPWSTTED HEURETLB TO TIE PCRNSNG PATIH OF YERWANGANATE AND TO DSCRETSU MATERH, AND POTI MERE UCRED HEYARATELB AFTER TIREE WONTIH OF HEURET HCFFERSNG. XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO DSD NOT HEE TIE MOWAN AGASN. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO OPTASNED IER YARDON AND HTABED MSTI IER CNTSL ISH DEATI.IER NAWE MAH YETRA UOTEH. OF TIESR LSNE. "TISH ONE MSLL PE A YRSEHT," HIE YROWSHED HOLEWNLB. "AND SF GOD GSVEH WE LSFE IE'LL PE YOYE HOWEDAB." XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO, MIO TOOK A LONG TSWE TO DSHUOVER TIAT IE IAD PEEN HCYYLANTED, MAH CNAPLE TO CNDERHTAND ISH PROTIER'H YAHHSON. DEAF TO ORHCLA'H ULAWOR AND TIE TEAHSNG OF ISH PROTIER, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO ONLB TIOCGIT AT TIAT TSWE OF FSNDSNG A TRADE TIAT MOCLD ALLOM ISW TO WASNTASN A IOCHE FOR YETRA UOTEH, AND TO DSE MSTI IER, ON TOY OF IER AND CNDER-NEATI IER, DCRSNG A NSGIT OF FEVERSHI LSUENHE. MIEN UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA OYENED CY ISH MORKHIOY AGASN, HEDCUED AT LAHT PB TIE YEAUEFCL UIARWH OF OLD AGE, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TIOCGIT TIAT ST MOCLD PE GOOD PCHSNEHH TO DEVOTE ISWHELF TO TIE WANCFAUTCRE OF LSTTLE GOLD FSHIEH. IE HYENT WANB IOCRH SN TIE IOT ROOW MATUISNG IOM TIE IARD HIEETH OF WETAL, MORKED PB TIE UOLONEL MSTI TIE SNUONUESVAPLE YATSENUE OF DSHSLLCHSONWENT, MERE HLOMLB PESNG UONVERTED SNTO GOLDEN HUALEH. TIE MORK HEEWED HO LAPORSOCH TO ISW AND TIE TIOCGIT OF YETRA UOTEH MAH HO YERHSHTENT AND YREHHSNG TIAT AFTER TIREE MEEKH IE DSHAYYEARED FROW TIE MORKHIOY. ST MAH DCRSNG TIAT TSWE TIAT ST OUUCRRED TO YETRA UOTEH TO RAFFLE OFF RAPPSTH. TIEB REYRODCUED AND GREM CY HO FAHT TIAT TIERE MAH PARELB TSWE TO HELL TIE TSUKETH FOR TIE RAFFLE. AT FSRHT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO DSD NOT NOTSUE TIE ALARWSNG YROYOR-TSONH OF TIE YROLSFERATSON. PCT ONE NSGIT, MIEN NOPODB SN TOMN MANTED TO IEAR APOCT TIE RAPPST RAFFLE ANB WORE, IE IEARD A NOSHE PB TIE UOCRTBARD DOOR. "DON'T GET MORRSED," YETRA, UOTEH HASD. "ST'H ONLB TIE RAPPSTH." TIEB UOCLD NOT HLEEY, TORWENTED PB TIE CYROAR OF TIE ANSWALH. AT DAMN ACRELSANO HEGCNDO OYENED TIE DOOR AND HAM TIE UOCRTBARD YAVED MSTI RAPPSTH, PLCE SN TIE GLOM OF DAMN. YETRA UOTEH, DBSNG MSTI LACGITER, UOCLD NOT REHSHT TIE TEWYTATSON OF TEAHSNG ISW."TIOHE ARE TIE ONEH MIO MERE PORN LAHT NSGIT," HIE ASD. "OI WB GOD!" IE HASD. "MIB DON'T BOC RAFFLE OFF UOMH?"A FEM DABH LATER, SN AN ATTEWYT TO ULEAN OCT IER UOCRTBARD, YETRA UOTEH EJUIANGED TIE RAPPSTH FOR A UOM, MIO TMO WONTIH LATER GAVE PSRTI TO TRSYLETH. TIAT MAH IOM TISNGH PEGAN. OVERNSGIT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO PE. UAWE TIE OMNER OF LAND AND LSVEHTOUK AND IE PARELB IAD TSWE TO ENLARGE ISH OVERFLOMSNG PARNH AND YSGYENH. ST MAH A DELSRSOCH YROHYERSTB TIAT EVEN WADE ISW LACGI, AND IE UOCLD NOT IELY DOSNG URAZB TISNGH TO RELEAHE ISH GOOD ICWOR. "UEAHE, UOMH, LSFE SH HIORT," IE MOCLD HIOCT. ORHCLA MONDERED MIAT ENTANGLEWENTH IE IAD GOT SNTO, MIETIER IE WSGIT PE HTEALSNG, MIETIER IE IAD PEUOWE A RCHTLER, AND EVERB TSWE HIE HAM ISW CNUORKSNG UIAWYAGNE XCHT FOR TIE YLEAHCRE OF YOCRSNG TIE FOAW OVER ISH IEAD, HIE MOCLD HIOCT AT ISW AND HUOLD ISW FOR TIE MAHTE. ST ANNOBED ISW HO WCUI TIAT ONE DAB MIEN IE AMOKE SN A WERRB WOOD, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO AYYEARED MSTI A UIEHT FCLL OF WONEB, A UAN OF YAHTE, AND A PRCHI, AND HSNGSNG AT TIE TOY OF ISH LCNGH TIE OLD HONGH OF FRANUSHUO TIE WAN, IE YAYERED TIE IOCHE SNHSDE AND OCT AND FROW TOY TO POTTOW, MSTI ONE-YEHO PANKNOTEH. TIE OLD WANHSON, YASNTED MISTE HSNUE TIE TSWE TIEB IAD PROCGIT TIE YSANOLA, TOOK ON TIE HTRANGE LOOK OF A WOHQCE. SN TIE WSDHT OF TIE EJUSTEWENT OF TIE FAWSLB TIE HUANDALSZATSON OF ORHCLA, TIE XOB OF TIE YEOYLE URAWWSNG TIE HTREET TO MATUI TIAT AYOTIEOHSH OF HQCAN-DERSNG. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO FSNSHIED PB YAYERSNG TIE IOCHE FROW TIE FRONT TO TIE KSTUIEN, SNULCDSNG PATIROOWH AND PEDROOWH, AND TIREM TIE LEFTOVER PSLLH SNTO TIE UOCRTBARD."NOM," IE HASD SN A FSNAL MAB, "S IOYE TIAT NOPODB SN TISH IOCHE EVER TALKH TO WE APOCT WONEB AGASN." TIAT MAH MIAT IAYYENED. ORHCLA IAD TIE PSLLH TAKEN DOMN, HTCUK TO GREAT UAKEH OF MISTEMAHI, AND TIE IOCHE MAH YASNTED MISTE AGASN. "DEAR LORD," HIE PEGGED, "WAKE CH YOOR AGASN TIE MAB ME MERE MIEN ME FOCNDED TISH TOMN HO TIAT BOC MSLL NOT UOLLEUT FOR TISH HQCANDERSNG SN TIE OTIER LSFE." IER YRABERH MERE ANHMERED SN REVERHE. ONE OF TIE MORKWEN REWOVSNG TIE PSLLH PCWYED SNTO AN ENORWOCH YLAHTER HTATCE OF HASNT XOHEYI TIAT HOWEONE IAD LEFT SN TIE IOCHE DCRSNG TIE LAHT BEARH OF TIE MAR AND TIE IOLLOM FSGCRE PROKE TO YSEUEH ON TIE FLOOR. ST IAD PEEN HTCFFED MSTI GOLD UOSNH. NO ONE UOCLD REWEWPER MIO IAD PROCGIT TIAT LSFE-HSZED HASNT. "TIREE WEN PROCGIT ST," AWARANTA EJYLASNED. "TIEB AHKED CH TO KEEY ST CNTSL TIE RASNH MERE OVER AND S TOLD TIEW TO YCT ST TIERE SN TIE UORNER MIERE NOPODB MOCLD PCWY SNTO ST, AND TIERE TIEB YCT ST, VERB UAREFCLLB, AND TIERE ST'H PEEN EVER HSNUE PEUACHE TIEB NEVER UAWE PAUK FOR ST." LATER ON, ORHCLA IAD YCT UANDLEH ON ST AND IAD YROHTRATED IERHELF PEFORE ST, NOT HCHYEUTSNG TIAT SNHTEAD OF A HASNT HIE MAH ADORSNG ALWOHT FOCR PCNDLED YOCNDH OF GOLD. TIE TARDB EVSDENUE OF IER SNVOLCNTARB YAGANSHW WADE IER EVEN WORE CYHET. HIE HYAT ON TIE HYEUTAU-CLAR YSLE OF UOSNH, YCT TIEW SN TIREE UANVAH HAUKH, AND PCRSED TIEW SN A HEURET YLAUE, IOYSNG TIAT HOONER OR LATER TIE TIREE CNKNOMN WEN MOCLD UOWE TO REULASW TIEW. WCUI LATER, DCRSNG TIE DSFFSUCLT BEARH OF IER DEUREYSTCDE, ORHCLA MOCLD SNTERVENE SN TIE UONVERHATSONH OF TIE WANB TRAVELERH MIO UAWE PB TIE IOCHE AT TIAT TSWE AND AHK TIEW SF TIEB IAD LEFT A YLAHTER HASNT XOHEYI TIERE DCRSNG TIE MAR TO PE TAKEN UARE OF CNTSL TIE RASNH YAHHED.TISNGH LSKE TIAT MISUI GAVE ORHCLA HCUI UONHTERNATSON, MERE UOWWONYLAUE SN TIOHE DABH. WAUONDO MAH HMAWYED SN A WSRAUCLOCH YROHYERSTB. TIE ADOPE IOCHEH OF TIE FOCNDERH IAD PEEN REYLAUED PB PRSUK PCSLDSNGH MSTI MOODEN PLSNDH AND UEWENT FLOORH MISUI WADE TIE HCFFOUATSNG IEAT OF TMO O'ULOUK SN TIE AFTERNOON WORE PEARAPLE. ALL TIAT REWASNED AT TIAT TSWE OF XOHE ARUA-DSO PCENDFA'H ANUSENT VSLLAGE MERE TIE DCHTB ALWOND TREEH, DEHTSNED TO REHSHT TIE WOHT ARDCOCH OF USRUCWHTANUEH, AND TIE RSVER OF ULEAR MATER MIOHE YREISHTORSU HTONEH IAD PEEN YCLVERSZED PB TIE FRANTSU IAWWERH OF XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MIEN IE HET APOCT OYENSNG TIE UIANNEL SN ORDER TO EHTAPLSHI A POAT LSNE. ST MAH A WAD DREAW, UOWYARAPLE TO TIOHE OF ISH GREAT-GRANDFATIER, FOR TIE ROUKB RSVERPED AND TIE NCWEROCH RAYSDH YREVENTED NAVSGATSON FROW WAUONDO TO TIE HEA. PCT XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO, SN AN CNFOREHEEN PCRHT OF TEWERSTB, HTCPPORNLB KEYT ON MSTI TIE YROXEUT. CNTSL TIEN IE IAD HIOMN NO HSGN OF SWAGSNATSON. EJUEYT FOR ISH YREUARSOCH ADVENTCRE MSTI YETRA UOTEH, IE IAD NEVER KNOMN A MOWAN. ORHCLA IAD UONHSDERED ISW TIE QCSETEHT EJAWYLE TIE FAWSLB IAD EVER YRODCUED SN ALL STH ISHTORB, SNUAYAPLE OF HTANDSNG OCT EVEN AH A IANDLER OF FSGITSNG UOUKH, MIEN UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA TOLD ISW TIE HTORB OF TIE HYANSHI GALLEON AGROCND ESGIT WSLEH FROW TIE HEA, TIE UARPONSZED FRAWE OF MISUI IE IAD HEEN ISWHELF DCRSNG TIE MAR. TIE HTORB, MISUI FOR HO WANB BEARH IAD HEEWED FANTAHTSU TO HO WANB YEOYLE, MAH A REVELATSON FOR XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO. IE ACUTSONED OFF ISH ROOHTERH TO TIE ISGIEHT PSDDER, REURCSTED WEN, POCGIT TOOLH, AND HET APOCT TIE AMEHOWE TAHK OF PREAKSNG HTONEH, DSGGSNG UANALH, ULEARSNG AMAB RAYSDH, AND EVEN IARNEHHSNG MATER-FALLH. "S KNOM ALL OF TISH PB IEART," ORHCLA MOCLD HIOCT. "ST'H AH SF TSWE IAD TCRNED AROCND AND ME MERE PAUK AT TIE PEGSNNSNG." MIEN IE TIOCGIT TIAT TIE RSVER MAH NAVSGAPLE, XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO GAVE ISH PROTIER A DETASLED AUUOCNT OF ISH YLANH AND TIE LATTER GAVE ISW TIE WONEB IE NEEDED FOR TIE ENTERYRSHE. IE DSHAYYEARED FOR A LONG TSWE. ST IAD PEEN HASD TIAT ISH YLAN TO PCB A POAT MAH NOTISNG PCT A TRSUK TO WAKE OFF MSTI ISH PROTIER'H WONEB MIEN TIE NEMH HYREAD TIAT A HTRANGE URAFT MAH AYYROAUISNG TIE TOMN. TIE SNIAPSTANTH OF WAUONDO, MIO NO LONGER REWEWPERED TIE UOLOHHAL CNDERTAKSNGH OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA, RAN TO TIE RSVERPANK AND HAM MSTI EBEH YOYYSNG SN DSHPELSEF TIE ARRSVAL OF TIE FSRHT AND LAHT POAT EVER TO DOUK SN TIE TOMN. ST MAH NOTISNG PCT A LOG RAFT DRAMN PB TISUK ROYEH YCLLED PB TMENTB WEN MIO MALKED ALONG TIE PANK. SN TIE YROM, MSTI A GLOM OF HATSHFAUTSON SN ISH EBEH, XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MAH DSREUTSNG TIE ARDCOCH WANECVER. TIERE ARRSVED MSTI ISW A RSUI GROCY OF HYLENDSD WATRONH MIO MERE YROTEUT-SNG TIEWHELVEH FROW TIE PCRNSNG HCN MSTI GACDB YARAHOLH, AND MORE ON TIESR HIOCLDERH FSNE HSLK KERUISEFH, MSTI UOLORED UREAWH ON TIESR FAUEH AND NATCRAL FLOMERH SN TIESR IASR AND GOLDEN HERYENTH ON TIESR ARWH AND DSAWONDH SN TIESR TEETI. TIE LOG RAFT MAH TIE ONLB VEHHEL TIAT XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MAH APLE TO PRSNG TO WAUON-DO, AND ONLB ONUE, PCT IE NEVER REUOGNSZED TIE FASLCRE OF ISH ENTERYRSHE, PCT YROULASWED ISH DEED AH A VSUTORB OFMSLL YOMER. IE GAVE A HURCYCLOCH AUUOCNTSNG TO ISH PROTIER AND VERB HOON YLCNGED PAUK SNTO TIE ROCTSNE OF UOUKFSGITH. TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT REWASNED OF TIAT CNFOR-TCNATE VENTCRE MAH TIE PREATI OF RENOVATSON TIAT TIE WATRONH FROW FRANUE PROCGIT, AH TIESR WAGNSFSUENT ARTH TRANHFORWED TRADSTSONAL WETIODH OF LOVE AND TIESR HENHE OF HOUSAL MELL-PESNG APOLSHIED UATARSNO'H ANTSQCATED YLAUE AND TCRNED TIE HTREET SNTO A PAZAAR OF XAYANEHE LANTERNH AND NOHTALGSU IAND ORGANH. TIEB MERE TIE YROWOTERH OF TIE PLOODB UARNSVAL TIAT YLCNGED WAUONDO SNTO DELSRSCW FOR TIREE DABH AND MIOHE ONLB LAHTSNG UONHEQCENUE MAH IAVSNG GSVEN ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TIE OYYORTCNSTB TO WEET FERNANDA DEL UARYSO.REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB MAH YROULASWED QCEEN. ORHCLA, MIO HICDDERED AT TIE DSHQCSETED PEACTB OF IER GREAT-GRANDDACGITER, UOCLD NOT YREVENT TIE UIOSUE. CNTSL TIEN HIE IAD HCUUEEDED SN KEEYSNG IER OFF TIE HTREETH CNLEHH ST MAH TO GO TO WAHH MSTI AWARANTA, PCT HIE WADE IER UOVER IER FAUE MSTI A PLAUK HIAML. TIE WOHT SWYSOCH WEN, TIOHE MIO MOCLD DSHGCSHE TIEWHELVEH AH YRSEHTH TO HAB HAURSLEGSOCH WAHHEH SN UATARSNO'H HTORE, MOCLD GO TO UICRUI MSTI AN ASW TO HEE, SF ONLB FOR AN SNHTANT, TIE FAUE OF REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB, MIOHE LEGENDARB GOOD LOOKH MERE HYOKEN OF MSTI ALARWSNG EJUSTEWENT TIROCGI-OCTTIE HMAWY. ST MAH A LONG TSWE PEFORE TIEB MERE APLE TO DO HO, AND ST MOCLD IAVE PEEN PETTER FOR TIEW SF TIEB NEVER IAD, PEUACHE WOHT OF TIEW NEVER REUOVERED TIESR YEAUEFCL IAPSTH OF HLEEY. TIE WAN MIO WADE ST YOHHSPLE, A FORESGNER, LOHT ISH HERENSTB FOREVER, PEUAWE SNVOLVED SN TIE HLOCGIH OF APXEUTSON AND WSHERB, AND BEARH LATER MAH UCT TO YSEUEH PB A TRASN AFTER IE IAD FALLEN AHLEEY ON TIE TRAUKH. FROW TIE WOWENT IE MAH HEEN SN TIE UICRUI, MEARSNG A GREEN VELVET HCST AND AN EWPROSDERED VEHT, NO ONE DOCPTED TIAT IE UAWE FROW FAR AMAB, YERIAYH FROW HOWE DSHTANT USTB OCTHSDE OF TIE UOCNTRB, ATTRAUTED PB TIE WAGSUAL FAHUSNATSON OF REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB. IE MAH HO IANDHOWE, HO ELEGANT AND DSGNSFSED, MSTI HCUI YREHENUE, TIAT YSETRO UREHYS MOCLD IAVE PEEN A WERE FOY PEHSDE ISW AND WANB MOWEN MISHYERED MSTI HYSTEFCL HWSLEH TIAT IE MAH TIE ONE MIO REALLB HIOCLD IAVE MORN TIE HIAML. IE DSD NOT HYEAK TO ANBONE SN WAUONDO. IE AYYEARED AT DAMN ON HCNDAB LSKE A YRSNUE SN A FASRB TALE, RSDSNG A IORHE MSTI HSLVER HTSRRCYH AND A VELVET PLANKET, AND IE LEFT TOMN AFTER WAHH.TIE YOMER OF ISH YREHENUE MAH HCUI TIAT FROW TIE FSRHT TSWE IE MAH HEEN SN TIE UICRUI EVERBPODB TOOK ST FOR GRANTED TIAT A HSLENT AND TENHE DCEL IAD PEEN EHTAP-LSHIED PETMEEN ISW AND REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB, A HEURET YAUT, AN SRREVOUAPLE UIALLENGE TIAT MOCLD END NOT ONLB SN LOVE PCT ALHO SN DEATI. ON TIE HSJTI HCNDAB TIE GENTLEWAN AYYEARED MSTI A BELLOM ROHE SN ISH IAND. IE IEARD WAHH HTANDSNG, AH IE ALMABH DSD, AND AT TIE END IE HTEYYED SN FRONT OF REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB AND OFFERED IER TIE HOLSTARB ROHE. HIE TOOK ST MSTI A NATCRAL GEHTCRE, AH SF HIE IAD PEEN YREYARED FOR TIAT IOWAGE, AND TIEN HIE CNUOVERED IER FAUE AND GAVE IER TIANKH MSTI A HWSLE. TIAT MAH ALL HIE DSD. NOT ONLB FOR TIE GENTLEWAN, PCT FOR ALL TIE WEN MIO IAD TIE CNFORTCNATE YRSVSLEGE OF HEESNG IER, TIAT MAH AN ETERNAL SNHTANT.FROW TIEN ON TIE GENTLEWAN IAD A PAND OF WCHSUSANH YLAB PEHSDE TIE MSNDOM OF REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB, HOWE-TSWEH CNTSL DAMN. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH TIE ONLB ONE MIO FELT A UORDSAL UOWYAHHSON FOR ISW AND IE TRSED TO PREAK ISH YERHEVERANUE. "DON'T MAHTE BOCR TSWE ANB WORE," IE TOLD ISW ONE NSGIT. "TIE MOWEN SN TISH IOCHE ARE MORHE TIAN WCLEH." IE OFFERED ISW ISH FRSEND-HISY, SNVSTED ISW TO PATIE SN UIAWYAGNE, TRSED TO WAKE ISW CNDERHTAND TIAT TIE FEWALEH OF ISH FAWSLB IAD SNHSDEH WADE OF FLSNT, PCT IE UOCLD NOT MEAKEN ISH OPHTSNAUB. EJAHYERATED PB TIE SNTERWSNAPLE NSGITH OF WCHSU, UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA TIREATENED TO UCRE ISH AFFLSUTSON MSTI A FEM YSHTOL HIOTH. NOTISNG WADE ISW DEHSHT EJUEYT ISH OMN LAWENTAPLE HTATE OF DEWORALSZA-TSON. FROW A MELL-DREHHED AND NEAT SNDSVSDCAL IE PEUAWE FSLTIB AND RAGGED. ST MAH RCWORED TIAT IE IAD APAN-DONED YOMER AND FORTCNE SN ISH DSHTANT NATSON, ALTIOCGI ISH ORSGSNH MERE AUTCALLB NEVER KNOMN. IE PEUAWE ARGC-WENTATSVE, A PARROOW PRAMLER, AND IE MOCLD MAKE CY ROLLSNG SN ISH OMN FSLTI SN UATARSNO'H HTORE. TIE HADDEHT YART OF ISH DRAWA MAH TIAT REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB DSD NOT NOTSUE ISW NOT EVEN MIEN IE AYYEARED SN UICRUI DREHHED LSKE A YRSNUE. HIE AUUEYTED TIE BELLOM ROHE MSTIOCT TIE LEAHT PST OF WALSUE, AWCHED, RATIER, PB TIE EJTRAVAGANUE OF TIE AUT, AND HIE LSFTED IER HIAML TO HEE ISH FAUE PETTER, NOT TO HIOM IERH. AUTCALLB, REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB MAH NOT A UREATCRE OF TISH MORLD. CNTSL HIE MAH MELL ALONG SN YCPERTB HANTA HOFSA DE LA. YSEDAD IAD TO PATIE AND DREHH IER, AND EVEN MIEN HIE UOCLD TAKE UARE OF IERHELF ST MAH NEUEHHARB TO KEEY AN EBE ON IER HO TIAT HIE MOCLD NOT YASNT LSTTLE ANSWALH ON TIE MALLH MSTI A HTSUK DACPED SN IER OMN EJUREWENT. HIE REAUIED TMENTB MSTIOCT KNOMSNG IOM TO READ OR MRSTE, CNAPLE TO CHE TIE HSLVER AT TIE TAPLE, MANDERSNG NAKED TIROCGI TIE IOCHE PEUACHE IER NATCRE REXEUTED ALL WANNER OF UONVENTSON. MIEN TIE BOCNG UOWWANDER OF TIE GCARD DEULARED ISH LOVE FOR IER, HIE REXEUTED ISW HSWYLB PEUACHE ISH FRSVOLSTB HTARTLED IER. "HEE IOM HSWYLE IE SH," HIE TOLD AWARANTA."IE HABH TIAT IE'H DBSNG PEUACHE OF WE, AH SF S MERE A PAD UAHE OF UOLSU." MIEN, SNDEED, TIEB FOCND ISW DEAD PEHSDE IER MSNDOM, REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB UONFSRWED IER FSRHT SWYREHHSON. "BOC HEE," HIE UOWWENTED. "IE MAH A UOWYLETE HSWYLETON." ST HEEWED AH SF HOWE YENETRATSNG LCUSDSTB YERWSTTED IER TO HEE TIE REALSTB OF TISNGH PEBOND ANB FORWALSHW. TIAT AT LEAHT MAH TIE YOSNT OF VSEM OF UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA, FOR MIOW REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB MAH SN NO MAB WENTALLB RETARDED, AH MAH GENERALLB PELSEVED, PCT QCSTE TIE OYYOHSTE. "ST'H AH SF HIE' H UOWE PAUK FROW TMENTB BEARH OF MAR," IE MOCLD HAB. ORHCLA, FOR IER YART, TIANKED GOD FOR IAVSNG AMARDED TIE FAWSLB MSTI A UREATCRE OF EJUEYTSONAL YCRSTB, PCT AT TIE HAWE TSWE HIE MAH DSHTCRPED PB IER PEACTB, FOR ST HEEWED A UONTRADSU-TORB VSRTCE TO IER, A DSAPOLSUAL TRAY AT TIE UENTER OF IER SNNOUENUE. ST MAH FOR TIAT REAHON TIAT HIE DEUSDED TO KEEY IER AMAB FROW TIE MORLD, TO YROTEUT IER FROW ALL EARTILB TEWYTATSON, NOT KNOMSNG TIAT REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB, EVEN FROW TIE TSWE MIEN HIE MAH SN IER WOTI-ER'H MOWP, MAH HAFE FROW ANB UONTAGSON. ST NEVER EN-TERED IER IEAD TIAT TIEB MOCLD ELEUT IER PEACTB QCEEN OF TIE UARNSVAL YANDEWONSCW. PCT ACRELSANO, HEGCNDO, EJUSTED AT TIE UAYRSUE OF DSHGCSHSNG ISWHELF AH A TSGER, PROCGIT FATIER ANTONSO SHAPEL TO TIE IOCHE SN ORDER TO UONVSNUE ORHCLA TIAT TIE UARNSVAL MAH NOT A YAGAN FEAHT, AH HIE HASD, PCT A UATIOLSU TRADSTSON. FSNALLB UONVSNUED, EVEN TIOCGI RELCUTANTLB, HIE UONHENTED TO TIE UORONATSON.TIE NEMH TIAT REWEDSOH PCENDFA MAH GOSNG TO PE TIE HOVERESGN RCLER OF TIE FEHTSVAL MENT PEBOND TIE LSWSTH OF TIE HMAWY SN A FEM IOCRH, REAUIED DSHTANT YLAUEH MIERE TIE YREHTSGE OF IER PEACTB MAH NOT KNOMN, AND ST AROCHED TIE ANJSETB OF TIOHE MIO HTSLL TIOCGIT OF IER LAHT NAWE AH A HBWPOL OF HCPVERHSON. TIE ANJSETB MAH PAHE-LEHH. SF ANBONE IAD PEUOWE IARWLEHH AT TIAT TSWE ST MAH TIE AGSNG AND DSHSLLCHSONED UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA, MIO MAH HLOMLB LOHSNG ALL UONTAUT MSTI TIE REALSTB OF TIE NATSON. ENULOHED SN ISH MORKHIOY, ISH ONLB RELA-TSONHISY MSTI TIE REHT OF TIE MORLD MAH ISH PCHSNEHH SN LSTTLE GOLD FSHIEH. ONE OF TIE HOLDSERH MIO IAD GCARDED ISH IOCHE DCRSNG TIE FSRHT DABH OF YEAUE MOCLD GO HELL TIEW SN TIE VSLLAGEH OF TIE HMAWY AND RETCRN LOADED DOMN MSTI UOSNH AND NEMH. TIAT TIE UONHERVATSVE GOV-ERNWENT, IE MOCLD HAB, MSTI TIE PAUKSNG OF TIE LSPERALH, MAH REFORWSNG TIE UALENDAR HO TIAT EVERB YREHSDENT UOCLD REWASN SN YOMER FOR A ICNDRED BEARH. TIAT TIE UONUORDAT MSTI TIE IOLB HEE IAD FSNALLB PEEN HSGNED AND A UARDSNAL IAD UOWE FROW ROWE MSTI A UROMN OF DSAWONDH AND A TIRONE OF HOLSD GOLD, AND TIAT TIE LSPERAL WSNSHTERH IAD IAD TIESR YSUTCREH TAKEN ON TIESR KNEEH SN TIE AUT OF KSHHSNG ISH RSNG. TIAT TIE LEADSNG LADB OF A HYANSHI UOWYANB YAHHSNG TIROCGI TIE UAYSTAL IAD PEEN KSDNAYYED PB A PAND OF WAHKED ISGIMABWEN AND ON TIE FOLLOMSNG HCNDAB HIE IAD DANUED SN TIE NCDE AT TIE HCWWER IOCHE OF TIE YREHSDENT OF TIE REYCPLSU. "DON' T TALK TO WE APOCT YOLSTSUH," TIE UOLONEL MOCLD TELL ISW. "OCR PCHSNEHH SH HELLSNG LSTTLE FSHIEH." TIE RCWOR TIAT IE DSD NOT MANT TO IEAR ANBTISNG APOCT TIE HSTCATSON SN TIE UOCNTRB PEUACHE IE MAH GROMSNG RSUI SN ISH MORKHIOY WADE ORHCLA LACGI MIEN ST REAUIED IER EARH. MSTI IER TERRSPLE YRAUTSUAL HENHE HIE UOCLD NOT CNDERHTAND TIE UOLONEL'H PCHSNEHH AH IE EJUIANGED LSTTLE FSHIEH FOR GOLD UOSNH AND TIEN UONVERTED TIE UOSNH SNTO LSTTLE FSHIEH, AND HO ON, MSTI TIE REHCLT TIAT IE IAD TO MORK ALL TIE IARDER MSTI TIE WORE IE HOLD SN ORDER TO HATSHFB AN EJAHYERATSNG VSUSOCH USRULE. AUTCALLB, MIAT SNTEREHTED ISW MAH NOT TIE PCHSNEHH PCT TIE MORK. IE NEEDED HO WCUI UONUENTRATSON TO LSNK HUALEH, FST WSNCTE RCPSEH SNTO TIE EBEH, LAWSNATE GSLLH, AND YCT ON FSNH TIAT TIERE MAH NOT TIE HWALLEHT EWYTB WOWENT LEFT FOR ISW TO FSLL MSTI ISH DSHSLLCHSONWENT OF TIE MAR. HO APHORPSNG MAH TIE ATTENTSON REQCSRED PB TIE DELSUAUB OF ISH ARTSHTRB TIAT SN A HIORT TSWE IE IAD AGED WORE TIAN DCRSNG ALL TIE BEARH OF TIE MAR, AND ISH YOHSTSON IAD TMSHTED ISH HYSNE AND TIE ULOHE MORK IAD CHED CY ISH EBEHSGIT, PCT TIE SWYLAUAPLE UONUENTRATSON AMARDED ISW MSTI A YEAUE OF TIE HYSRST. TIAT MAH TIE REAL DATE OF IER PSRTI FOR IER. FOR ACRELSANO HEGCNDO ST MAH ALWOHT HSWCLTANEOCHLB TIE PEGSNNSNG AND TIE END OF IAYYSNEHH. NOT UOCNT-SNG IOLB MEEK, HCNDABH, IOLB DABH OF OPLSGATSON, FSRHT FRSDABH, RETREATH, HAURSFSUEH, AND UBULSUAL SWYEDSWENTH, IER EFFEUTSVE BEAR MAH REDCUED TO FORTB-TMO DABH TIAT MERE HYREAD OCT TIROCGI A MEP OF YCRYLE UROHHEH. ACRELS-ANO HEGCNDO, UONVSNUED TIAT TSWE MOCLD PREAK CY TIAT IOHTSLE NETMORK, YROLONGED TIE MEDDSNG UELEPRATSON PE-BOND TIE EJYEUTED TSWE. TSRED OF TIROMSNG OCT HO WANB EWYTB PRANDB AND UIAWYAGNE POTTLEH HO TIAT TIEB MOCLD NOT ULCTTER CY TIE IOCHE AND AT TIE HAWE TSWE SNTRSGCED PB TIE FAUT TIAT TIE NEMLBMEDH HLEYT AT DSFFERENT TSWEH AND SN HEYARATE ROOWH MISLE TIE FSREMORKH AND WCHSU AND TIE HLACGITERSNG OF UATTLE MENT ON, ORHCLA REWEW-PERED IER OMN EJYERSENUE AND MONDERED MIETIER FER-NANDA WSGIT IAVE A UIAHTSTB PELT TOO MISUI MOCLD HOONER OR LATER YROVOKE XOKEH SN TIE TOMN AND GSVE RSHE TO A TRAGEDB. PCT FERNANDA UONFEHHED TO IER TIAT HIE MAH XCHT LETTSNG TMO MEEKH GO PB PEFORE ALLOMSNG TIE FSRHT UONTAUT MSTI IER ICHPAND. SNDEED, MIEN TIE YERSOD MAH OVER, HIE OYENED IER PEDROOW MSTI A REHSGNATSON MORTIB OF AN EJYSATORB VSUTSW AND ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HAM TIE WOHT PEACTSFCL MOWAN ON EARTI, MSTI IER GLORSOCH EBEH OF A FRSGITENED ANSWAL AND IER LONG, UOYYER-UOLORED IASR HYREAD OCT AUROHH TIE YSLLOM. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO UOCLD NOT HCYYREHH AN EJYLOHSON OF LACGITER. "TIAT'H TIE WOHT OPHUENE TISNG S'VE EVER HEEN SN WB LSFE," IE HIOCTED MSTI A LACGI TIAT RANG TIROCGI TIE IOCHE. "S WARRSED A HSHTER OF UIARSTB." A WONTI LATER, CNHCUUEHHFCL SN GETTSNG ISH MSFE TO TAKE OFF IER NSGITGOMN, IE IAD TIE YSUTCRE TAKEN OF YETRA UOTEH DREHHED AH A QCEEN. LATER ON, MIEN IE HCUUEEDED SN GETTSNG FERNANDA TO UOWE PAUK IOWE, HIE GAVE SN TO ISH CRGEH SN TIE FEVER OF REUONUSLSATSON, PCT HIE UOCLD NOT GSVE ISW TIE REYOHE IE IAD DREAWED APOCT MIEN IE MENT TO FETUI IER SN TIE USTB MSTI TIE TISRTB-TMO PELFRSEH. ONE NSGIT, A HIORT TSWE PEFORE TIESR FSRHT UISLD MAH PORN, FERNANDA REALSZED TIAT IER ICHPAND IAD RETCRNED SN HEURET TO TIE PED OF YETRA UOTEH."TIAT'H MIAT IAYYENED," IE ADWSTTED. "S MAH HABSNG," HIE TOLD IER, "TIAT BOC'RE ONE OF TIOHE YEOYLE MIO WSJ CY TIESR AHH AND TIESR AHIEH." FROW TIAT TSWE ON TIEB DSD NOT HYEAK TO EAUI OTIER AGASN. AH LONG AH ORHCLA IAD FCLL CHE OF IER FAUCLTSEH HOWE OF TIE OLD UCHTOWH HCRVSVED AND TIE LSFE OF TIE FAWSLB KEYT HOWE QCALSTB OF IER SWYCLHSVENEHH, PCT MIEN HIE LOHT IER HSGIT AND TIE MESGIT OF IER BEARH RELEGATED IER TO A UORNER, TIE USRULE OF RSGSDSTB PEGCN PB FERNANDA FROW TIE WOWENT HIE ARRSVED FSNALLB ULOHED UOWYLETELB AND NO ONE PCT HIE DETERWSNED TIE DEHTSNB OF TIE FAWSLB. EVEN TIE MSTIDRAMN XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO OFFERED TIEW AN AFTERNOON OF UOUKFSGITH, MISUI MAH AT TIE YOSNT OF ENDSNG SN TRAGEDB PEUACHE HEVERAL OF TIE ACRELSANOH MERE HO EJYERT SN WATTERH OF TIE UOUKYST TIAT TIEB HYOTTED FATIER ANTONSO SHAPEL'H TRSUKH AT ONUE. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, MIO HAM TIE LSWSTLEHH YROHYEUT OFMSLD TSWEH OFFERED PB TIOHE WAD RELATSVEH, DEUSDED TIAT TIEB HIOCLD ALL HTAB AND MORK FOR ISW. TIE ONLB ONE MIO AUUEYTED MAH ACRELSANO TRSHTE, A PSG WCLATTO MSTI TIE DRSVE AND EJYLORER'H HYSRST OF ISH GRANDFATIER. TIEB MERE ALL HKSLLFCL URAFTHWEN, TIE WEN OF TIESR IOCHEH, YEAUE-LOVSNG YEOYLE. TIE AHI MEDNEHDAB PEFORE TIEB MENT PAUK TO HUATTER OCT ALONG TIE UOAHT, AWARANTA GOT TIEW TO YCT ON HCNDAB ULOTIEH AND AUUOWYANB IER TO UICRUI. WORE AWCHED TIAN DEVOCT, TIEB LET TIEWHELVEH PE LED TO TIE ALTAR RASL MIERE FATIER ANTONSO SHAPEL WADE TIE HSGN OF TIE UROHH SN AHIEH ON TIEW. PAUK AT TIE IOCHE, MIEN TIE BOCNGEHT TRSED TO ULEAN ISH FOREIEAD, IE DSHUOVERED TIAT TIE WARK MAH SNDELSPLE AND HO MERE TIOHE OF ISH PROTIERH. TIE HCYYOHSTSON TIAT REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB YOHHEHHED YOMERH OF DEATI MAH TIEN PORNE OCT PB FOCR SRREFCTAPLE EVENTH. ALTIOCGI HOWE WEN MIO MERE EAHB MSTI TIESR MORDH HASD TIAT ST MAH MORTI HAURSFSUSNG ONE'H LSFE FOR A NSGIT OF LOVE MSTI HCUI AN AROCHSNG MOWAN, TIE TRCTI MAH TIAT NO ONE WADE ANB EFFORT TO DO HO. YERIAYH, NOT ONLB TO ATTASN IER PCT ALHO TO UONXCRE AMAB IER DANGERH, ALL TIAT MAH NEEDED MAH A FEELSNG AH YRSWSTSVE AND AH HSWYLE AH TIAT OF LOVE, PCT TIAT MAH TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT DSD NOT OUUCR TO ANBONE. ORHCLA DSD NOT MORRB APOCT IER ANB WORE. ON ANOTIER OUUAHSON, MIEN HIE IAD NOT BET GSVEN CY TIE SDEA OF HAVSNG IER FOR TIE MORLD, HIE IAD TRSED TO GET IER SNTEREHTED SN PAHSU DOWEHTSU AFFASRH. "WEN DEWAND WCUI WORE TIAN BOC TISNK," HIE MOCLD TELL IER ENSGWATSUALLB. "TIERE'H A LOT OF UOOKSNG, A LOT OF HMEEYSNG, A LOT OF HCFFERSNG OVER LSTTLE TISNGH PEBOND MIAT BOC TISNK." FERNANDA DSD NOT EVEN WAKE ANB ATTEWYT TO CNDERHTAND IER. MIEN HIE HAM REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB DREHHED AH A QCEEN AT TIE PLOODB UARNSVAL HIE TIOCGIT TIAT HIE MAH AN EJTRAORDSNARB UREATCRE. ISH OLD FELLOM YARTB WEWPERH, TO MIOW IE MENT AHKSNG FOR IELY, ISD HO AH NOT TO REUESVE ISW. ST MAH AROCND TIAT TSWE TIAT IE MAH IEARD TO HAB. NEVERTIELEHH IE SNHSHTED MSTI HCUI YERHEVERANUE, PEGGED SN HCUI A MAB, PROKE ISH UODE OF DSGNSTB TO HCUI A DEGREE, TIAT MSTI A LSTTLE IELY FROW IERE AND A LSTTLE WORE FROW TIERE, HNEAKSNG APOCT EVERBMIERE, MSTI A HLSYYERB DSLSGENUE AND A YSTSLEHH YERHEVERANUE, IE WANAGED TO YCT TOGETIER SN ESGIT WONTIH WORE WONEB TIAN ORHCLA IAD PCRSED. FOR IER, MSTI NO FCRTIER QCEHTSONH AHKED, YROYER YEOYLE MERE TIOHE MIO IAD NOTISNG TO DO MSTI TIE PANANA UOWYANB. EVEN XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO, IER PROTIER-SN-LAM, MAH TIE VSUTSW OF IER DSHURSWSNATORB XEALOCHB PE-UACHE DCRSNG TIE EJUSTEWENT OF TIE FSRHT DABH IE GAVE CY ISH HTCYENDOCH FSGITSNG UOUKH AGASN AND TOOK A XOP AH FOREWAN MSTI TIE PANANA UOWYANB."IE MON'T EVER UOWE SNTO TISH IOCHE AGASN," FERNANDA HASD, "AH LONG AH IE UARRSEH TIE RAHI OF TIE FORESGN-ERH." HCUI MAH TIE NARROMNEHH SWYOHED SN TIE IOCHE TIAT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO FELT WORE UOWFORTAPLE AT YETRA UOTEH'H. FSRHT, MSTI TIE YRETEJT OF TAKSNG TIE PCRDEN OFF ISH MSFE, IE TRANHFERRED ISH YARTSEH. TIEN, MSTI TIE YRETEJT TIAT TIE ANSWALH MERE LOHSNG TIESR FERTSLSTB, IE TRANHFERRED ISH PARNH AND HTAPLEH. FSNALLB, MSTI TIE YRE -TEJT TIAT ST MAH UOOLER SN ISH UONUCPSNE'H IOCHE, IE TRANHFERRED TIE HWALL OFFSUE SN MISUI IE IANDLED ISH PCHSNEHH. MIEN FERNANDA REALSZED TIAT HIE MAH A MSDOM MIOHE ICHPAND IAD HTSLL NOT DSED, ST MAH ALREADB TOO LATE FOR TISNGH TO RETCRN TO TIESR FORWER HTATE. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO PARELB ATE AT IOWE AND TIE ONLB AYYEARANUEH IE YCT SN, HCUI AH TO HLEEY MSTI ISH MSFE, MERE NOT ENOCGI TO UONVSNUE ANBONE. ONE NSGIT, OCT OF UARELEHHNEHH, WORNSNG FOCND ISW SN YETRA UOTEH'H PED. FERNAN-DA, UONTRARB TO EJYEUTATSONH, DSD NOT REYROAUI ISW SN TIE LEAHT OR GSVE TIE HLSGITEHT HSGI OF REHENTWENT, PCT ON TIE HAWE DAB HIE HENT TMO TRCNKH MSTI ISH ULOTISNG TO TIE IOCHE OF ISH UONUCPSNE. HIE HENT TIEW SN PROAD DABLSGIT AND MSTI SNHTRCUTSONH TIAT TIEB PE UARRSED TIROCGI TIE WSDDLE OF TIE HTREET HO TIAT EVERBONE UOCLD HEE TIEW, TISNKSNG TIAT IER HTRABSNG ICHPAND MOCLD PE CNAPLE TO PEAR TIE HIAWE AND MOCLD RETCRN TO TIE FOLD MSTI ISH IEAD ICNG LOM. PCT TIAT IEROSU GEHTCRE MAH XCHT ONE WORE YROOF OF IOM YOORLB FERNANDA KNEM NOT ONLB TIE UIARAUTER OF IER ICHPAND PCT TIE UIARAUTER OF A UOWWCNSTB TIAT IAD NOTISNG TO DO MSTI TIAT OF IER YARENTH, FOR EVERBONE MIO HAM TIE TRCNKH YAHH PB HASD TIAT ST MAH TIE NATCRAL UCLWSNATSON OF A HTORB MIOHE SNTSWAUSEH MERE KNOMN TO EVERBONE, AND ACRELSANO HEGCNDO UELEPRATED TIE FREEDOW IE IAD REUESVED MSTI A YARTB TIAT LAHTED FOR TIREE DABH. TO TIE GREATER DSHAD-VANTAGE OF ISH MSFE, AH HIE MAH ENTERSNG SNTO A HAD WATCRSTB MSTI IER HOWPER LONG DREHHEH, IER OLD-FAHISONED WEDALH, AND IER OCT-OF-YLAUE YRSDE, TIE UONUCPSNE HEEWED TO PE PCRHTSNG MSTI A HEUOND BOCTI, ULOTIED SN GACDB DREHHEH OF NATCRAL HSLK AND MSTI IER EBEH TSGER-HTRSYED MSTI A GLOM OF VSNDSUATSON. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO GAVE ISWHELF OVER TO IER AGASN MSTI TIE FCRB OF ADOLEHUENUE, AH PEFORE, MIEN YETRA UOTEH IAD NOT LOVED ISW FOR ISWHELF PCT PEUACHE HIE IAD ISW WSJED CY MSTI ISH TMSN PROTIER AND AH HIE HLEYT MSTI POTI OF TIEW AT TIE HAWE TSWE HIE TIOCGIT TIAT GOD IAD GSVEN IER TIE GOOD FORTCNE OF IAVSNG A WAN MIO UOCLD WAKE LOVE LSKE TMO. TIE REHTORED YAHHSON MAH HO YREHHSNG TIAT ON WORE TIAN ONE OUUAHSON TIEB MOCLD LOOK EAUI OTIER SN TIE EBEH AH TIEB MERE GETTSNG READB TO EAT AND MSTIOCT HABSNG ANBTISNG TIEB MOCLD UOVER TIESR YLATEH AND GO SNTO TIE PEDROOW DBSNG OF ICNGER AND OF LOVE. SNHYSRED PB TIE TISNGH IE IAD HEEN ON ISH FCRTSVE VSHSTH TO TIE FRENUI WATRONH, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO POCGIT YETRA UOTEH A PED MSTI AN ARUISEYSHUOYAL UANOYB, YCT VELVET UCRTASNH ON TIE MSNDOMH, AND UOVERED TIE UESLSNG AND TIE MALLH OF TIE PEDROOW MSTI LARGE ROUK-URBHTAL WSRRORH. AT TIE HAWE TSWE IE MAH WORE OF A UAROCHER AND HYENDTIRSFT TIAN EVER. ON TIE TRASN, MISUI ARRSVED EVERB DAB AT ELEVEN O' ULOUK, IE MOCLD REUESVE UAHEH AND WORE UAHEH OF UIAW-YAGNE AND PRANDB. ON TIE MAB PAUK FROW TIE HTATSON IE MOCLD DRAG TIE SWYROVSHEDUCWPSAWPA ALONG SN FCLL VSEM OF ALL TIE YEOYLE ON TIE MAB, NATSVEH OR OCTHSDERH, AUQCASNTANUEH OR YEOYLE BET TO PE KNOMN, MSTIOCT DSH-TSNUTSONH OF ANB KSND. EVEN TIE HLSYYERB WR. PROMN, MIO TALKED ONLB SN A HTRANGE TONGCE, LET ISWHELF PE HEDCUED PB TIE TEWYTSNG HSGNH TIAT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO WADE ISW AND HEVERAL TSWEH IE GOT DEAD DRCNK SN YETRA UOTEH'H IOCHE AND IE EVEN WADE TIE FSERUE GERWAN HIEYIERD DOGH TIAT MENT EVERBMIERE MSTI ISW DANUE TO HOWE TEJAH HONGH TIAT IE ISWHELF WCWPLED SN ONE MAB OR ANOTIER TO TIE AUUOWYANSWENT OF TIE AUUORDSON."UEAHE, UOMH," ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HIOCTED AT TIE IESGIT OF TIE YARTB. "UEAHE, PEUACHE LSFE SH HIORT." IE NEVER LOOKED PETTER, NOR IAD IE PEEN LOVED WORE, NOR IAD TIE PREEDSNG OF ISH ANSWALH PEEN MSLDER. TIERE MAH A HLACGITERSNG OF HO WANB UOMH, YSGH, AND UISUKENH FOR TIE ENDLEHH YARTSEH TIAT TIE GROCND SN TIE UOCRTBARD TCRNED PLAUK AND WCDDB MSTI HO WCUI PLOOD. ST MAH AN ETERNAL EJEUCTSON GROCND OF PONEH AND SNNARDH, A WCD YST OF LEFTOVERH, AND TIEB IAD TO KEEY EJYLODSNG DBNA-WSTE POWPH ALL TIE TSWE HO TIAT TIE PCZZARDH MOCLD NOT YLCUK OCT TIE GCEHTH' EBEH. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO GREM FAT, YCRYLE-UOLORED, TCRTLE-HIAYED, PEUACHE OF AN AYYETSTE UOWYARAPLE ONLB TO TIAT OF XOHE ARUADSO MIEN IE UAWE PAUK FROW TRAVELSNG AROCND TIE MORLD. TIE YREHTSGE OF ISH OCTLANDSHI VORAUSTB, OF ISH SWWENHE UAYAUSTB AH A HYENDTIRSFT, OF ISH CNYREUEDENTED IOHYSTALSTB MENT PE-BOND TIE PORDERH OF TIE HMAWY AND ATTRAUTED TIE PEHT-QCALSFSED GLCTTONH FROW ALL ALONG TIE UOAHT. FAPCLOCH EATERH ARRSVED FROW EVERBMIERE TO TAKE YART SN TIE SRRATSONAL TOCRNEBH OF UAYAUSTB AND REHSHTANUE TIAT MERE ORGANSZED SN TIE IOCHE OF YETRA UOTEH. ACRELSANO HEGCN-DO MAH TIE CNUONQCERED EATER CNTSL TIE LCUKLEHH HATCR-DAB MIEN UAWSLA HAGAHTCWE AYYEARED, A TOTEWSU FEWALE KNOMN ALL TIROCGI TIE LAND PB TIE GOOD NAWE OF "TIE ELEYIANT." TIE DCEL LAHTED CNTSL DAMN ON TCEHDAB. DCRSNG TIE FSRHT TMENTB-FOCR IOCRH, IAVSNG DSHYATUIED A DSNNER OF VEAL, MSTI UAHHAVA, BAWH, AND FRSED PANANAH, AND A UAHE AND A IALF OF UIAWYAGNE SN ADDSTSON, ACRELS-ANO HEGCNDO MAH HCRE OF VSUTORB. IE HEEWED WORE ENTICHSAHTSU, WORE VSTAL TIAN ISH SWYERTCRPAPLE ADVERHARB, MIO YOHHEHHED A HTBLE TIAT MAH OPVSOCHLB WORE YROFEH-HSONAL, PCT AT TIE HAWE TSWE LEHH EWOTSONAL FOR TIE LARGE UROMD TIAT FSLLED TIE IOCHE. MISLE ACRELSANO HEGCNDO ATE MSTI GREAT PSTEH, OVERUOWE PB TIE ANJSETB OF VSUTORB, TIE ELEYIANT MAH HLSUSNG IER WEAT MSTI TIE ART OF A HCRGEON AND EATSNG ST CNICRRSEDLB AND EVEN MSTI A UERTASN YLEAHCRE. HIE MAH GSGANTSU AND HTCRDB, PCT OVER IER UOLOHHAL FORW A TENDERNEHH OF FEWSNSNSTB YREVASLED AND HIE IAD A FAUE TIAT MAH HO PEACTSFCL, IANDH HO FSNE AND MELL UARED FOR, AND HCUI AN SRREHSHTSPLE YERHONAL UIARW TIAT MIEN ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HAM IER ENTER TIE IOCHE IE UOWWENTED SN A LOM VOSUE TIAT IE MOCLD IAVE YREFERRED TO IAVE TIE TOCRNEB SN PED AND NOT AT TIE TAPLE. LATER ON, MIEN IE HAM IER UONHCWE A HSDE OF VEAL MSTIOCT PREAKSNG A HSNGLE RCLE OF GOOD TAPLE WANNERH, IE UOWWENTED HERSOCHLB TIAT TIAT DELSUATE, FAHUSNATSNG, AND SNHATSAPLE YROPOHUSDSAN MAH SN A UERTASN MAB TIE SDEAL MOWAN. IE MAH NOT WSHTAKEN. TIE REYCTATSON OF A PONE URCHIER TIAT IAD YREUEDED TIE ELEYIANT IAD NO PAHSH. HIE MAH NOT A PEEF URCNUIER OR A PEARDED LADB FROW A GREEK USRUCH, AH IAD PEEN HASD, PCT TIE DSREUTOR OF A HUIOOL OF VOSUE. HIE IAD LEARNED TO EAT MIEN HIE MAH ALREADB TIE REHYEUTAPLE WOTIER OF A FAWSLB, LOOKSNG FOR A MAB FOR IER UISLDREN TO EAT PETTER AND NOT PB WEANH OF ANB ARTSFSUSAL HTSWCLATSON OF TIESR AYYETSTEH PCT TIROCGI TIE APHOLCTE TRANQCSLSTB OF TIESR HYSRSTH. FROW TIE FSRHT WOWENT HIE HAM ISW HIE HAM TIAT ACRELSANO HEGCN-DO MOCLD LOHE NOT ISH HTOWAUI PCT ISH UIARAUTER. AT TIE END OF TIE FSRHT NSGIT, MISLE TIE ELEYIANT MAH POLDLB GOSNG ON, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH MEARSNG ISWHELF OCT MSTI A GREAT DEAL OF TALKSNG AND LACGISNG. TIEB HLEYT FOCR IOCRH. IE MAH, TIEREFORE, WORE DANGEROCH TIAN HIE IADTIOCGIT. NEVERTIELEHH, MIEN YETRA UOTEH PROCGIT TMO ROAHT TCRKEBH TO TIE TAPLE, ACRELSANO HEGCN-DO MAH A HTEY AMAB FROW PESNG HTCFFED. "LET'H UALL ST A TSE."HIE HASD ST FROW IER IEART, CNDERHTANDSNG TIAT HIE UOCLD NOT EAT ANOTIER WOCTIFCL ESTIER, OCT OF REWORHE FOR PRSNGSNG ON TIE DEATI OF IER ADVERHARB. PCT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO SNTERYRETED ST AH ANOTIER UIALLENGE AND IE FSLLED ISWHELF MSTI TCRKEB PEBOND ISH SNUREDSPLE UAYAUSTB. IE LOHT UONHUSOCHNEHH. IE FELL FAUE DOMN SNTO TIE YLATE FSLLED MSTI PONEH, FROTISNG AT TIE WOCTI LSKE A DOG, AND DROMNSNG SN WOANH OF AGONB. "TAKE WE TO FERNANDA," IE WANAGED TO HAB.ISH FRSENDH LEFT ISW AT TIE IOCHE TISNKSNG TIAT TIEB IAD IELYED ISW FCLFSLL ISH YROWSHE TO ISH MSFE NOT TO DSE SN ISH UONUCPSNE'H PED. YETRA UOTEH IAD HISNED ISH YATENT LEATIER POOTH TIAT IE MANTED TO MEAR SN ISH UOFFSN, AND HIE MAH ALREADB LOOKSNG FOR HOWEONE TO TAKE TIEW MIEN TIEB UAWE TO TELL IER TIAT ACRELSANOHEGCNDO MAH OCT OF DANGER. IE DSD REUOVER, SNDEED, SN LEHH TIAN A MEEK, AND TMO MEEKH LATER IE MAH UELEPRATSNG TIE FAUT OF ISH HCRVSVAL MSTI CNYREUEDENTED FEHTSVSTSEH. DCRSNG TIE POREDOW OF IER APANDONWENT IER ONLB DSHTRAUTSONH MERE TIE ULAV-SUIORD LEHHONH AT HSEHTA TSWE AND TIE LETTERH FROW IER UISLDREN. UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA MAH A HIADOM. HSNUE TIE LAHT TSWE TIAT IE IAD GONE OCT SNTO TIE HTREET TO YROYOHE A MAR MSTIOCT ANB FCTCRE TO UOLONEL GERS-NELDO WARQCEZ, IE LEFT TIE MORKHIOY ONLB TO CRSNATE CNDER TIE UIEHTNCT TREE. "BOC IAVE A IEART OF HTONE," HIE TOLD ISW."ST'H NOT A QCEHTSON OF A IEART," IE HASD. "TIE ROOW'H GETTSNG FCLL OF WOTIH."AWARANTA MAH MEAVSNG IER HIROCD. FERNANDA DSD NOT CNDERHTAND MIB HIE MOCLD MRSTE OUUAHSONAL LETTERH TO WEWE AND EVEN HEND IER GSFTH AND ON TIE OTIER IAND DSD NOT EVEN MANT TO IEAR APOCT XOHE ARUADSO. "TIEB'LL DSE MSTIOCT KNOMSNG MIB," AWARANTA ANHMERED MIEN HIE MAH AHKED TIROCGI ORHCLA, AND TIAT ANHMER YLANTED AN ENSGWA SN FERNANDA'H IEART TIAT HIE MAH NEVER APLE TO ULARSFB. TALL, PROAD-HIOCLDERED, YROCD, ALMABH DREHHED SN APCNDANT YETTSUOATH MSTI TIE LAUE AND SN ASR OF DSHTSNUTSON TIAT REHSHTED TIE BEARH AND PAD WEWORSEH, AWARANTA HEEWED TO UARRB TIE UROHH OF AHIEH OF VSRGSNSTB ON IER FOREIEAD. FERNANDA LAWENTED. "TISH UISLD SH AH WCUI OF A PARPARSAN AH IER FATIER!"ST MAH NEUEHHARB TO PORROM PEDH AND IAWWOUKH FROW TIE NESGIPORH, TO HET CY NSNE HISFTH AT TIE TAPLE, TO FSJ IOCRH FOR PATISNG, AND TO PORROM FORTB HTOOLH HO TIAT TIE GSRLH SN PLCE CNSFORWH MSTI WAHUCLSNE PCTTONH MOCLD NOT HYEND TIE MIOLE DAB RCNNSNG FROW ONE YLAUE TOANOTIER . "ARHENSU," AWARANTA ANHMERED.TIE NSGIT OF TIESR ARRSVAL TIE HTCDENTH UARRSED ON SN HCUI A MAB, TRBSNG TO GO TO TIE PATIROOW PEFORE TIEB MENT TO PED, TIAT AT ONE O'ULOUK SN TIE WORNSNG TIE LAHT ONEH MERE HTSLL GOSNG SN. FERNANDA TIEN POCGIT HEVENTB-TMO UIAWPERYOTH PCT HIE ONLB WANAGED TO UIANGE TIE NOUTCRNAL YROPLEW SNTO A WORNSNG ONE, PEUACHE FROW DAMN ON TIERE MAH A LONG LSNE OF GSRLH, EAUI MSTI IER YOT SN IER IAND, MASTSNG FOR IER TCRN TO MAHI ST. HIE RE-TCRNED TIE PORROMED PEDH AND HTOOLH AND KEYT TIE HEVENTB-TMO UIAWPERYOTH SN WELQCFADEH'ROOW. TIE LOUKED ROOW, APOCT MISUI TIE HYSRSTCAL LSFE OF TIE IOCHE REVOLVED SN FORWER TSWEH, MAH KNOMN FROW TIAT TSWE ON AH TIE "UIAWPERYOT ROOW." FOR UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA ST MAH TIE WOHT AYYROYRSATE NAWE, PEUACHE MISLE TIE REHT OF TIE FAWSLB MAH HTSLL AWAZED PB TIE FAUT TIAT WELQCFADEH' ROOW MAH SWWCNE TO DCHT AND DE-HTRCUTSON, IE HAM ST TCRNED SNTO A DCNGISLL. SN ANB UAHE, ST DSD NOT HEEW TO POTIER ISW MIO MAH UORREUT, AND SF IE FOCND OCT APOCT TIE FATE OF TIE ROOW ST MAH PEUACHE FERNANDA KEYT YAHHSNG PB AND DSHTCRPSNG ISH MORK FOR A MIOLE AFTERNOON AH HIE YCT AMAB TIE UIAWPERYOTH.DCRSNG TIOHE DABH XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO REAYYEARED SN TIE IOCHE. IE MENT ALONG TIE YORUI MSTIOCT GREETSNG ANBONE AND IE HICT ISWHELF CY SN TIE MORKHIOY TO TALK TO TIE UOLONEL. SN HYSTE OF TIE FAUT TIAT HIE UOCLD NOT HEE ISW, ORHCLA ANALBZED TIE ULSUKSNG OF ISH FOREWAN'H POOTH AND MAH HCRYRSHED AT TIE CNPRSDGEAPLE DSHTANUE TIAT HEYARATED ISW FROW TIE FAWSLB, EVEN FROW TIE TMSN PROTIER MSTI MIOW IE IAD YLABED SNGENSOCH GAWEH OF UONFCHSON SN UISLDIOOD AND MSTI MIOW IE NO LONGER IAD ANB TRASTH SN UOWWON. IE MAH LSNEAR, HOLEWN, AND IAD A YENHSVE ASR AND TIE HADNEHH OF A HARAUEN AND A WOCRNFCL GLOM ON ISH FAUE TIAT MAH TIE UOLOR OF AC-TCWN. IE MAH TIE ONE MIO WOHT REHEWPLED ISH WOTIER, HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD. ORHCLA REYROAUIED IERHELF FOR TIE IAPST OF FORGETTSNG APOCT ISW MIEN HIE HYOKE APOCT TIE FAWSLB, PCT MIEN HIE HENHED ISW SN TIE IOCHE AGASN AND NOTSUED TIAT TIE UOLONEL LET ISW SNTO TIE MORKHIOY DCRSNG MORKSNG IOCRH, HIE REEJAWSNED IER OLD WEWORSEH AND UONFSRWED TIE PELSEF TIAT AT HOWE WOWENT SN UISLDIOOD IE IAD UIANGED YLAUEH MSTI ISH TMSN PROTIER, PEUACHE ST MAH IE AND NOT TIE OTIER ONE MIO HIOCLD IAVE PEEN UALLED ACRELSANO. NO ONE KNEM TIE DETASLH OF ISH LSFE. AT ONE TSWE ST MAH DSHUOVERED TIAT IE IAD NO FSJED APODE, TIAT IE RASHED FSGITSNG UOUKH AT YSLAR TERNERA'H IOCHE AND TIAT HOWETSWEH IE MOCLD HTAB TIERE TO HLEEY PCT TIAT IE ALWOHT ALMABH HYENT TIE NSGIT SN TIE ROOWH OF TIE FRENUI WATRONH. IE DRSFTED APOCT, MSTI NO TSEH OF AFFEUTSON, MSTI NO AWPSTSONH, LSKE A MANDERSNG HTAR SN ORHCLA'H YLANETARB HBHTEW.SN REALSTB, XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MAH NOT A WEWPER OF TIE FAWSLB, NOR MOCLD IE EVER PE OF ANB OTIER HSNUE TIAT DSHTANT DAMN MIEN UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ TOOK ISW TO TIE PARRAUKH, NOT HO TIAT IE UOCLD HEE AN EJEUCTSON, PCT HO TIAT FOR TIE REHT OF ISH LSFE IE MOCLD NEVER FORGET TIE HAD AND HOWEMIAT WOUKSNG HWSLE OF TIE WAN PESNG HIOT. TIAT MAH NOT ONLB ISH OLDEHT WEWORB, PCT TIE ONLB ONE IE IAD OF ISH UISLDIOOD. TIE OTIER ONE, TIAT OF AN OLD WAN MSTI AN OLD-FAHISONED VEHT AND A IAT MSTI A PRSW LSKE A UROM 'H MSNGH MIO TOLD ISW WARVELOCH TISNGH FRAWED SN A DAZZLSNG MSNDOM, IE MAH CNAPLE TO YLAUE SN ANB YERSOD. ST MAH AN CNUERTASN WEWORB, ENTSRELB DEVOSD OF LEHHONH OR NOHTALGSA, TIE OYYOHSTE OF TIE WEWORB OF TIE EJEUCTED WAN, MISUI IAD REALLB HET TIE DSREUTSON OF ISH LSFE AND MOCLD RETCRN TO ISH WEWORB ULEARER AND DEARER AH IE GREM OLDER, AH SF TIE YAHHAGE OF TSWE MERE PRSNGSNG ISW ULOHER TO ST. ORHCLA TRSED TO CHE XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO TO GET UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA TO GSVE CY ISH SWYRSHON-WENT. "GET ISW TO GO TO TIE WOVSEH," HIE HASD TO ISW. "EVEN SF IE DOEHN'T LSKE TIE YSUTCRE, AH LEAHT IE'LL PREATIE A LSTTLE FREHI ASR." PCT ST DSD NOT TAKE IER LONG TO REALSZE TIAT IE MAH AH SNHENHSPLE TO IER PEGGSNG AH TIE UOLONEL MOCLD IAVE PEEN, AND TIAT TIEB MERE ARWORED PB TIE HAWE SWYERWEAPSLSTB OF AFFEUTSON. ALTIOCGI HIE NEVER KNEM, NOR DSD ANBONE KNOM, MIAT TIEB HYOKE APOCT SN TIESR YROLONGED HEHHSONH HICT CY SN TIE MORKHIOY, HIE CNDERHTOOD TIAT TIEB MERE YROPAPLB TIE ONLB WEWPERH OF TIE FAWSLB MIO HEEWED DRAMN TOGETIER PB HOWE AFFSNSTB.TIE TRCTI SH TIAT NOT EVEN XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MOCLD IAVE PEEN APLE TO DRAM TIE UOLONEL OCT OF ISH UONFSNEWENT. TIE SNVAHSON OF HUIOOLGSRLH IAD LOMERED TIE LSWSTH OF ISH YATSENUE. MSTI TIE YRETEJT TIAT ISH MEDDSNG PEDROOW MAH AT TIE WERUB OF TIE WOTIH SN HYSTE OF TIE DEHTRCUTSON OF REWEDSOH' AYYETSZSNG DOLLH, IE ICNG A IAWWOUK SN TIE MORKHIOY AND TIEN IE MOCLD LEAVE ST ONLB TO GO SNTO TIE UOCRTBARD TO TAKE UARE OF ISH NEUEHHSTSEH. ORHCLA MAH CNAPLE TO HTRSNG TOGETIER EVEN A TRSVSAL UONVERHATSON MSTI ISW. HIE KNEM TIAT IE DSD NOT LOOK AT TIE DSHIEH OF FOOD PCT MOCLD YCT TIEW AT ONE END OF ISH MORKPENUI MISLE IE FSNSHIED A LSTTLE FSHI AND ST DSD NOT WATTER TO ISW SF TIE HOCY UCRDLED OR SF TIE WEAT GOT UOLD. IE GREM IARDER AND IARDER EVER HSNUE UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ REFCHED TO PAUK ISW CY SN A HENSLE MAR. IE LOUKED ISWHELF CY SNHSDE ISWHELF AND TIE FAWSLB FSNALLB TIOCGIT OFISW SH SF IE MERE DEAD. NO OTIER ICWAN REAUTSON MAH HEEN SN ISW CNTSL ONE OUTOPER ELEVENTI, MIEN IE MENT TO TIE HTREET DOOR TO MATUI A USRUCH YARADE. FOR UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA ST IAD PEEN A DAB XCHT LSKE ALL TIOHE OF ISH LAHT BEARH. AT FSVE O'ULOUK SN TIE WORNSNG TIE NOSHE OF TIE TOADH AND URSUKETH OCTHSDE TIE MALL MOKE ISW CY. TIE DRSZZLE IAD YERHSHTED HSNUE HATCRDAB AND TIERE MAH NO NEUEHHSTB FOR ISW TO IEAR TIESR TSNB MISHYERSNG AWONG TIE LEAVEH OF TIE GARDEN PEUACHE IE MOCLD IAVE FELT TIE UOLD SN ISH PONEH SN ANB UAHE. IE MAH, AH ALMABH, MRAYYED SN ISH MOOLEN PLANKET AND MEARSNG ISH URCDE UOTTON LONG DRAM-ERH, MISUI IE HTSLL MORE FOR UOWFORT, EVEN TIOCGI PE-UACHE OF TIESR WCHTB, OLD-FAHISONED HTBLE IE UALLED TIEW ISH "GOTI DRAMERH." IE YCT ON ISH TSGIT YANTH PCT DSD NOT PCTTON TIEW CY, NOR DSD IE YCT TIE GOLD PCTTON SNTO ISH HISRT UOLLAR AH IE ALMABH DSD, PEUACHE IE YLANNED TO TAKE A PATI. TIEN IE YCT TIE PLANKET OVER ISH IEAD LSKE A UOML. PRCHIED ISH DRSYYSNG WCHTAUIE MSTI ISH FSNGERH, AND MENT TO CRSNATE SN TIE UOCRTBARD. TIERE MAH HTSLL HO WCUI TSWE LEFT FOR TIE HCN TO UOWE OCT TIAT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MAH HTSLL DOZSNG CNDER TIE HIELTER OF YALW FRONDH TIAT IAD PEEN ROTTED PB TIE RASN. IE DSD NOT HEE ISW, AH IE IAD NEVER HEEN ISW, NOR DSD IE IEAR TIE SNUOWYREIENHSPLE YIRAHE TIAT TIE GIOHT OF ISH FATIER ADDREHHED TO ISW AH IE AMAKENED, HTARTLED PB TIE HTREAW OF IOT CRSNE TIAT HYLATTERED ISH HIOEH. IE YCT TIE PATI OFF FOR LATER, NOT PEUACHE OF TIE UOLD AND TIE DAWYNEHH, PCT PEUACHE OF TIE OYYREHHSVE OUTOPER WSHT. ON ISH MAB PAUK TO TIE MORKHIOY IE NOTSUED TIE ODOR OF TIE MSUK TIAT HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD MAH CHSNG TO LSGIT TIE HTOVEH, AND IE MASTED SN TIE KSTUIEN FOR TIE UOFFEE TO POSL HO TIAT IE UOCLD TAKE ALONG ISH WCG MSTIOCT HCGAR. HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD AHKED ISW, AH ON EVERB WORNSNG, MIAT DAB OF TIE MEEK ST MAH, AND IE ANHMERED TIAT ST MAH TCEHDAB, OUTOPER ELEVENTI. MATUISNG TIE GLOM OF TIE FSRE AH ST GSLDED TIE YERHSHTENT MOWAN MIO NESTIER TIEN NOR SN ANB SNHTANT OF IER LSFE HEEWED TO EJSHT UOWYLETELB, IE HCDDENLB REWEWPERED TIAT ON ONE OUTOPER ELEVENTI SN TIE WSDDLE OF TIE MAR IE IAD AMAKENED MSTI TIE PRCTAL UERTASNTB TIAT TIE MOWAN MSTI MIOW IE IAD HLEYT MAH DEAD. HIE REALLB MAH AND IE UOCLD NOT FORGET TIE DATE PEUACHE HIE IAD AHKED ISW AN IOCR PEFORE MIAT DAB ST MAH. SN HYSTE OF TIE WEWORB IE DSD NOT IAVE AN AMARENEHH TISH TSWE ESTIER OF TO MIAT DEGREE ISH OWENH IAD APANDONED ISW AND MISLE TIE UOFFEE MAH POSLSNG IE KEYT ON TISNKSNG OCT OF YCRE UCRSOHSTB PCT MSTIOCT TIE HLSGITEHT RSHK OF NOHTALGSA APOCT TIE MOWAN MIOHE NAWE IE IAD NEVER KNOMN AND MIOHE FAUE IE IAD NOT HEEN PEUACHE HIE IAD HTCWPLED TO ISH IAWWOUK SN TIE DARK. NEVERTIELEHH, SN TIE EWYTSNEHH OF HO WANB MOWEN MIO UAWE SNTO ISH LSFE SN TIE HAWE MAB, IE DSD NOT REWEWPER TIAT HIE MAH TIE ONE MIO SN TIE DELSRSCW OF TIAT FSRHT WEETSNG MAH ON TIE YOSNT OF FOCNDERSNG SN IER OMN TEARH AND HUARUELB AN IOCR PEFORE IER DEATI IAD HMORN TO LOVE ISW CNTSL HIE DSED. IE DSD NOT TISNK APOCT IER AGASN OR APOCT ANB OF TIE OTIERH AFTER IE MENT SNTO TIE MORKHIOY MSTI TIE HTEAWSNG UCY, AND IE LSGITED TIE LAWY SN ORDER TO UOCNT TIE LSTTLE GOLD FSHIEH, MISUI IE KEYT SN A TSN YASL. TIERE MERE HEVENTEEN OF TIEW. HSNUE IE IAD DEUSDED NOT TO HELL ANB, IE KEYT ON WAKSNG TMO FSHIEH A DAB AND MIEN IE FSNSHIED TMENTB-FSVE IE MOCLD WELT TIEW DOMN AND HTART ALL OVER AGASN. IE MORKED ALL WORNSNG, APHORPED, MSTI-OCT TISNKSNG APOCT ANBTISNG, MSTIOCT REALSZSNG TIAT AT TEN O'ULOUK TIE RASN IAD GROMN HTRONGER AND HOWEONE RAN YAHT TIE MORKHIOY HIOCTSNG TO ULOHE TIE DOORH PEFORE TIE IOCHE MAH FLOODED, AND MSTIOCT TISNKSNG EVEN APOCT ISWHELF CNTSL ORHCLA UAWE SN MSTI ISH LCNUI AND TCRNED OCT TIE LSGIT."MIAT A RASN!" ORHCLA HASD. "OUTOPER," IE HASD.MIEN IE HASD ST IE DSD NOT RASHE ISH EBEH FROW TIE FSRHT LSTTLE FSHI OF TIE DAB PEUACHE IE MAH YCTTSNG SN TIE RCPSEH FOR TIE EBEH. ONLB MIEN IE FSNSHIED ST AND YCT ST MSTI TIE OTIERH SN TIE YASL DSD IE PEGSN TO DRSNK TIE HOCY. TIEN, VERB HLOMLB, IE ATE TIE YSEUE OF WEAT ROAHTED MSTI ONSONH, TIE MISTE RSUE, AND TIE HLSUEH OF FRSED PANANAH ALL ON TIE HAWE YLATE TOGETIER. ISH AYYE-TSTE DSD NOT UIANGE CNDER ESTIER TIE PEHT OR TIE IARHIEHT OF USRUCWHTANUEH. AFTER LCNUI IE FELT TIE DROMHSNEHH OF SNAUTSVSTB. PEUACHE OF A KSND OF HUSENTSFSU HCYERHTSTSON IE NEVER MORKED, OR READ, OR PATIED, OR WADE LOVE CNTSL TMO IOCRH OF DSGEHTSON IAD GONE PB, AND ST MAH HCUI A DEEY-ROOTED PELSEF TIAT HEVERAL TSWEH IE IELD CY WSLSTARB OYERATSONH HO AH NOT TO HCPWST TIE TROOYH TO TIE RSHKH OF SNDSGEHTSON. HO IE LAB DOMN SN TIE IAWWOUK, REWOVSNG TIE MAJ FROW ISH EARH MSTI A YENKNSFE, AND SN A FEM WSNCTEH IE MAH AHLEEY. IE DREAWED TIAT IE MAH GOSNG SNTO AN EWYTB IOCHE MSTI MISTE MALLH AND TIAT IE MAH CYHET PB TIE PCRDEN OF PESNG TIE FSRHT ICWAN PESNG TO ENTER ST. SN TIE DREAW IE REWEWPERED TIAT IE IAD DREAWED TIE HAWE TISNG TIE NSGIT PEFORE AND ON WANB NSGITH OVER TIE YAHT BEARH AND IE KNEM TIAT TIE SWAGE MOCLD PE ERAHED FROW ISH WEWORB MIEN IE AMAKENED PEUACHE TIAT REUCRRENT DREAW IAD TIE QCALSTB OF NOT PESNG REWEWPERED EJUEYT MSTISN TIE DREAW STHELF. A WOWENT LATER, SNDEED, MIEN TIE PARPER KNOUKED AT TIE MORKHIOY DOOR, UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AMOKE MSTI TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT IE IAD FALLEN AHLEEY SNVOLCN-TARSLB FOR A FEM HEUONDH AND TIAT IE IAD NOT IAD TSWE TO DREAW ANBTISNG. "NOT TODAB." IE TOLD TIE PARPER. "ME'LL WAKE ST ON FRSDAB." IE IAD A TIREE-DAB PEARD HYEUKLED MSTI MISTE IASRH, PCT IE DSD NOT TISNK ST NEUEHHARB TO HIAVE PEUACHE ON FRSDAB IE MAH GOSNG TO IAVE ISH IASR UCT AND ST UOCLD ALL PE DONE AT TIE HAWE TSWE. TIE HTSUKB HMEAT OF TIE CNMANTED HSEHTA AROCHED TIE HUARH OF TIE HOREH SN ISH ARWYSTH. TIE HKB IAD ULEARED PCT TIE HCN IAD NOT UOWE OCT. UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA RELEAHED A HONOROCH PELUI MISUI PROCGIT PAUK TIE AUSDSTB OF TIE HOCY TO ISH YALATE AND MISUI MAH LSKE A UOWWAND FROW ISH ORGANSHW TO TIROM ISH PLANKET OVER ISH HIOCLDERH AND GO TO TIE TOSLET. IE HTABED TIERE LONGER TIAN MAH NEUEHHARB, UROCUIED OVER TIE DENHE FERWENTATSON TIAT MAH UOWSNG OCT OF TIE MOODEN POJ CNTSL IAPST TOLD ISW TIAT ST MAH TSWE TO HTART MORK AGASN. DCRSNG TIE TSWE IE LSNGERED IE REWEWPERED AGASN TIAT ST MAH TCEHDAB, AND TIAT XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO IAD NOT UOWE TO TIE MORKHIOY PEUACHE ST MAH YABDAB ON TIE PANANA UOWYANB FARWH. TIAT REUOLLEUTSON, AH ALL OF TIOHE OF TIE YAHT FEM BEARH, LED ISW TO TISNK APOCT TIE MAR MSTIOCT ISH REALSZSNG ST. IE REWEWPERED TIAT UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ IAD ONUE YROWSHED TO GET ISW A IORHE MSTI A MISTE HTAR ON STH FAUE AND TIAT IE IAD NEVER HYOKEN APOCT ST AGASN. TIEN IE MENT ON TOMARD HUATTERED EYSHODEH PCT IE PROCGIT TIEW PAUK MSTIOCT ANB XCDGWENT PEUACHE HSNUE IE UOCLD NOT TISNK APOCT ANBTISNG ELHE, IE IAD LEARNED TO TISNK UOLDLB HO TIAT SNEHUAYAPLE WEWORSEH MOCLD NOT TOCUI ANB FEELSNG. ON ISH MAB PAUK TO TIE MORKHIOY, HEESNG TIAT TIE ASR MAH PEGSNNSNG TO DRB OCT, IE DEUSDED TIAT ST MAH A GOOD TSWE TO TAKE A PATI, PCT AWARANTA IAD GOT TIERE AIEAD OF ISW. HO IE HTARTED ON TIE HEUOND LSTTLE FSHI OF TIE DAB. IE MAH YCTTSNG A IOOK ON TIE TASL MIEN TIE HCN UAWE OCT MSTI HCUI HTRENGTI TIAT TIE LSGIT UREAKED LSKE A FSHISNG POAT. TIE ASR, MISUI IAD PEEN MAHIED PB TIE TIREE-DAB DRSZZLE, MAH FSLLED MSTI FLBSNG ANTH. TIEN IE UAWE TO TIE REALSZATSON TIAT IE FELT LSKE CRSNATSNG AND IE IAD PEEN YCTTSNG ST OFF CNTSL IE IAD FSNSHIED FSJSNG TIE LSTTLE FSHI. IE MENT OCT SNTO TIE UOCRTBARD AT TEN WSNCTEH AFTER FOCR, MIEN IE IEARD TIE DSHTANT PRAHH SNHTRCWENTH, TIE PEATSNG OF TIE PAHH DRCW AND TIE HIOCTSNG OF TIE UISLDREN, AND FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE HSNUE ISH BOCTI IE KNOMSNGLB FELL SNTO A TRAY OF NOHTALGSA AND RELSVED TIAT YRODSGSOCH AFTERNOON OF TIE GBYHSEH MIEN ISH FATIER TOOK ISW TO HEE SUE. HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD DROYYED MIAT HIE MAH DOSNG SN TIE KSTUIEN AND RAN TO TIE DOOR."ST'H TIE USRUCH," HIE HIOCTED.SNHTEAD OF GOSNG TO TIE UIEHTNCT TREE, UOLONEL ACRELS-ANO PCENDFA ALHO MENT TO TIE HTREET DOOR AND WSNGLED MSTI TIE PBHTANDERH MIO, MERE MATUISNG TIE YARADE. IE HAM A MOWAN DREHHED SN GOLD HSTTSNG ON TIE IEAD OF AN ELEYIANT. IE HAM A HAD DROWEDARB. IE HAM A PEAR DREHHED LSKE A DCTUI GSRL KEEYSNG TSWE TO TIE WCHSU MSTI A HOCY HYOON AND A YAN. IE HAM TIE ULOMNH DOSNG UARTMIEELH AT TIE END OF TIE YARADE AND ONUE WORE IE HAM TIE FAUE OF ISH WSHERAPLE HOLSTCDE MIEN EVERBTISNG IAD YAHHED PB AND TIERE MAH NOTISNG PCT TIE PRSGIT EJYANHE OF TIE HTREET AND TIE ASR FCLL OF FLBSNG ANTH MSTI A FEM ONLOOKERH YEERSNG SNTO TIE YREUSYSUE OF CNUERTASN-TB. IE YCLLED ISH IEAD SN PETMEEN ISH HIOCL-DERH LSKE A PAPB UISUK AND REWASNED WOTSONLEHH MSTI ISH FOREIEAD AGASNHT TIE TRCNK OF TIE UIEHTNCT TREE. TIE HICTTERED IOCHE MAH NO YLAUE FORYARTSEH. TIEB HYOKE SN MISHYERH, ATE SN HSLENUE, REUSTED TIE ROHARB TIREETSWEH A DAB, AND EVEN ULAVSUIORD YRAUTSUE DCRSNG TIE IEAT OF HSEHTA TSWEIAD A FCNEREAL EUIO. SN HYSTE OF IER HEURET IOHTSLSTB TOMARD TIE UOLONEL, STMAH FERNANDA MIO SWYOHED TIE RSGOR OF TIAT WOCRNSNG, SWYREHHED PB TIEHOLEWNSTB MSTI MISUI TIE GOVERNWENT EJALTED TIE WEWO-RB OF STH DEADENEWB. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, AH MAH ISH UCHTOW UAWE PAUK TO HLEEYSN TIE IOCHE DCRSNG ISH DACGITER'H VAUATSON AND FERNANDA WCHT IAVEDONE HOWE. TISNG TO REGASN IER YRSVSLEGEH AH ISH LEGSTSWATE MSFE PEUACHETIE FOLLOMSNG BEAR WEWE FOCND A NEMPORN LSTTLE HSHTER MIO AGASNHT TIEMSHIEH OF IER WOTIER IAD PEEN PAYTSZED MSTI TIE NAWE AWARANTA ORHCLA.WEWE IAD FSNSHIED IER UOCRHE OF HTCDB.
