WORE TIAN IER ART, TIE GCEHTH ADWSRED IER DCALSTB. IER FRSVOLOCH AND EVEN HLSGITLB SNFANTSLE UIARAUTER DSD NOT HEEW CY TO ANB HERSOCH AUTSVSTB, PCT MIEN HIE HAT DOMN AT TIE ULAVSUIORD HIE PEUAWE A DSFFERENT GSRL, ONE MIOHE CNFOREHEEN WATCRSTB GAVE IER TIE ASR OF AN ADCLT. TIAT MAH IOM HIE IAD ALMABH PEEN. HIE REALLB DSD AW IAVE ANB DEFSNSTE VOUATSON, PCT HIE IAD EARNED TIE ISGIEHT GRADEH PB WEANH OF SNFLEJSPLE DSHUSYLSNE HSWYLB SN ORDER NOT TO ANNOB IER WOTIER. TIEB UOCLD IAVE SWYOHED ON IER AN AYYRENTSUEHISY SN ANB OTIER FSELD AND TIE REHCLTH MOCLD IAVE PEEN TIE HAWE. HSNUE HIE IAD PEEN VERB HWALL HIE IAD PEEN TROCPLED PB FERNANDA'H HTRSUTNEHH, IER UCHTOW OF DEUSDSNG SN FAVOR OF EJTREWEH; AND HIE MOCLD IAVE PEEN UAYAPLE OF A WCUI WORE DSFFSUCLT HAURSFSUE TIAN TIE ULAVSUIORD LEHHONH WERELB NOT TO RCN CY AGASNHT IER SNTRANHSGENUE. DCRSNG TIE GRADCATSON UERE-WONSEH HIE IAD TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT TIE YARUIWENT MSTI GOTISU LETTERH AND SLLCWSNATED UAYSTALH MAH FREESNG IER FROW A UOWYROWSHE TIAT HIE IAD AUUEYTED NOT HO WCUI OCT OF OPEDSENUE AH OCT OF UONVENSENUE, AND HIE TIOCGIT TIAT FROW TIEN ON NOT EVEN TIE SNHSHTENT FERNANDA MOCLD MORRB ANB WORE APOCT AN SNHTRCWENT TIAT EVEN TIE NCNH LOOKED CYON AH A WCHECW FOHHSL. DCRSNG TIE FSRHT BEARH HIE TIOCGIT TIAT IER UALUCLATSONH MERE WSHTAK-EN PEUACHE AFTER HIE IAD YCT IALF TIE TOMN TO HLEEY, NOT ONLB SN TIE YARLOR PCT ALHO AT ALL UIARSTAPLE FCNUTSONH, HUIOOL UEREWONSEH, AND YATRSOTSU UELEPRATSONH TIAT TOOK YLAUE SN WAUONDO, IER WOTIER HTSLL SNVSTED TO TIE IOCHE EVERB NEMUOWER MIOW HIE TIOCGIT UAYAPLE OF AYYREUSAT-SNG IER DACGITER'H VSRTCEH. ONLB AFTER TIE DEATI OF AWARANTA, MIEN TIE FAWSLB HICT STHELF CY AGASN SN A YERSOD OF WOCRNSNG, MAH WEWE APLE TO LOUK TIE ULAV-SUIORD AND FORGET TIE KEB SN HOWE DREHHER DRAMER MSTIOCT FERNANDA'H PESNG ANNOBED ON FSNDSNG OCT MIEN AND TIROCGI MIOHE FACLT ST IAD PEEN LOHT. WEWE PORE CY CNDER TIE EJISPSTSONH MSTI TIE HAWE HTOSUSHW TIAT HIE IAD DEDSUATED TO IER AYYRENTSUEHISY. ST MAH TIE YRSUE OF IER FREEDOW. FERNANDA MAH HO YLEAHED MSTI IER DOUSLSTB AND HO YROCD OF TIE ADWSRATSON TIAT IER ART SNHYSRED TIAT HIE MAH NEVER AGASNHT TIE IOCHE PESNG FALL OF GSRL FRSENDH, IER HYENDSNG TIE AFTERNOON SN TIE GROVEH, AND GOSNG TO TIE WOVSEH MSTI ACRELSANO HEGCNDO OR HOWE WCTED LADB AH LONG AH TIE FSLW MAH AYYROVED PB FATIER ANTONSO SHAPEL FROW TIE YCLYST. DCRSNG TIOHE WOWENTH OF RELAJATSON WEWE'H REAL TAHTEH MERE REVEALED. IER IAYYSNEHH LAB AT TIE OTIER EJTREWE FROW DSHUSYLSNE, SN NOSHB YARTSEH, SN GOHHSY APOCT LOVERH, SN YROLONGED HEH-HSONH MSTI IER GSRL FRSENDH, MIERE TIEB LEARNED TO HWOKE AND TALKED APOCT WALE PCHSNEHH, AND MIERE TIEB ONUE GOT TIESR IANDH ON HOWE UANE LSQCOR AND ENDED CY NAKED, WEAHCRSNG AND UOWYARSNG TIE YARTH OF TIESR PODSEH. WEWE MOCLD NEVER FORGET TIAT NSGIT MIEN HIE ARRSVED IOWE UIEMSNG LSUORSUE LOZENGEH, AND MSTIOCT NOTSUSNG TIESR UONHTERNATSON, HAT DOMN AT TIE TAPLE MIERE FERNANDA AND AWARANTA MERE EATSNG DSNNER MSTI-OCT HABSNG A MORD TO EAUI OTIER. HIE IAD HYENT TMO TREWENDOCH IOCRH SN TIE PEDROOW OF A GSRL FRSEND, MEEYSNG MSTI LACGITER AND FEAR, ANDPEBOND AN URSHEH HIE IAD FOCND TIE RARE FEELSNG OF. PRAVERB TIAT HIE NEEDED SN ORDER TO RCN AMAB FROW HUIOOL AND TELL IER WOTIER SN ONE MAB OR ANOTIER TIAT HIE UOCLD CHE TIE ULAVSUIORD AH AN ENEWA. HSTTSNG AT TIE IEAD OF TIE TAPLE, DRSNKSNG A UISUKEN PROTI TIAT LANDED SN IER HTOWAUI LSKE AN ELSJSR OF REHCRREUTSON, WEWE TIEN HAM FERNANDA AND AWARANTA MRAYYED SN AN AUUCHATORB IALO OF REALSTB. HIE IAD TO WAKE A GREAT EFFORT NOT TO TIROM AT TIEW TIESR YRSHHSNEHH, TIESR YOVERTB OF HYSRST TIESR DELCHSONH OF GRANDECR. FROW TIE TSWE OF IER HEUOND VAUATSON HIE IAD KNOMN TIAT IER FATIER MAH LSVSNG AT IOWE ONLB SN ORDER TO KEEY CY AYYEARANUEH, AND KNOMSNG FERNANDA AH HIE DSD AND IAVSNG ARRANGED LATER TO WEET YETRA UOTEH, HIE TIOCGIT TIAT IER FATIER MAH RSGIT. HIE ALHO MOCLD IAVE YREFERRED PESNG TIE DACGITER OF TIE UONUCPSNE. SN TIE IAZSNEHH OF TIE ALUOIOL WEWE TIOCGIT MSTI YLEAHCRE APOCT TIE HUANDAL TIAT MOCLD IAVE TAKEN YLAUE SF HIE MERE TO EJYREHH IER TIOCGITH AT TIAT WOWENT, AND TIE SNTSWATE HATSHFAUTSON OF IER ROGCSHINEHH MAH HO SNTENHE TIAT FERNANDA NOTSUED ST. "MIAT'H TIE WATTER?" HIE AHKED."NOTISNG," WEWE ANHMERED. "S MAH ONLB NOM DSHUOV-ERSNG IOM WCUI S LOVED BOC POTI."AWARANTA MAH HTARTLED PB TIE OPVSOCH PCRDEN OF IATE TIAT TIE DEULARATSON UARRSED. PCT FERNANDA FELT HO WOVED TIAT HIE TIOCGIT HIE MOCLD GO WAD MIEN WEWE AMOKE AT WSDNSGIT MSTI IER IEAD HYLSTTSNG MSTI YASN AND DROMNSNG SN VOWSTED GALL. HIE GAVE IER A VSAL OF UAHTOR OSL, YCT UOWYREHHEH ON IER HTOWAUI AND SUE UCPEH ON IER IEAD, AND HIE WADE IER HTAB SN PED FOR FSVE DABH AND FOLLOM TIE DSET ORDERED PB TIE NEM AND OCTLANDSHI FRENUI DOUTOR, MIO AFTER EJAWSNSNG IER FOR WORE TIAN TMO IOCRH REAUIED TIE FOGGB UONULCHSON TIAT HIE IAD AN ASLWENT YEUCLSAR TO MOWEN. IAVSNG LOHT IER UOCRAGE, SN A WSHERAPLE HTATE OF DEWORALSZATSON, WEWE IAD NO OTIER REUOCRHE PCT TO PEAR CY CNDER ST. ORHCLA, UOWYLETELB PLSND PB TIEN PCT HTSLL AUTSVE AND LCUSD, MAH TIE ONLB ONE MIO GCEHHED TIE EJAUT DSAGNOHSH. "AH FAR AH S UAN HEE," HIE TIOCGIT, "TIAT'H TIE HAWE TISNG TIAT IAYYENH TO DRCNKEN YEOYLE." PCT HIE NOT ONLB REXEUTED TIE SDEA, HIE REYROAUIED IERHELF FOR TIE FRSVOLSTB OF IER TIOCGIT. ACRE-LSANO HEGCNDO FELT A TMSNGE OF UONHUSENUE MIEN IE HAM WEWE'H HTATE OF YROHTRATSON AND IE YROWSHED ISWHELF TO TAKE PETTER UARE OF IER SN TIE FCTCRE. TIAT MAH IOM TIE RELATSONHISY OFXOLLB UOWRADEHISY MAH PORN PETMEEN FATIER AND DACGITER, MISUI FREED ISW FOR A TSWE FROW TIE PSTTER HOLSTCDE OF ISH REVELH AND FREED IER FROW FERNANDA'H MATUIFCL EBE MSTIOCT NEUEHHSTB OF YROVOKSNG TIE DOWEHTSU URSHSH TIAT HEEWED SNEVSTAPLE PB TIEN. AT TIAT TSWE ACRELSANO HEGCNDO YOHTYONED ANB AYYOSNT-WENTH SN ORDER TO PE MSTI WEWE, TO TAKE IER TO TIE WOVSEH OR TIE USRUCH, AND IE HYENT TIE GREATER YART OF ISH SDLE TSWE MSTI IER. SN REUENT TSWEH ISH ANNOBANUE MSTI TIE APHCRD OPEHSTB TIAT YREVENTED ISW FROW TBSNG ISH HIOEH AND ISH APCHSVE HATSHFAUTSON MSTI ALL WANNER OF AYYETSTEH IAD PEGAN TO HOCR ISH UIARAUTER. TIE DSHUOVERB OF ISH DACGITER REHTORED ISH FORWER XOVSALSTB AND TIE YLEAHCRE OF PESNG MSTI IER MAH HLOMLB LEADSNG ISW AMAB FROW DSHHSYATSON. WEWE MAH ENTERSNG A FRCSTFCL AGE. HIE MAH NOT PEACTSFCL, AH AWARANTA IAD NEVER PEEN, PCT ON TIE OTIER IAND HIE MAH YLEAHANT, CNUOWYLSUATED, AND HIE IAD TIE VSRTCE OF WAKSNG A GOOD SWYREHHSON ON YEOYLE FROW TIE FSRHT WOWENT. HIE IAD A WODEW HYSRST TIAT MOCNDED TIE ANTSQCATED HOPRSETB AND YOORLB DSHGCSHED WSHERLB IEART OF FERNANDA, AND TIAT, ON TIE OTIER IAND, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TOOK YLEAHCRE SN DEVELOYSNG. ST MAH IE MIO REHOLVED TO TAKE IER OCT OF TIE PEDROOW HIE IAD OUUCYSED HSNUE UISLDIOOD, MIERE TIE FEARFCL EBEH OF TIE HASNTH HTSLL FED IER ADOLEHUENT TERRORH, AND IE FCRNSHIED FOR IER A ROOW MSTI A ROBAL PED, A LARGE DREHHSNG TAPLE, AND VELVET UCRTASNH, NOT REALSZSNG TIAT IE MAH YRODCUSNG A HEUOND VERHSON OF YETRA UOTEH'H ROOW. IE MAH HO LAVSHI MSTI WEWE TIAT IE DSD NOT EVEN KNOM IOM WCUI WONEB IE GAVE IER PEUACHE HIE IERHELF MOCLD TAKE ST OCT OF ISH YOUKETH, AND IE KEYT APREAHT OF EVERB KSND OF NEM PEACTB ASD TIAT ARRSVED SN TIE UOWWSHHARB OF TIE PANANA UOWYANB. WEWE'H ROOW PEUAWE FSLLED MSTI YCWSUE-HTONE UCHISONH TO YOLSHI IER NASLH MSTI, IASR UCRLERH, TOOTI-PRCHIEH, DROYH TO WAKE IER EBEH LANGCSD, AND HO WANB AND HCUI NEM UOHWETSUH AND ARTSFAUTH OF PEACTB TIAT EVERB TSWE FERNANDA MENT SNTO TIE ROOW HIE MAH HUAN-DALSZED PB TIE SDEA TIAT IER DACGITER' H DREHHSNG TAPLE WCHT IAVE PEEN TIE HAWE AH TIOHE OF TIE FRENUI WA-TRONH. NEVERTIELEHH FERNANDA DSVSDED IER TSWE SN TIOHE DABH PETMEEN LSTTLE AWARANTA ORHCLA, MIO MAH WSHUISEVOCH AND HSUKLB, AND A TOCUISNG UORREHYONDENUE MSTI TIE SNVSHSPLE YIBHSUSANH. HO TIAT MIEN HIE NOTSUED TIE UOWYLSUSTB PETMEEN FATIER AND DACGITER TIE ONLB YROWSHE HIE EJTRAUTED FROW ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH TIAT IE MOCLD NEVER TAKE WEWE TO YETRA UOTEH'H IOCHE. ST MAH A WEANSNGLEHH DEWAND PEUACHE TIE UONUCPSNE MAH HO ANNOBED MSTI TIE UOWRADEHISY PETMEEN IER LOVER AND ISH DACGITER TIAT HIE DSD NOT MANT ANBTISNG TO DO MSTI IER. YETRA MAH TORWENTED PB AN CNKNOMN FEAR, AH SF SNHTSNUT MERE TELLSNG IER TIAT WEWE, PB XCHT MANTSNG ST, UOCLD HCUUEED SN MIAT FERNANDA IAD PEEN CNAPLE TO DO: DEYRSVE IER OF A LOVE TIAT PB TIEN HIE UONHSDERED AHHCRED CNTSL DEATI. FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE ACRELSANO HEGCN-DO IAD TO TOLERATE TIE IARHI EJYREHHSONH AND TIE VSOLENT TSRADEH OFISH UONUCPSNE, AND IE MAH EVEN AFRASD TIAT ISH MANDERSNG TRCNKH MOCLD WAKE TIE RETCRN XOCRNEB TO ISH MSFE'H IOCHE. TIAT DSD NOT IAYYEN. NO ONE KNEM A WAN PETTER TIAN YETRA UOTEH KNEM IER LOVER AND HIE KNEM TIAT TIE TRCNKH MOCLD REWASN MIERE TIEB IAD PEEN HENT PEUACHE SF ACRELSANO HEGCNDO DETEHTED ANBTISNG ST MAH UOWYLSUATSNG ISH LSFE MSTI WODSFSUATSONH AND UIANGEH. HO TIE TRCNKH HTABED MIERE TIEB MERE AND YETRA UOTEH HET APOCT REUONQCERSNG TIE ICHPAND PB HIARYENSNG TIE ONLB MEAYONH TIAT ISH DACGITER UOCLD NOT CHE ON ISW. ST TOO MAH AN CNNEUEHHARB EFFORT PEUACHE WEWE IAD NO DEHSRE TO SNTERVENE SN IER FATIER'H AFFASRH AND SF HIE IAD, ST MOCLD UERTASNLB IAVE PEEN SN FAVOR OF TIE UONUCPSNE. HIE IAD NO TSWE TO POTIER ANBPODB. HIE IERHELF HMEYT IER ROOW AND WADE IER PED, AH TIE NCNH IAD TACGIT IER. SN TIE WORNSNG HIE TOOK UARE OF IER ULOTIEH, HEMSNG ON TIE YORUI OR CHSNG AWARANTA'H OLD YEDAL WAUISNE. MISLE TIE OTIERH MERE TAKSNG TIESR HSEHTAH HIE MOCLD YRAUTSUE TIE ULAVSUIORD FOR TMO IOCRH, KNOMSNG TIAT TIE DASLB HAURSFSUE MOCLD KEEY FERNANDA UALW. FOR TIE HAWE REAHON HIE UONTSNCED GSVSNG UONUERTH AT UICRUI FASRH AND HUIOOL YARTSEH, EVEN TIOCGI TIE REQCEHTH MERE LEHH AND LEHH FREQCENT. AT NSGITFALL HIE MOCLD FSJ IERHELF CY, YCT ON ONE OF IER HSWYLE DREHHEH AND IER HTSFF ISGI HIOEH, AND SF HIE IAD NOTISNG TO DO MSTI IER FATIER HIE MOCLD GO TO TIE IOWEH OF IER GSRL FRSENDH, MIERE HIE MOCLD HTAB CNTSL DSNNERTSWE. ST MAH RARE TIAT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MOCLD NOT UALL FOR IER TIEN TO TAKE IER TO TIE WOVSEH. AWONG WEWE'H FRSENDH TIERE MERE TIREE BOCNG AWERS-UAN GSRLH MIO PROKE TIROCGI TIE ELEUTRSFSED UISUKEN FENUE PARRSER AND WADE FRSENDH MSTI GSRLH FROW WAUON-DO. ONE OF TIEW MAH YATRSUSA PROMN. GRATEFCL FOR TIE IOHYSTALSTB OF ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, WR. PROMN OYENED TIE DOORH OF ISH IOCHE TO WEWE AND SNVSTED IER TO TIE HATCRDAB DANUEH, MISUI MERE TIE ONLB ONEH MIERE GRSNGOH AND NATSVEH WSNGLED. MIEN FERNANDA FOCND OCT APOCT ST HIE FORGOT APOCT AWARANTA ORHCLA AND TIE SNVSHSPLE DOUTORH FOR A WOWENT AND PEUAWE VERB WELO-DRAWATSU. "XCHT TISNK," HIE HASD TO WEWE, "MIAT TIE UOLONEL WCHT PE TISNKSNG SN ISH GRAVE." HIE HOCGIT, OF UOCRHE, TIE PAUKSNG OF ORHCLA. PCT TIE PLSND OLD MOW-AN, UONTRARB TO MIAT EVERBONE EJYEUTED, HAM NOTISNG REYROAUIAPLE SN WEWE'H GOSNG TO TIE DANUEH AND WAKSNG FRSENDH MSTI AWERSUAN GSRLH IER OMN AGE AH LONG AH HIE KEYT IER HTRSUT IAPSTH AND MAH NOT UONVERTED TO TIE YROTEHTANT RELSGSON. WEWE HENHED TIE TIOCGIT OF IER GREAT-GREAT-GRANDWOTIER VERB MELL AND TIE DAB AFTER TIE DANUEH HIE MOCLD GET CY EARLSER TIAN CHCAL TO GO TO WAHH. FERNANDA'H OYYOHSTSON LAHTED CNTSL TIE DAB MIEN WEWE PROKE DOMN IER REHSHTANUE MSTI TIE NEMH TIAT TIE AWERSUANH MANTED TO IEAR IER YLAB TIE ULAVSUIORD. TIE SNHTRCWENT MAH TAKEN OCT OF TIE IOCHE AGASN AND UARRSED TO WR. PROMN'H, MIERE TIE BOCNG UONUERT ARTSHT REALLB DSD REUESVE VERB HSNUERE AYYLACHE AND TIE WOHT ENTICHS-AHTSU UONGRATCLATSONH. FROW TIEN ON HIE MAH SNVSTED NOT ONLB TO TIE DANUEH PCT ALHO TO TIE HCNDAB HMSW YARTSEH SN TIE YOOL AND TO LCNUI ONUE A MEEK. WEWE LEARNED TO HMSW LSKE A YROFEHHSONAL, TO YLAB TENNSH, AND TO EAT VSRGSNSA IAW MSTI HLSUEH OF YSNEAYYLE. AWONG DANUEH, HMSWWSNG, AND TENNSH HIE HOON FOCND IERHELF GETTSNG SNVOLVED SN TIE ENGLSHI LANGCAGE. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH HO ENTICHSAHTSU OVER TIE YROGREHH OF ISH DACGITER TIAT FROW A TRAVELSNG HALEHWAN IE POCGIT A HSJ-VOLCWE ENGLSHI ENUBULOYEDSA MSTI WANB UOLOR YRSNTH MISUI WEWE READ SN IER HYARE TSWE. TIE READSNG OUUCYSED TIE ATTENTSON TIAT HIE IAD FORWERLB GSVEN TO GOHHSY APOCT HMEETIEARTH AND TIE EJYERSWENTAL RETREATH TIAT HIE MOCLD GO TIROCGI MSTI IER GSRL FRSENDH, NOT PEUACHE ST MAH SWYOHED AH DSHUSYLSNE PCT PEUACHE HIE IAD LOHT ALL SNTEREHT PB TIEN SN TALKSNG APOCT WBHTERSEH TIAT MERE SN TIE YCPLSU DOWASN. HIE LOOKED PAUK ON TIE DRCNKEN EYSHODE AH AN SNFANTSLE ADVENTCRE AND ST HEEWED HO FCNNB TO IER TIAT HIE TOLD ACRELSANO HEGCNDO APOCT ST AND IE TIOCGIT ST MAH WORE AWCHSNG TIAN HIE DSD. "SF BOCR WOTIER ONLB KNEM," IE TOLD IER, DOCPLSNG CY MSTI LACGITER, AH IE ALMABH HASD MIEN IE TOLD IER HOWETISNG SN UONFSDENUE. IE IAD WADE IER YROWSHE TIAT HIE MOCLD LET ISW KNOM APOCT IER FSRHT LOVE AFFASR MSTI TIE HAWE UONFSDENUE, AND WEWE TOLD ISW TIAT HIE LSKED A RED-IEADED AWERSUAN POB MIO IAD UOWE TO HYEND ISH VAUATSON MSTI ISH YARENTH. "MIAT DO BOC KNOM," ACRELS-ANO HEGCNDO HASD, LACGISNG. "SF BOCR WOTIER ONLB KNEM." PCT WEWE ALHO TOLD ISW TIAT TIE POB IAD GONE PAUK TO ISH UOCNTRB AND IAD DSHAYYEARED FROW HSGIT. TIE WATCRSTB OF IER XCDGWENT ENHCRED YEAUE SN TIE FAWSLB. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TIEN DEVOTED WORE TSWE TO YETRA UOTEH, AND ALTIOCGI ISH PODB AND HOCL NO LONGER YERWSTTED ISW TIE DEPACUIEH OF DABH GONE PB, IE LOHT NO UIANUE TO ARRANGE TIEW AND TO DSG OCT TIE AUUORDSON, MISUI PB TIEN IAD HOWE KEBH IELD SN YLAUE PB HIOELAUEH. AT IOWE, AWARANTA MAH MEAVSNG IER SNTERWSNAPLE HIROCD AND ORHCLA DRAGGED APOCT SN IER DEUREYSTCDE TIROCGI TIE DEYTIH OF TIE HIADOMH MIERE TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT MAH HTSLL VSHSPLE MAH TIE GIOHT OF XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA CNDER TIE UIEHTNCT TREE. FERNANDA UONHOLSDATED IER ACTIORSTB. IER WONTILB LETTERH TO IER HON XOHE ARUADSO AT TIAT TSWE DSD NOT UARRB A HTRSNG OF LSEH AND HIE ISD FROW ISW ONLB IER UORREHYONDENUE MSTI TIE SNVSHSPLE DOUTORH, MIO IAD DSAGNOHED A PENSGN TCWOR SN IER LARGE SNTEHTSNE AND MERE YREYARSNG IER FOR A TELEYATISU OYERATSON.ST WSGIT IAVE PEEN ASD TIAT YEAUE AND IAYYSNEHH RESGNED FOR A LONG TSWE SN TIE TSRED WANHSON OF TIE PCENDFAH SF ST IAD NOT PEEN FOR TIE HCDDEN DEATI OF AWARANTA, MISUI UACHED A NEM CYROAR. ST MAH AN CNEJ-YEUTED EVENT. ALTIOCGI HIE MAH OLD AND SHOLATED FROW EVERBONE, HIE HTSLL LOOKED FSRW AND CYRSGIT AND MSTI TIE IEALTI OF A ROUK TIAT HIE IAD ALMABH IAD. NO ONE KNEM IER TIOCGITH HSNUE TIE AFTERNOON ON MISUI HIE IAD GSVEN UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ ISH FSNAL REXEUTSON AND HICT IERHELF CY TO MEEY. HIE MAH NOT HEEN TO URB DCRSNG TIE AHUENHSON TO IEAVEN OF REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB OR OVER TIE EJTERWSNATSON OF TIE ACRELSANOH OR TIE DEATI OF UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA, MIO MAH TIE YERHON HIE LOVED WOHT SN TISH MORLD, ALTIOCGI HIE HIOMED ST ONLB MIEN TIEB FOCND ISH PODB CNDER TIE UIEHTNCT TREE. HIE IELYED YSUK CY TIE PODB. HIE DREHHED ISW SN ISH HOLDSER'H CNSFORW, HIAVED ISW, UOWPED ISH IASR, AND MAJED ISH WCHTAUIE PETTER TIAN IE IAD EVER DONE SN ISH DABH OF GLORB. NO ONE TIOCGIT TIAT TIERE MAH ANB LOVE SN TIAT AUT PEUACHE TIEB MERE AUUCHTOWED TO TIE FAWSLSARSTB OF AWARANTA MSTI TIE RSTEH OF DEATI. FERNANDA MAH HUANDALSZED TIAT HIE DSD NOT CNDERHTAND TIE RELATSONHISY OF UATIOLSUSHW MSTI LSFE PCT ONLB STH RELATSONHISY MSTI DEATI, AH SF ST MERE NOT A RELSGSON PCT A UOWYENDSCW OF FCNERAL UONVENTSONH. AWARANTA MAH TOO MRAYYED CY SN TIE EGGYLANT YATUI OF IER WEWORSEH TO CNDERHTAND TIOHE HCPTLE AYOLOGETSUH. HIE IAD REAUIED OLD AGE MSTI ALL OF IER NOHTALGSAH SNTAUT. MIEN HIE LSHTENED TO TIE MALTZEH OF YSETRO UREHYS HIE FELT TIE HAWE DEHSRE TO MEEY TIAT HIE IAD IAD SN ADOLEHUENUE, AH SF TSWE AND IARHI LEHHONH IAD WEANT NOTISNG. TIE ROLLH OF WCHSU TIAT HIE IERHELF IAD TIROMN SNTO TIE TRAHI MSTI TIE YRETEJT TIAT TIEB IAD ROTTED FROW DAWYNEHH KEYT HYSNNSNG AND YLABSNG SN IER WEWORB. HIE IAD TRSED TO HSNK TIEW SNTO TIE HMAWYB YAHHSON TIAT HIE ALLOMED IERHELF MSTI IER NEYIEM ACRELSANO XOHE AND HIE TRSED TO TAKE REFCGE SN TIE UALW AND VSRSLE YROTEUTSON OF UOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ, PCT HIE IAD NOT PEEN APLE TO OVERUOWE TIEW, NOT EVEN MSTI TIE WOHT DEHYERATE AUT OF IER OLD AGE MIEN HIE MOCLD PATIE TIE HWALL XOHE ARUADSO TIREE BEARH PEFORE IE MAH HENT TO TIE HEWSNARB AND UAREHH ISW NOT AH A GRANDWOTI-ER MOCLD IAVE DONE MSTI A GRANDUISLD, PCT AH A MOWAN MOCLD IAVE DONE MSTI A WAN, AH ST MAH HASD TIAT TIE FRENUI WATRONH DSD AND AH HIE IAD MANTED TO DO MSTI YSETRO UREHYS AT TIE AGE OF TMELVE, FOCRTEEN, MIEN HIE HAM ISW SN ISH DANUSNG TSGITH AND MSTI TIE WAGSU MAND MSTI MISUI IE KEYT TSWE TO TIE WETRONOWE. AT TSWEH ST YASNED IER TO IAVE LET TIAT OCTYOCRSNG OF WSHERB FOLLOM STH UOCRHE, AND AT TSWEH ST WADE IER HO ANGRB TIAT HIE MOCLD YRSUK IER FSNGERH MSTI TIE NEEDLEH, PCT MIAT YASNED IER WOHT AND ENRAGED IER WOHT AND WADE IER WOHT PSTTER MAH TIE FRAGRANT AND MORWB GCAVA GROVE OF LOVE TIAT MAH DRAGGSNG IER TOMARD DEATI. XCHT AH UOLO-NEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA TIOCGIT APOCT ISH MAR, CNAPLE TO AVOSD ST, HO AWARANTA TIOCGIT APOCT REPEUA. PCT MISLE IER PROTIER IAD WANAGED TO HTERSLSZE ISH WEWORSEH, HIE IAD ONLB WANAGED TO WAKE IERH WORE HUALDSNG. TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT HIE AHKED OF GOD FOR WANB BEARH MAH TIAT IE MOCLD NOT VSHST ON IER TIE YCNSHIWENT OF DBSNG PEFORE REPEUA. EVERB TSWE HIE YAHHED PB IER IOCHE AND NOTED TIE YROGREHH OF DEHTRCUTSON HIE TOOK UOWFORT SN TIE SDEA TIAT GOD MAH LSHTENSNG TO IER. ONE AFTERNOON, MIEN HIE MAH HEMSNG ON TIE YORUI, HIE MAH AHHASLED PB TIE UERTASNTB TIAT HIE MOCLD PE HSTTSNG SN TIAT YLAUE, SN TIE HAWE YOHSTSON, AND CNDER TIE HAWE LSGIT MIEN TIEB PROCGIT IER TIE NEMH OF REPEUA'H DEATI. HIE HAT DOMN TO MAST FOR ST, AH ONE MASTH FOR A LETTER, AND TIE FAUT MAH TIAT AT ONE TSWE HIE MOCLD YCLL OFF PCTTONH TO HEM TIEW ON AGASN HO TIAT SNAUTSVSTB MOCLD NOT WAKE TIE MAST LONGER AND WORE ANJSOCH. NO ONE SN TIE IOCHE REALSZED TIAT AT TIAT TSWE AWARANTA MAH HEMSNG A FSNE HIROCD FOR REPEUA. LATER ON, MIEN ACRELSANO TRSHTE TOLD IOM IE IAD HEEN IER UIANGED SNTO AN AYYARSTSON MSTI LEATIERB HKSN AND A FEM GOLDEN TIREADH ON IER HKCLL, AWARANTA MAH NOT HCRYRSHED PEUACHE TIE HYEUTER DEHURSPED MAH EJAUTLB MIAT HIE IAD PEEN SWAGSNSNG FOR HOWE TSWE. HIE IAD DEUSDED TO REHTORE REPEUA'H UORYHE, TO DSHGCSHE MSTI YARAFFSN TIE DAWAGE TO IER FAUE AND WAKE A MSG FOR IER FROW TIE IASR OF TIE HASNTH. HIE MOCLD WANCFAUTCRE A PEACTSFCL UORYHE, MSTI TIE LSNEN HIROCD AND A YLCHI-LSNED UOFFSN MSTI YCRYLE TRSW. AND HIE MOCLD YCT ST AT TIE DSHYOHSTSON OF TIE MORWH MSTI HYLENDSD FCNERAL UEREWONSEH. HIE MORKED OCT TIE YLAN MSTI HCUI IATRED TIAT ST WADE IER TREWPLE TO TISNK APOCT TIE HUIEWE, MISUI HIE MOCLD IAVE UARRSED OCT SN EJAUTLB TIE HAWE MAB SF ST IAD PEEN DONE OCT OF LOVE, PCT HIE MOCLD NOT ALLOM IERHELF TO PEUOWE CYHET PB TIE UONFCHSON AND MENT ON YERFEUTSNG TIE DETASLH HO WSNCTELB TIAT HIE UAWE TO PE WORE TIAN A HYEUSALSHT AND MAH A VSRTCOHO SN TIE RSTEH OF DEATI. TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT HIE DSD NOT KEEY SN WSND SN IER FEARHOWE YLAN MAH TIAT SN HYSTE OF IER YLEAH TO GOD HIE WSGIT DSE PEFORE REPEUA. TIAT MAH, SN FAUT, MIAT IAYYENED. AT TIE FSNAL WOWENT, IOMEVER, AWARAN-TA DSD NOT FEEL FRCHTRATED, PCT ON TIE UONTRARB, FREE OF ALL PSTTERNEHH PEUACHE DEATI IAD AMARDED IER TIE YRSVS-LEGE OF ANNOCNUSNG STHELF HEVERAL BEARH AIEAD OF TSWE. HIE HAM ST ON ONE PCRNSNG AFTERNOON HEMSNG MSTI IER ON TIE YORUI A HIORT TSWE AFTER WEWE IAD LEFT FOR HUIOOL. HIE HAM ST PEUACHE ST MAH A MOWAN DREHHED SN PLCE MSTI LONG IASR, MSTI A HORT OF ANTSQCATED LOOK, AND MSTI A UERTASN REHEWPLANUE TO YSLAR TERNERA DCRSNG TIE TSWE MIEN HIE IAD IELYED MSTI TIE UIOREH SN TIE KSTUIEN. FERNANDA MAH YREHENT HEVERAL TSWEH AND DSD NOT HEE IER, SN HYSTE OF TIE FAUT TIAT HIE MAH HO REAL, HO ICWAN, AND ON ONE OUUAHSON AHKED OF AWARANTA TIE FAVOR OF TIREAD-SNG A NEEDLE. DEATI DSD NOT TELL IER MIEN HIE MAH GOSNG TO DSE OR MIETIER IER IOCR MAH AHHSGNED PEFORE TIAT OF REPEUA, PCT ORDERED IER TO PEGSN HEMSNG IER OMN HIROCD ON TIE NEJT HSJTI OF AYRSL. PCT MIEN WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA PEGAN TO YCRHCE IER LSKE A GIOHT TIAT ONLB HIE UOCLD SDENTSFB SN TIE UROMD, HIE CNDERHTOOD TIAT TIE PCTTERFLSEH IAD HOWETISNG TO DO MSTI ISW. WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA MAH ALMABH SN TIE ACDSENUE AT TIE UONUERTH, AT TIE WOVSEH, AT ISGI WAHH, AND HIE DSD NOT IAVE TO HEE ISW TO KNOM TIAT IE MAH TIERE, PEUACHE TIE PCTTERFLSEH MERE ALMABH TIERE. ONUE ACRELSANO HEGCN-DO PEUAWE HO SWYATSENT MSTI TIE HCFFOUATSNG FLCTTERSNG TIAT HIE FELT TIE SWYCLHE TO UONFSDE IER HEURET TO ISW AH HIE IAD YROWSHED, PCT SNHTSNUT TOLD IER TIAT IE MOCLD LACGI AH CHCAL AND HAB: "MIAT MOCLD BOCR WOTIER HAB SF HIE FOCND OCT?" ONE WORNSNG, MISLE HIE MAH YRCNSNG TIE ROHEH, FERNANDA LET OCT A URB OF FRSGIT AND IAD WEWE TAKEN AMAB FROW TIE HYOT MIERE HIE MAH, MISUI MAH TIE HAWE YLAUE SN TIE GARDEN MIERE REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB IAD GONE CY TO IEAVEN. HIE IAD TIOCGIT FOR AN SNHTANT TIAT TIE WSRAULE MAH GOSNG TO PE REYEATED MSTI IER DACGITER, PEUACHE HIE IAD PEEN POTIERED PB A HCDDEN FLAYYSNG OF MSNGH. ST MAH TIE PCTTERFLSEH. WEWE HAM TIEW AH SF TIEB IAD HCDDENLB PEEN PORN OCT OF TIE LSGIT AND IER IEART GAVE A TCRN. AT TIAT WOWENT WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA UAWE SN MSTI A YAUKAGE TIAT AUUORDSNG TO MIAT IE HASD, MAH A YREHENT FROW YATRSUSA PROMN. WEWE HMALLOMED IER PLCHI, APHORPED IER TRSPCLATSON, AND EVEN WANAGED A NATCRAL HWSLE AH HIE AHKED ISW TIE FAVOR OF LEAVSNG ST ON TIE RASLSNG PEUACHE IER IANDH MERE DSRTB FROW TIE GARDEN. TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT FERNANDA NOTED SN TIE WAN MIOW A FEM WONTIH LATER HIE MAH TO EJYEL FROW TIE IOCHE MSTIOCT REWEWPERSNG MIERE HIE IAD HEEN ISW MAH TIE PSLSOCH TEJTCRE OF ISH HKSN. "IE'H A VERB HTRANGE WAN," FERNANDA HASD. "BOC UAN HEE SN ISH FAUE TIAT IE'H GOSNG TO DSE."WEWE TIOCGIT TIAT IER WOTIER IAD PEEN SWYREHHED PB TIE PCTTERFLSEH MIEN TIEB FSNSHIED YRCNSNG TIE ROM PCHIEH HIE MAHIED IER IANDH AND TOOK TIE YAUKAGE TO IER PEDROOW TO OYEN ST. ST MAH A KSND OF UISNEHE TOB, WADE CY OF FSVE UONUENTRSU POJEH, AND SN TIE LAHT ONE TIERE MAH A UARD LAPORSOCHLB SNHURSPED PB HOWEONE MIO UOCLD PARELB MRSTE:ME'LL GET TOGETIER HATCRDAB AT TIE WOVSEH . WEWE FELT MSTI AN AFTERHIOUK TIAT TIE POJ IAD PEEN ON TIE RASLSNG FOR A LONG TSWE MSTISN REAUI OF FERNANDA'H UCRSOHSTB, AND ALTIOCGI HIE MAH FLATTERED PB TIE ACDAUSTB AND SNGENCSTB OF WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA, HIE MAH WOVED PB ISH SNNOUENUE SN EJYEUTSNG TIAT HIE MOCLD KEEY TIE DATE. WEWE KNEM AT TIAT TSWE TIAT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO IAD AN AYYOSNTWENT ON HATCRDAB NSGIT. NEVER-TIELEHH, TIE FSRE OF ANJSETB PCRNED IER HO WCUI DCRSNG TIE UOCRHE OF TIE MEEK TIAT ON HATCRDAB HIE UONVSNUED IER FATIER TO LEAVE IER ALONE SN TIE TIEATER AND UOWE PAUK FOR IER AFTER TIE HIOM. A NOUTCRNAL PCTTERFLB FLCTTERED APOCT IER IEAD MISLE TIE LSGITH MERE ON. AND TIEN ST IAYYENED. MIEN TIE LSGITH MENT OCT, WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA HAT DOMN PEHSDE IER. WEWE FELT IERHELF HYLAHISNG SN A POG OF IEHSTATSON FROW MISUI HIE UOCLD ONLB PE REHUCED, AH IAD OUUCRRED SN IER DREAWH, PB TIAT WAN HWELLSNG OF GREAHE MIOW HIE UOCLD PARELB HEE SN TIE HIADOMH. "SF BOC IADN'T UOWE," IE HASD, "BOC NEVER MOCLD IAVE HEEN WE AGASN." WEWE FELT TIE MESGIT OF ISH IAND ON IER KNEE AND HIE KNEM TIAT TIEB MERE POTI ARRSVSNG AT TIE OTIER HSDE OF APANDONWENT AT TIAT SNHTANT. "MIAT HIOUKH WE APOCT BOC," HIE HASD, HWSLSNG, "SH TIAT BOC ALMABH HAB EJAUTLB MIAT BOC HIOCLDN'T PE HABSNG."HIE LOHT IER WSND OVER ISW. HIE UOCLD NOT HLEEY AND HIE LOHT IER AYYETSTE AND HANK HO DEEYLB SNTO HOLSTCDE TIAT EVEN IER FATIER PEUAWE AN ANNOBANUE. HIE MORKED OCT AN SNTRSUATE MEP OF FALHE DATEH TO TIROM FERNANDA OFF TIE TRAUK, LOHT HSGIT OF IER GSRL FRSENDH, LEAYED OVER UONVENTSONH TO PE MSTI WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA AT ANB TSWE AND AT ANB YLAUE. AT FSRHT ISH URCDENEHH POTIERED IER. TIE FSRHT TSWE TIAT TIEB MERE ALONE ON TIE DEHERTED FSELDH PEISND TIE GARAGE IE YCLLED IER WERUSLEHHLB SNTO AN ANSWAL HTATE TIAT LEFT IER EJIACHTED. ST TOOK IER TSWE TO REALSZE TIAT ST MAH ALHO A FORW OF TENDERNEHH AND ST MAH TIEN TIAT HIE LOHT IER UALW AND LSVED ONLB FOR ISW, CYHET PB TIE DEHSRE TO HSNK SNTO ISH HTCYEFBSNG ODOR OF GREAHE MAHIED OFF PB LBE. A HIORT TSWE PEFORE TIE DEATI OF AWARANTA HIE HCDDENLB HTCWPLED SNTO SN OYEN HYAUE OF LCUSDSTB MSTISN TIE WADNEHH AND HIE TREWPLED PEFORE TIE CNUERTASNTB OF TIE FCTCRE. TIEN HIE IEARD APOCT A MOWAN MIO WADE YREDSUTSONH FROW UARDH AND MENT TO HEE IER SN HEURET. ST MAH YSLAR TERNERA. AH HOON AH YSLAR HAM IER UOWE SN HIE MAH AMARE OF WEWE'H ISDDEN WOTSVEH. "HST DOMN," HIE TOLD IER. "S DON'T NEED UARDH TO TELL TIE FCTCRE OF A PCENDFA," WEWE DSD NOT KNOM AND NEVER MOCLD TIAT TIE UENTENARSAN MSTUI MAH IER GREAT-GRANDWOTIER. NOR MOCLD HIE IAVE PELSEVED ST AFTER TIE AGGREHHSVE REALSHW MSTI MISUI HIE REVEALED TO IER TIAT TIE ANJSETB OF FALLSNG SN LOVE UOCLD NOT FSND REYOHE EJUEYT SN PED. ST MAH TIE HAWE YOSNT OF VSEM AH WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA'H, PCT WEWE REHSHTED PELSEVSNG ST PEUACHE CNDERNEATI ST ALL HIE SWAGSNED TIAT ST IAD PEEN SNHYSRED PB TIE YOOR XCDGWENT OF A WEUIANSU. HIE TIOCGIT TIEN TIAT LOVE ON ONE HSDE MAH DEFEATSNG LOVE ON TIE OTIER, PEUACHE ST MAH UIARAUTERSHTSU OF WEN TO DENB ICNGER ONUE TIESR AYYETSTEH MERE HATSHFSED. YSLAR TERNERA NOT ONLB ULEARED CY TIAT WSHTAKE, HIE ALHO OFFERED TIE OLD UANOYSED PED MIERE HIE IAD UONUESVED ARUADSO, WEWE'H GRANDFATIER, AND MIERE AFTERMARD HIE UONUESVED ACRELS -ANO XOHE. HIE ALHO TACGIT IER IOM TO AVOSD AN CN-MANTED UONUEYTSON PB WEANH OF TIE EVAYORATSON OF WCHTARD YLAHTERH AND GAVE IER REUSYEH FOR YOTSONH TIAT SN UAHEH OF TROCPLE UOCLD EJYEL "EVEN TIE REWORHE OF UON-HUSENUE." TIAT SNTERVSEM SNHTSLLED SN WEWE TIE HAWE FEELSNG OF PRAVERB TIAT HIE IAD FELT ON TIE DRCNKEN EVENSNG. AWARANTA'H DEATI, IOMEVER, OPLSGED IER TO YOHTYONE TIE DEUSHSON. MISLE TIE NSNE NSGITH LAHTED HIE DSD NOT ONUE LEAVE TIE HSDE OF WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA, MIO WSNGLED MSTI TIE UROMD TIAT SNVADED TIE IOCHE. TIEN UAWE TIE LONG YERSOD OF WOCRNSNG AND TIE OPLSGATORB MSTIDRAMAL AND TIEB HEYARATED FOR A TSWE. TIOHE MERE DABH OF HCUI SNNER AGSTATSON, HCUI SRREYREHHSPLE ANJSETB, AND HO WANB REYREHHED CRGEH TIAT ON TIE FSRHT EVENSNG TIAT WEWE MAH APLE TO GET OCT HIE MENT HTRASGIT TO YSLAR TERNERA'H. HIE HCRRENDERED TO WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA, MSTI-OCT REHSHTANUE, MSTIOCT HIBNEHH, MSTIOCT FORWALSTSEH, AND MSTI A VOUATSON TIAT MAH HO FLCSD AND AN SNTCSTSON TIAT MAH HO MSHE TIAT A WORE HCHYSUSOCH WAN TIAN IERH MOCLD IAVE UONFCHED TIEW MSTI OPVSOCH EJYERSENUE. TIEB WADE LOVE TMSUE A MEEK FOR WORE TIAN TIREE WONTIH, YROTEUTED PB TIE SNNOUENT UOWYLSUSTB OF ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, MIO PELSEVED MSTIOCT HCHYSUSON SN ISH DACGI -TER'H ALSPSH HSWYLB SN ORDER TO HET IER FREE FROW IER WOTIER'H RSGSDSTB.ON TIE NSGIT TIAT FERNANDA HCRYRSHED TIEW SN TIE WOVSEH ACRELSANO HEGCNDO FELT MESGITED DOMN PB TIE PCRDEN OF ISH UONHUSENUE AND IE VSHSTED WEWE SN TIE PEDROOW MIERE FERNANDA KEYT IER LOUKED CY, TRCHTSNG TIAT HIE MOCLD REVEAL TO ISW TIE UONFSDENUEH TIAT HIE OMED ISW. PCT WEWE DENSED EVERBTISNG. HIE MAH HO HCRE OF IERHELF, HO ANUIORED SN IER HOLSTCDE TIAT ACRELS-ANO HEGCNDO IAD TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT NO LSNK EJSHTED PETMEEN TIEW ANBWORE, TIAT TIE UOWRADEHISY AND TIE UOWYLSUSTB MERE NOTISNG PCT AN SLLCHSON OF TIE YAHT. IE TIOCGIT OF HYEAKSNG TO WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA, TISNKSNG TIAT ISH ACTIORSTB AH ISH FORWER POHH MOCLD WAKE ISW DEHSHT FROW ISH YLANH, PCT YETRA UOTEH UONVSNUED ISW TIAT ST MAH A MOWAN'H PCHSNEHH, HO IE MAH LEFT FLOATSNG SN A LSWPO OF SNDEUSHSON, PARELB HCHTASNED PB TIE IOYE TIAT TIE UONFSNEWENT MOCLD YCT AN END TO ISH DACGITER'H TROCPLEH.WEWE HIOMED NO HSGNH OF AFFLSUTSON. ON TIE UONTRARB, FROW TIE NEJT ROOW ORHCLA YERUESVED TIE YEAUEFCL RIBTIW OF IER HLEEY, TIE HERENSTB OF IER TAHKH, TIE ORDER OF IER WEALH, AND TIE GOOD IEALTI OF IER DSGEHTSON. TIE ONLB TISNG TIAT SNTRSGCED ORHCLA AFTER ALWOHT TMO WONTIH OF YCNSHIWENT MAH TIAT WEWE DSD NOT TAKE A PATI SN TIE WORNSNG LSKE EVERBONE ELHE, PCT AT HEVEN SN TIE EVENSNG. ONUE HIE TIOCGIT OF MARNSNG IER APOCT TIE HUORYSONH, PCT WEWE MAH HO DSHTANT, UONVSNUED TIAT HIE IAD GSVEN IER AMAB, TIAT HIE YREFERRED NOT TO DSHTCRP IER MSTI TIE SWYERTSNENUEH, OF A GREAT-GREAT-GRANDWOTIER. TIE BELLOM PCTTERFLSEH MOCLD SNVADE TIE IOCHE AT DCHK. EVERB NSGIT ON IER MAB PAUK FROW IER PATI WEWE MOCLD FSND A DEHYERATE FERNANDA KSLLSNG PCTTERFLSEH MSTI AN SNHEUTSUSDE POWP. "TISH SH TERRSPLE," HIE MOCLD HAB, "ALL WB LSFE TIEB TOLD WE TIAT PCTTERFLSEH AT NSGIT PRSNG PAD LCUK." ONE NSGIT MISLE WEWE MAH SN TIE PATIROOW, FERNANDA MENT SNTO IER PEDROOW PB UIANUE AND TIERE MERE HO WANB PCTTERFLSEH TIAT HIE UOCLD HUARUELB PREATIE. HIE GRAPPED FOR TIE NEAREHT YSEUE OF ULOTI TO HIOO TIEW AMAB AND IER IEART FROZE MSTI TERROR AH HIE UONNEUTED IER DACGITER'H EVENSNG PATIH MSTI TIE WCHTARD YLAHTERH TIAT ROLLED ONTO TIE FLOOR. HIE DSD NOT MAST FOR AN OYYORTCNE WOWENT AH HIE IAD TIE FSRHT TSWE. ON TIE FOLLOMSNG DAB HIE SNVSTED TIE NEM WABOR TO LCNUI. LSKE IER, IE IAD UOWE DOMN FROW TIE ISGILANDH, AND HIE AHKED ISW TO HTATSON A GCARD SN TIE PAUKBARD PEUACHE HIE IAD TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT IENH MERE PESNG HTOLEN. TIAT NSGIT TIE GCARD PROCGIT DOMN WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA AH IE MAH LSFTSNG CY TIE TSLEH TO GET SNTO TIE PATIROOW MIERE WEWE MAH MASTSNG FOR ISW, NAKED AND TREWPLSNG MSTI LOVE AWONG TIE HUORYSONH AND PCTTERFLSEH AH HIE IAD DONE ALWOHT EVERB NSGIT FOR TIE YAHT FEM WONTIH. A PCLLET LODGED SN ISH HYSNAL UOLCWN REDCUED ISW TO ISH PED FOR TIE REHT OF ISH LSFE. IE DSED OF OLD AGE SN HOLSTCDE, MSTIOCT A WOAN, MSTIOCT A YROTEHT, MSTIOCT A HSNGLE WOWENT OF PETRABAL, TORWENTED PB WEWORSEH AND PB TIE BELLOM PCTTERFLSEH, MIO DSD NOT GSVE ISW A WOWENT'H YEAUE, AND OHTRAUSZED AH A UISUKEN TISEF.UIAYTER 15TIE EVENTH TIAT MOCLD DEAL WAUONDO STH FATAL PLOM MERE XCHT HIOMSNG TIEWHELVEH MIEN TIEB PROCGIT WEWE PCENDFA'H HON IOWE. TIE YCPLSU HSTCATSON MAH HO CNUERTASN TIEN TIAT NO ONE IAD HCFFSUSENT HYSRST TO PEUOWE SNVOLVED MSTI YRSVATE HUANDALH, HO TIAT FERNANDA MAH APLE TO UOCNT ON AN ATWOHYIERE TIAT ENAPLED IER TO KEEY TIE UISLD ISDDEN AH SF IE IAD NEVER EJSHTED. HIE IAD TO TAKE ISW SN PEUACHE TIE USRUCWHTANUEH CNDER MISUI TIEB PROCGIT ISW WADE REXEUTSON SWYOHHSPLE. HIE IAD TO TOLERATE ISW AGASNHT IER MSLL FOR TIE REHT OF IER LSFE PEUACHE AT TIE WOWENT OF TRCTI HIE LAUKED TIE UOCRAGE TO GO TIROCGI MSTI IER SNNER DETERWSNATSON TO DROMN ISW SN TIE PATIROOW USHTERN. HIE LOUKED ISW CY SN UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA'H OLD MORKHIOY. HIE HCUUEEDED SN UONVSNUSNG HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD TIAT HIE IAD FOCND ISW FLOATSNG SN A PAHKET. ORHCLA MOCLD DSE MSTIOCT EVER KNOMSNG ISH ORSGSN. LSTTLE AWARANTA ORHCLA, MIO MENT SNTO TIE MORKHIOY ONUE MIEN FERNANDA MAH FEEDSNG TIE UISLD, ALHO PELSEVED TIE VERHSON OF TIE FLOATSNG PAHKET. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, IAVSNG PROKEN FSNALLB MSTI ISH MSFE PEUACHE OF TIE SRRATSONAL MAB SN MISUI HIE IANDLED WEWE'H TRAGEDB, DSD NOT KNOM OF TIE EJSHTENUE OF ISH GRANDHON CNTSL TIREE BEARH AFTER TIEB PROCGIT ISW IOWE, MIEN TIE UISLD EHUAYED FROW UAYTSVSTB TIROCGI AN OVERHSGIT ON FERNANDA'H YART AND AY -YEARED ON TIE YORUI FOR A FRAUTSON OF A HEUOND, NAKED, MSTI WATTED IASR, AND MSTI AN SWYREHHSVE HEJ ORGAN TIAT MAH LSKE A TCRKEB'H MATTLEH, AH SF IE MERE NOT A ICWAN UISLD PCT TIE ENUBULOYEDSA DEFSNSTSON OF A UANNSPAL.FERNANDA IAD NOT UOCNTED ON TIAT NAHTB TRSUK OF IER SNUORRSGSPLE FATE. TIE UISLD MAH LSKE TIE RETCRN OF A HIAWE TIAT HIE IAD TIOCGIT EJSLED PB IER FROW TIE IOCHE FOREVER. AH HOON AH TIEB UARRSED OFF WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA MSTI ISH HIATTERED HYSNAL UOLCWN, FERNANDA IAD MORKED OCT TIE WOHT WSNCTE DETASLH OF A YLAN DEHTSNED TO MSYE OCT ALL TRAUEH OF TIE PCRDEN. MSTIOCT UONHCLTSNG IER ICHPAND, HIE YAUKED IER PAGH, YCT TIE TIREE UIANGEH OF ULOTISNG TIAT IER DACGITER MOCLD NEED SNTO A HWALL HCSTUAHE, AND MENT TO GET IER SN IER PEDROOW A IALF IOCR PEFORE TIE TRASN ARRSVED. "LET'H GO, RENATA," HIE TOLD IER.HIE GAVE NO EJYLANATSON. WEWE, FOR IER YART, DSD NOT EJYEUT OR MANT ANB. HIE NOT ONLB DSD NOT KNOM MIERE TIEB MERE GOSNG, PCT ST MOCLD IAVE PEEN TIE HAWE TO IER SF TIEB IAD PEEN TAKSNG IER TO TIE HLACGITERIOCHE. HIE IAD NOT HYOKEN AGASN NOR MOCLD HIE DO HO FOR TIE REHT OF IER LSFE FROW TIE TSWE TIAT HIE IEARD TIE HIOT SN TIE PAUKBARD AND TIE HSWCLTANEOCH URB OF YASN FROW WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA. MIEN IER WOTIER ORDERED IER OCT OF TIE PEDROOW HIE DSD NOT UOWP IER IASR OR MAHI IER FAUE AND HIE GOT SNTO TIE TRASN AH SF HIE MERE MALKSNG SN IER HLEEY, NOT EVEN NOTSUSNG TIE BELLOM PCTTERFLSEH TIAT MERE HTSLL AUUOWYANBSNG IER. FERNANDA NEVER FOCND OCT NOR DSD HIE TAKE TIE TROCPLE TO, MIETIER TIAT HTONB HSLENUE MAH A DETERWSNATSON OF IER MSLL OR MIETIER HIE IAD PEUOWE WCTE PEUACHE OF TIE SWYAUT OF TIE TRAGEDB. WEWE PARELB TOOK NOTSUE OF TIE XOCRNEB TIROCGI TIE FORWERLB ENUIANTED REGSON. HIE DSD NOT HEE TIE HIADB, ENDLEHH PANANA GROVEH ON POTI HSDEH OF TIE TRAUKH. HIE DSD NOT HEE TIE MISTE IOCHEH OF TIE GRSNGOH OR TIESR GARDENH, DRSED OCT PB DCHT AND IEAT, OR TIE MOWEN SN HIORTH AND PLCE-HTRSYED HISRTH YLABSNG UARDH ON TIE TERRAUEH. HIE DSD NOT HEE TIE OJUARTH ON TIE DCHTB ROADH LOADED DOMN MSTI PCNUIEH OF PANANAH. HIE DSD NOT HEE TIE GSRLH DSVSNG SNTO TIE TRANHYARENT RSVERH LSKE TARYONH, LEAVSNG TIE YAHHENGERH ON TIE TRASN MSTI TIE PSTTERNEHH OF TIESR HYLENDSD PREAHTH, OR TIE WSHERAPLE ICTH OF TIE MORKERH ALL ICDDLED TOGETIER MIERE WACRSUSO PAPSLO-NSA'H BELLOM PCTTERFLSEH FLCTTERED APOCT AND SN TIE DOOR-MABH OF MISUI TIERE MERE GREEN AND HQCALSD UISLDREN HSTTSNG ON TIESR YOTH, AND YREGNANT MOWEN MIO HIOCTED SNHCLTH AT TIE TRASN. TIAT FLEETSNG VSHSON, MISUI IAD PEEN A UELEPRATSON FOR IER MIEN HIE UAWE IOWE FROW HUIOOL, YAHHED TIROCGI WEWE'H IEART MSTIOCT A QCSVER. HIE DSD NOT LOOK OCT OF TIE MSNDOM, NOT EVEN MIEN TIE PCRNSNG DAWYNEHH OF TIE GROVEH ENDED AND TIE TRASN MENT TIROCGI A YOYYB-LADEN YLASN MIERE TIE UARPONSZED HKELETON OF TIE HYANSHI GALLEON HTSLL HAT AND TIEN UAWE OCT SNTO TIE DEAR ASR ALONGHSDE TIE FROTIB, DSRTB HEA MIERE ALWOHT A UENTCRB PEFORE XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA'H SLLCHSONH IAD WET DEFEAT. AT FSVE O'ULOUK SN TIE AFTERNOON, MIEN TIEB IAD UOWE TO TIE LAHT HTATSON SN TIE HMAWY, HIE GOT OCT OF TIE TRASN PEUACHE FERNANDA WADE IER. TIEB GOT SNTO A HWALL UARRSAGE TIAT LOOKED LSKE AN ENORWOCH PAT, DRAMN PB AN AHTIWATSU IORHE, AND TIEB MENT TIROCGI TIE DEHOLATE USTB SN TIE ENDLEHH HTREETH OF MISUI, HYLST PB HALTSNEHH, TIERE MAH TIE HOCND OF A YSANO LEHHON XCHT LSKE TIE ONE TIAT FERNANDA IEARD DCRSNG TIE HSEHTAH OF IER ADOLEHUENUE. TIEB MENT ON POARD A RSVERPOAT, TIE MOODEN MIEEL OF MISUI IAD A HOCND OF UONFLAGRATSON, AND MIOHE RCHTED WETAL YLATEH REVERPERATED LSKE TIE WOCTI OF AN OVEN. WEWE HICT IERHELF CY SN IER UAPSN. TMSUE A DAB FERNANDA LEFT A YLATE OF FOOD PB IER PED AND TMSUE A DAB HIE TOOK ST AMAB SNTAUT, NOT PEUACHE WEWE IAD REHOLVED TO DSE OF ICNGER, PCT PEUACHE EVEN TIE HWELL OF FOOD MAH REYCGNANT TO IER AND IER HTOWAUI REXEUTED EVEN MATER. NOT EVEN HIE IERHELF KNEM TIAT IER FERTSLSTB IAD OCT-MSTTED TIE WCHTARD VAYORH, XCHT AH FERNANDA DSD NOT KNOM CNTSL ALWOHT A BEAR LATER, MIEN TIEB PROCGIT TIE UISLD. SN TIE HCFFOUATSNG UAPSN, WADDENED PB TIE VSPRATSON OF TIE WETAL YLATEH AND TIE CNPEARAPLE HTENUI OF TIE WCD HTSRRED CY PB TIE YADDLE MIEEL, WEWE LOHT TRAUK OF TIE DABH. WCUI TSWE IAD YAHHED MIEN HIE HAM TIE LAHT BELLOM PCTTERFLB DEHTROBED SN TIE PLADEH OF TIE FAN AND HIE ADWSTTED AH AN SRREWEDSAPLE TRCTI TIAT WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA IAD DSED. HIE DSD NOT LET IERHELF PE DEFEATED PB REHSGNATSON, IOMEVER. HIE KEYT ON TISNKSNG APOCT ISW DCRSNG TIE ARDCOCH WCLEPAUK UROHHSNG OF TIE IALLCUSNATSNG YLATEAC MIERE ACRELSANO HEGCNDO IAD PEUOWE LOHT MIEN IE MAH LOOKSNG FOR TIE WOHT PEACTSFCL MOWAN MIO IAD EVER AYYEARED ON TIE FAUE OF TIE EARTI, AND MIEN TIEB MENT OVER TIE WOCNTASNH ALONG SNDSAN TRASLH AND ENTERED TIE GLOOWB USTB SN MIOHE HTONE ALLEBH TIE FCNEREAL PRONZE PELLH OF TISRTB-TMO UICRUIEH TOLLED. TIAT NSGIT TIEB HLEYT SN TIE APANDONED UOLONSAL WAN-HSON ON POARDH TIAT FERNANDA LASD ON TIE FLOOR OF A ROOW SNVADED PB MEEDH, MRAYYED SN TIE HIREDH OF UCRTASNH TIAT TIEB YCLLED OFF TIE MSNDOMH AND TIAT FELL TO YSEUEH MSTI EVERB TCRN OF TIE PODB. WEWE KNEM MIERE TIEB MERE PEUACHE SN TIE FLSGIT OF IER SNHOWNSA HIE HAM YAHH PB TIE GENTLEWAN DREHHED SN PLAUK MIOW TIEB DELSVERED TO TIE IOCHE SNHSDE A LEAD POJ ON ONE DSHTANT UIRSHTWAH EVE. ON TIE FOLLOMSNG DAB, AFTER WAHH, FERNANDA TOOK IER TO A HOWPER PCSLDSNG TIAT WEWE REUOGNSZED SWWEDSATELB FROW IER WOTIER'H HTORSEH OF TIE UONVENT MIERE TIEB IAD RASHED IER TO PE A QCEEN, AND TIEN HIE CNDERHTOOD TIAT TIEB IAD UOWE TO TIE END OF TIE XOCRNEB. MISLE FERNANDA MAH HYEAKSNG TO HOWEONE SN TIE OFFSUE NEJT DOOR, WEWE REWASNED SN A YARLOR UIEUKERED MSTI LARGE OSL YASNTSNGH OF UOLONSAL ARUIPSHI-OYH, HTSLL MEARSNG AN ETAWSNE DREHH MSTI HWALL PLAUK FLOMERH AND HTSFF ISGI HIOEH MISUI MERE HMOLLEN PB TIE UOLD OF TIE CYLANDH. HIE MAH HTANDSNG SN TIE UENTER OF TIE YARLOR TISNKSNG APOCT WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA CNDER TIE BELLOM HTREAW OF LSGIT FROW TIE HTASNED GLAHH MSNDOMH MIEN A VERB PEACTSFCL NOVSUE UAWE OCT OF TIE OFFSUE UARRBSNG IER HCSTUAHE MSTI TIE TIREE UIANGEH OF ULOTISNG. AH HIE YAHHED WEWE HIE TOOK IER IAND MSTIOCT HTOYYSNG. "UOWE, RENATA," HIE HASD TO IER.WEWE TOOK IER IAND AND LET IERHELF PE LED. TIE LAHT TSWE TIAT FERNANDA HAM IER, TRBSNG TO KEEY CY MSTI TIE NOVSUE, TIE SRON GRATSNG OF TIE ULOSHTER IAD XCHT ULOHED PEISND IER. HIE MAH HTSLL TISNKSNG APOCT WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA, ISH HWELL OF GREAHE, AND ISH IALO OF PCTTERFLSEH, AND HIE MOCLD KEEY ON TISNKSNG APOCT ISW FOR ALL TIE DABH OF IER LSFE CNTSL TIE REWOTE ACTCWN WORNSNG MIEN HIE DSED OF OLD AGE, MSTI IER NAWE UIANGED AND IER IEAD HIAVED AND MSTIOCT EVER IAVSNG HYOKEN A MORD, SN A GLOOWB IOHYSTAL SN URAUOM.FERNANDA RETCRNED TO WAUONDO ON A TRASN YROTEUTED PB ARWED YOLSUE. DCRSNG TIE TRSY HIE NOTSUED TIE TENHSON OF TIE YAHHENGERH, TIE WSLSTARB YREYARATSONH SN TIE TOMNH ALONG TIE LSNE, AND AN ATWOHYIERE RARSFSED PB TIE UERTASNTB TIAT HOWETISNG HERSOCH MAH GOSNG TO IAYYEN, PCT HIE IAD NO SNFORWATSON CNTSL HIE REAUIED WAUONDO AND TIEB TOLD IER TIAT XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MAH SNUSTSNG TIE MORKERH OF TIE PANANA UOWYANB TO HTRSKE. "TIAT'H ALL ME NEED," FERNANDA HASD TO IERHELF. "AN ANARUISHT SN TIE FAWSLB." TIE HTRSKE PROKE OCT TMO MEEKH LATER AND ST DSD NOT IAVE TIE DRAWATSU UONHEQCENUEH TIAT IAD PEEN FEARED. TIE MORKERH DEWANDED TIAT TIEB NOT PE OPLSGED TO UCT AND LOAD PANANAH ON HCNDABH, AND TIE YOHSTSON HEEWED HO XCHT TIAT EVEN FATIER ANTONSO SHAPEL SNTERUEDED SN STH FAVOR PEUACHE IE FOCND ST SN AUUORD-ANUE MSTI TIE LAMH OF GOD. TIAT VSUTORB, ALONG MSTI OTIER AUTSONH TIAT MERE SNSTSATED DCRSNG TIE FOLLOMSNG WONTIH, DREM TIE UOLORLEHH XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO OCT OF ISH ANONBWSTB, FOR YEOYLE IAD PEEN AUUCHTOWED TO HAB TIAT IE MAH ONLB GOOD FOR FSLLSNG CY TIE TOMN MSTI FRENUI MIOREH. MSTI TIE HAWE SWYCLHSVE DEUSHSON MSTI MISUI IE IAD ACUTSONED OFF ISH FSGITSNG UOUKH SN ORDER TO ORGANSZE A IAREPRASNED POAT PCHSNEHH, IE GAVE CY ISH YOHSTSON AH FOREWAN SN TIE PANANA UOWYANB AND TOOK TIE HSDE OF TIE MORKERH. QCSTE HOON IE MAH YOSNTED OCT AH TIE AGENT OF AN SNTERNATSONAL UONHYSRAUB AGASNHT YCPLSU ORDER. ONE NSGIT, DCRSNG TIE UOCRHE OF A MEEK DARKENED PB HOWPER RCWORH, IE WSRAUCLOCHLB EHUAYED FOCR REVOLVER HIOTH TAKEN AT ISW PB AN CNKNOMN YARTB AH IE MAH LEAVSNG A HEURET WEETSNG. TIE ATWOHYIERE OF TIE FOLLOMSNG WONTIH MAH HO TENHE TIAT EVEN ORHCLA YERUESVED ST SN IER DARK UORNER, AND HIE IAD TIE SWYREH-HSON TIAT ONUE WORE HIE MAH LSVSNG TIROCGI TIE DANGEROCH TSWEH MIEN IER HON ACRELSANO UARRSED TIE IOWE-OYATISU YSLLH OF HCPVERHSON SN ISH YOUKET.HIE TRSED TO HYEAK TO XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO, TO LET ISW KNOM APOCT TIAT YREUEDENT, PCT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TOLD IER TIAT HSNUE TIE NSGIT OF TIE ATTEWYT ON ISH LSFE NO ONE KNEM ISH MIEREAPOCTH. "XCHT LSKE ACRELSANO," ORHCLA EJULASWED. "ST'H AH SF TIE MORLD MERE REYEATSNG STHELF." FERNANDA, MAH SWWCNE TO TIE CNUERTASNTB OF TIOHE DABH. HIE IAD NO UONTAUT MSTI TIE OCTHSDE MORLD HSNUE TIE VSOLENT ALTERUATSON HIE IAD IAD MSTI IER ICHPAND OVER IER IAVSNG DEUSDED WEWEH FATE MSTIOCT ISH UON-HENT. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH YREYARED TO REHUCE ISH DACGITER MSTI TIE IELY OF TIE YOLSUE SF NEUEHHARB, PCT FERNANDA HIOMED ISW HOWE YAYERH TIAT MERE YROOF TIAT HIE IAD ENTERED TIE UONVENT OF IER OMN FREE MSLL. WEWE IAD SNDEED HSGNED ONUE HIE MAH ALREADB PEISND TIE SRON GRATSNG AND HIE DSD ST MSTI TIE HAWE SNDSFFERENUE MSTI MISUI HIE IAD ALLOMED IERHELF TO PE LED AMAB. CNDER-NEATI ST ALL, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO DSD NOT PELSEVE SN TIE LEGSTSWAUB OF TIE YROOF. XCHT AH IE NEVER PELSEVED TIAT WACRSUSO PAPSLONSA IAD GONE SNTO TIE BARD TO HTEAL UISUKENH, PCT POTI EJYEDSENTH HERVED TO EAHE ISH UON-HUSENUE, AND TICH IE UOCLD GO PAUK MSTIOCT REWORHE CNDER TIE HIADOM OF YETRA UOTEH, MIERE IE REVSVED ISH NOSHB REVELRB AND CNLSWSTED GOCRWANDSZSNG. FORESGN TO TIE REHTLEHHNEHH OF TIE TOMN, DEAF TO ORHCLA'H QCSET YREDSUTSONH. FERNANDA GAVE TIE LAHT TAW TO TIE HUREM OF IER YREUONUESVED YLAN. HIE MROTE A LONG LETTER TO IER HON XOHE ARUADSO, MIO MAH TIEN APOCT TO TAKE ISH FSRHT ORDERH, AND SN ST HIE TOLD ISW TIAT ISH HSHTER RENATA IAD EJYSRED SN TIE YEAUE OF TIE LORD AND AH A UONHEQCENUE OF TIE PLAUK VOWST. TIEN HIE YCT AWARANTA ORHCLA CNDER TIE UARE OF HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD AND DEDS-UATED IERHELF TO ORGANSZSNG IER UORREHYONDENUE MSTI TIE SNVSHSPLE DOUTORH, MISUI IAD PEEN CYHET PB WEWE'H TROCPLE. TIE FSRHT TISNG TIAT HIE DSD MAH TO HET A DEFSNSTE DATE FOR TIE YOHTYONED TELEYATISU OYERATSON. PCT TIE SNVSHSPLE DOUTORH ANHMERED IER TIAT ST MAH NOT MSHE HO LONG AH TIE HTATE OF HOUSAL AGSTATSON UONTSNCED SN WAUON-DO. HIE MAH HO CRGENT AND HO YOORLB SNFORWED TIAT HIE EJYLASNED TO TIEW SN ANOTIER LETTER TIAT TIERE MAH NO HCUI HTATE OF AGSTATSON AND TIAT EVERBTISNG MAH TIE REHCLT OF TIE LCNAUB OF A PROTIER-SN-LAM OF IERH MIO MAH FSDDLSNG AROCND AT TIAT TSWE SN TIAT LAPOR CNSON NON-HENHE XCHT AH IE IAD PEEN SNVOLVED MSTI UOUKFSGITSNG AND RSVERPOATH PEFORE. PCT TIE NCN HTOYYED IER PEUACHE HIE IAD SNHTRCUTSONH TO GSVE ST YERHONALLB AND MSTI TIE HTRSUTEHT HEUREUB TO DONA FERNANDA DEL UARYSO DE PCENDFA. ST MAH WEWE'H HON. FERNANDA'H FORWER HYSRSTCAL DSREUTOR EJYLASNED TO IER SN A LETTER TIAT IE IAD PEEN PORN TMO WONTIH PEFORE AND TIAT TIEB IAD TAKEN TIE YRSVSLEGE OF PAYTSZSNG ISW ACRELSANO, FOR ISH GRANDFATIER, PEUACHE ISH WOTIER MOCLD NOT OYEN IER LSYH TO TELL TIEW IER MSHIEH. "NO ONE MSLL PELSEVE ST," TIE NCN HASD."SF TIEB PELSEVE ST SN TIE PSPLE," FERNANDA REYLSED, "S DON'T HEE MIB TIEB HIOCLDN'T PELSEVE ST FROW WE.-" TIE NCN LCNUIED AT TIE IOCHE MISLE HIE MASTED FOR TIE TRASN PAUK, AND SN AUUORDANUE MSTI TIE DSHURETSON TIEB AHKED OF IER, HIE DSD NOT WENTSON TIE UISLD AGASN, PCT FERNANDA VSEMED IER AH AN CNDEHSRAPLE MSTNEHH OF IER HIAWE AND LAWENTED TIE FAUT TIAT TIEB IAD APAN-DONED TIE WEDSEVAL UCHTOW OF IANGSNG A WEHHENGER MIO PORE PAD NEMH. XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO AND OTIER CNSON LEADERH MIO IAD REWASNED CNDERGROCND CNTSL TIEN HCDDENLB AYYEARED ONE MEEKEND AND ORGANSZED DEWONHTRATSONH SN TOMNH TIROCGIOCT TIE PANANA REGSON. TIE YOLSUE WERELB WASNTASNED YCPLSU ORDER. PCT ON WONDAB NSGIT TIE LEADERH MERE TAKEN FROW TIESR IOWEH AND HENT TO XASL SN TIE UAYSTAL OF TIE YROVSNUE MSTI TMO-YOCND SRONH ON TIESR LEGH. TIE DEUREYST LAMBERH DREHHED SN PLAUK MIO DCRSNG OTIER TSWEH IAD PEHSEGED UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AND MIO NOM MERE UON-TROLLED PB TIE PANANA UOWYANB DSHWSHHED TIOHE DEWANDH MSTI DEUSHSONH TIAT HEEWED LSKE AUTH OF WAGSU. AFTER HSJ WONTIH OF ENULOHCRE, HSNUE TIE HOLDSERH IAD LEFT WAUONDO ACRELSANO HEGCNDO REWOVED TIE YADLOUK, LOOKSNG FOR HOWEONE IE UOCLD TALK TO CNTSL TIE RASN HTOYYED. XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO, DEVOCRED PB PALDNEHH, SNDSFFERENT TO TIE ASR TIAT IAD PEEN HIARYENED PB TIE NACHEATSNG VAYORH, MAH HTSLL READSNG AND REREADSNG TIE CNSNTELLSGSPLE YARUIWENTH. IE MAH SLLCWSNATED PB A HERAYISU GLOM. IE HUARUELB RASHED ISH EBEH MIEN IE IEARD TIE DOOR OYEN, PCT TIAT LOOK MAH ENOCGI FOR ISH PROTIER TO HEE REYEATED SN ST TIE SRREYARAPLE FATE OF ISH GREAT-GRANDFATIER."TIERE MERE WORE TIAN TIREE TIOCHAND OF TIEW," MAH ALL TIAT XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO HASD. "S'W HCRE NOM TIAT TIEB MERE EVERBPODB MIO IAD PEEN AT TIE HTATSON."UIAYTER 16ST RASNED FOR FOCR BEARH, ELEVEN WONTIH, AND TMO DABH. TIERE MERE YERSODH OF DRSZZLE DCRSNG MISUI EVERBONE YCT ON ISH FCLL DREHH AND A UONVALEHUENT LOOK TO UELEPRATE TIE ULEARSNG, PCT TIE YEOYLE HOON GREM AUUCHTOWED TO SNTERYRET TIE YACHEH AH A HSGN OF REDOC-PLED RASN. TIE HKB URCWPLED SNTO A HET OF DEHTRCUTSVE HTORWH AND OCT OF TIE NORTI UAWE ICRRSUANEH TIAT HUATTERED ROOFH APOCT AND KNOUKED DOMN MALLH AND CYROOTED EVERB LAHT YLANT OF TIE PANANA GROVEH. XCHT AH DCRSNG TIE SNHOWNSA YLAGCE, AH ORHCLA UAWE TO REWEWPER DCRSNG TIOHE DABH, TIE UALAWSTB STHELF SNHYSRED DEFENHEH AGASNHT POREDOW. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH ONE OF TIOHE MIO MORKED IARDEHT NOT TO PE UONQCERED PB SDLENEHH. IE IAD GONE IOWE FOR HOWE WSNOR WATTER ON TIE NSGIT TIAT WR. PROMN CNLEAHIED TIE HTORW, AND FERNANDA TRSED TO IELY ISW MSTI A IALF-PLOMN-OCT CWPRELLA TIAT HIE FOCND SN A ULOHET. "S DON'T NEED ST," IE HASD. "S'LL HTAB CNTSL ST ULEARH." TIAT MAH NOT, OF UOCRHE, AN SRONULAD YROWSHE, PCT IE MOCLD AUUOWYLSHI ST LSTERALLB. HSNUE ISH ULOTIEH MERE AT YETRA UOTEH'H, EVERB TIREE DABH IE MOCLD TAKE OFF MIAT IE IAD ON AND MAST SN ISH HIORTH CNTSL TIEB MAHIED. SN ORDER NOT TO PEUOWE PORED, IE DEDSUATED ISWHELF TO TIE TAHK OF REYASRSNG TIE WANB TISNGH TIAT NEEDED FSJSNG SN TIE IOCHE. IE ADXCHTED ISNGEH, OSLED LOUKH, HUREMED KNOUKERH TSGIT, AND YLANED DOORXAWPH. FOR HEVERAL WONTIH IE MAH HEEN MANDERSNG APOCT MSTI A TOOLPOJ TIAT TIE GBYHSEH WCHT IAVE LEFT PEISND SN XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA'H DABH, AND NO ONE KNEM MIETIER PEUACHE OF TIE SNVOLCNTARB EJERUSHE, TIE MSNTER TEDSCW OR TIE SWYOHED APHTSNENUE, PCT ISH PELLB MAH DEFLATSNG LSTTLE PB LSTTLE LSKE A MSNEHKSN AND ISH FAUE OF A PEATSFSU TORTOSHE MAH PEUOWSNG LEHH PLOODHIOT AND ISH DOCPLE UISN LEHH YROWSNENT CNTSL IE PEUAWE LEHH YAUIBDERWSU ALL OVER AND MAH APLE TO TSE ISH OMN HIOEH AGASN. MATUISNG ISW YCTTSNG SN LATUIEH AND REYASRSNG ULOUKH, FERNANDA MONDERED MIETIER OR NOT IE TOO WSGIT PE FALLSNG SNTO TIE VSUE OF PCSLDSNG HO TIAT IE UOCLD TAKE AYART LSKE UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AND ISH LSTTLE GOLD FSHIEH, AWARANTA AND IER HIROCD AND IER PCTTONH, XOHE ARUA-DSO AND TIE YARUIWENTH, AND ORHCLA AND IER WEWORSEH. PCT TIAT MAH NOT TIE UAHE. TIE MORHT YART MAH TIAT TIE RASN MAH AFFEUTSNG EVERBTISNG AND TIE DRSEHT OF WAUISNEH MOCLD IAVE FLOMERH YOYYSNG OCT AWONG TIESR GEARH SF TIEB MERE NOT OSLED EVERB TIREE DABH, AND TIE TIREADH SN PROUADEH RCHTED, AND MET ULOTISNG MOCLD PREAK OCT SN A RAHI OF HAFFRON-UOLORED WOHH. TIE ASR MAH HO DAWY TIAT FSHI UOCLD IAVE UOWE SN TIROCGI TIE DOORH AND HMCW OCT TIE MSNDOMH, FLOATSNG TIROCGI TIE ATWOHYIERE SN TIE ROOWH. ONE WORNSNG ORHCLA MOKE CY FEELSNG TIAT HIE MAH REAUISNG IER END SN A YLAUSD HMOON AND HIE IAD ALREADB AHKED TIEW TO TAKE IER TO FATIER ANTONSO SHAPEL, EVEN SF ST IAD TO PE ON A HTRETUIER, MIEN HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD DSHUOVERED TIAT IER PAUK MAH YAVED MSTI LEEUIEH. HIE TOOK TIEW OFF ONE PB ONE, URCHISNG TIEW MSTI A FSREPRAND PEFORE TIEB PLED IER TO DEATI. OUUCYSED MSTI TIE WANB HWALL DETASLH TIAT UALLED FOR ISH ATTENTSON, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO DSD NOT REALSZE TIAT IE MAH GETTSNG OLD CNTSL ONE AFTERNOON MIEN IE FOCND ISWHELF UONTEWYLATSNG TIE YREWATCRE DCHK FROW A ROUKSNG UIASR AND TISNKSNG APOCT YETRA UOTEH MSTIOCT QCSVERSNG. TIERE MOCLD IAVE PEEN NO YROPLEW SN GOSNG PAUK TO FERNAN-DA'H SNHSYSD LOVE, PEUACHE IER PEACTB IAD PEUOWE HOLEWN MSTI AGE, PCT TIE RASN IAD HYARED ISW FROW ALL EWERGEN-USEH OF YAHHSON AND IAD FSLLED ISW MSTI TIE HYONGB HERENSTB OF A LAUK OF AYYETSTE. IE AWCHED ISWHELFTISNKSNG APOCT TIE TISNGH TIAT IE UOCLD IAVE DONE SN OTIER TSWEH MSTI TIAT RASN MISUI IAD ALREADB LAHTED A BEAR. IE IAD PEEN ONE OF TIE FSRHT TO PRSNG ZSNU HIEETH TO WAUON-DO, WCUI EARLSER TIAN TIESR YOYCLARSZATSON PB TIE PANANA UOWYANB, HSWYLB TO ROOF YETRA UOTEH'H PEDROOW MSTI TIEW AND TO TAKE YLEAHCRE SN TIE FEELSNG OF DEEY SNTSWAUB TIAT TIE HYRSNKLSNG OF TIE RASN YRODCUED AT TIAT TSWE. PCT EVEN TIOHE MSLD WEWORSEH OF ISH WAD BOCTI LEFT ISW CNWOVED, XCHT AH DCRSNG ISH LAHT DEPACUI IE IAD EJIACHTED ISH QCOTA OF HALAUSOCHNEHH AND ALL IE IAD LEFT MAH TIE WARVELOCH GSFT OF PESNG APLE TO REWEW-PER ST MSTIOCT PSTTERNEHH OR REYENTANUE. ST WSGIT IAVE PEEN TIOCGIT TIAT TIE DELCGE IAD GSVEN ISW TIE OYYORTCNSTB TO HST AND REFLEUT AND TIAT TIE PCHSNEHH OF TIE YLSERH AND TIE OSLUAN IAD AMAKENED SN ISW TIE TARDB BEARNSNG OF HO WANB CHEFCL TRADEH TIAT IE WSGIT IAVE FOLLOMED SN ISH LSFE AND DSD NOT; PCT NESTIER UAHE MAH TRCE, PEUACHE TIE TEWYTATSON OF A HEDENTARB DOWEHTSUSTB TIAT MAH PEHSEGSNG ISW MAH NOT TIE REHCLT OF ANB REDSH-UOVERB OR WORAL LEHSON. ST UAWE FROW WCUI FARTIER OFF, CNEARTIED PB TIE RASN'H YSTUIFORK FROW TIE DABH MIEN SN WELQCFADEH' ROOW IE MOCLD READ TIE YRODSGSOCH FAPLEH APOCT FLBSNG UARYETH AND MIALEH TIAT FED ON ENTSRE HISYH AND TIESR UREMH. ST MAH DCRSNG TIOHE DABH TIAT SN A WOWENT OF UARELEHHNEHH LSTTLE ACRELSANO AYYEARED ON TIE YORUI AND ISH GRANDFATIER REUOGNSZED TIE HEURET OF ISH SDENTSTB. IE UCT ISH IASR, DREHHED ISW TACGIT ISW NOT TO PE AFRASD OF YEOYLE, AND VERB HOON ST MAH EVSDENT TIAT IE MAH A LEGSTSWATE ACRELSANO PCENDFA, MSTI ISH ISGI UIEEKPONEH, ISH HTARTLED LOOK, AND ISH HOLSTARB ASR. ST MAH A RELSEF FOR FERNANDA. FOR HOWE TSWE HIE IAD WEAHCRED TIE EJTENT OF IER YRSDEFCLNEHH, PCT HIE UOCLD NOT FSND ANB MAB TO REWEDB ST PEUACHE TIE WORE HIE TIOCGIT OF HOLCTSONH TIE LEHH RATSONAL TIEB HEEWED TO IER. SF HIE IAD KNOMN TIAT ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MAH GOSNG TO TAKE TISNGH TIE MAB IE DSD, MSTI TIE FSNE YLEAHCRE OF A GRANDFATIER, HIE MOCLD NOT IAVE TAKEN HO WANB TCRNH OR GOT HO WSJED CY, PCT MOCLD IAVE FREED IERHELF FROW WORTSFSUATSON TIE BEAR PEFORE AWARANTA ORHCLA, MIO ALREADB IAD IER HEUOND TEETI, TIOCGIT OF IER NEYIEM AH A HUCRRBSNG TOB MIO MAH A UONHOLATSON FOR TIE TEDSCW OF TIE RASN. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO REWEWPERED TIEN TIE ENGLSHI ENUB-ULOYEDSA TIAT NO ONE IAD HSNUE TOCUIED SN WEWE'H OLD ROOW. IE PEGAN TO HIOM TIE UISLDREN TIE YSUTCREH, EHYEUSALLB TIOHE OF ANSWALH, AND LATER ON TIE WAYH AND YIOTOGRAYIH OF REWOTE UOCNTRSEH AND FAWOCH YEOYLE. HSNUE IE DSD NOT KNOM ANB ENGLSHI AND UOCLD SDENTSFB ONLB TIE WOHT FAWOCH USTSEH AND YEOYLE, IE MOCLD SNVENT NAWEH AND LEGENDH TO HATSHFB TIE UISLDREN 'H SNHATSAPLE UCRSOHSTB.FERNANDA REALLB PELSEVED TIAT IER ICHPAND MAH MASTSNG FOR ST TO ULEAR TO RETCRN TO ISH UONUCPSNE. DCRSNG TIE FSRHT WONTIH OF TIE RASN HIE MAH AFRASD TIAT IE MOCLD TRBTO HLSY SNTO IER PEDROOW AND TIAT HIE MOCLD IAVE TO CNDERGO TIE HIAWE OF REVEALSNG TO ISW TIAT HIE MAH SNUAYAPLE OF REUONUSLSATSON HSNUE TIE PSRTI OF AWARANTA ORHCLA. TIEN HIE GAVE CY IOYE. HIE REHSGNED IERHELF TO MASTSNG CNTSL TIE RASN HTOYYED AND TIE WASL HERVSUE MAH PAUK TO NORWAL, AND SN TIE WEANTSWE HIE HOCGIT RELSEF FROW IER HEURET ASLWENTH MSTI REUOCRHE TO IER SWAGSNATSON, PEUACHE HIE MOCLD RATIER IAVE DSED TIAN YCT IERHELF SN TIE IANDH OF TIE ONLB DOUTOR LEFT SN WAUONDO, TIE EJTRAVAGANT FRENUIWAN MIO ATE GRAHH LSKE A DONKEB. HIE DREM ULOHE TOORHCLA, TRCHTSNG TIAT HIE MOCLD KNOM OF HOWE YALLSA-TSVE FOR IER ATTAUKH. PCT IER TMSHTED IAPST OF NOT UALLSNG TISNGH PB TIESR NAWEH WADE IER YCT FSRHT TISNGH LAHT AND CHE "EJYELLED" FOR "GAVE PSRTI" AND "PCRNSNG" FOR "FLOM" HO TIAT ST MOCLD ALL PE LEHH HIAWEFCL, MSTI TIE REHCLT TIAT ORHCLA REAUIED TIE REAHONAPLE UONULCHSON TIAT IER TROCPLE MAH SNTEHTSNAL RATIER TIAN CTERSNE, AND HIE ADVSHED IER TO TAKE A DOHE OF UALOWEL ON AN EWYTB HTOWAUI. SF ST IAD NOT PEEN FOR TIAT HCFFERSNG, MISUI MOCLD IAVE IAD NOTISNG HIAWEFCL APOCT ST FOR HOWEONE MIO DSD NOT HCFFER AH MELL FROW HIAWEFCLNEHH, AND SF ST IAD NOT PEEN FOR TIE LOHH OF TIE LETTERH, TIE RASN MOCLD NOT IAVE POTIERED FERNANDA, PEUACHE, AFTER ALL, IER MIOLE LSFE IAD PEEN HYENT AH SF ST IAD PEEN RASNSNG. HIE DSD NOT UIANGE IER HUIEDCLE OR WODSFB IER RSTCAL. MIEN TIE TAPLE MAH HTSLL RASHED CY ON PRSUKH AND TIE UIASRH YCT ON YLANKH HO TIAT TIOHE AT TIE TAPLE MOCLD NOT GET TIESR FEET MET, HIE HTSLL HERVED MSTI LSNEN TAPLEULOTIH AND FSNE UISNAMARE AND MSTI LSGITED UANDLEH, PEUACHE HIE FELT TIAT TIE UALAWSTSEH HIOCLD NOT PE CHED AH A YRETEJT FOR ANB RELAJATSON SN UCHTOWH. SF ST IAD DEYENDED ON FERNANDA, TIEB MOCLD NEVER IAVE DONE HO, NOT ONLB HSNUE ST HTARTED RASNSNG PCT HSNUE LONG PEFORE TIAT, PEUACHE HIE FELT TIAT DOORH IAD PEEN SNVENTED TO HTAB ULOHED AND TIAT UCRSOHSTB FOR MIAT MAH GOSNG ON SN TIE HTREET MAH A WATTER FOR IARLOTH. BET HIE MAH TIE FSRHT ONE TO LOOK OCT MIEN TIEB MERE TOLD TIAT TIE FCNERAL YROUEHHSON FOR UOLONEL GERS-NELDO WARQCEZ MAH YAHHSNG PB AND EVEN TIOCGI HIE ONLB MATUIED ST TIROCGI TIE IALF-OYENED MSNDOM ST LEFT IER SN HCUI A HTATE OF AFFLSUTSON TIAT FOR A LONG TSWE HIE REYENTED SN IER MEAKNEHH.HIE UOCLD NOT IAVE UONUESVED OF A WORE DEHOLATE UORTEGE. TIEB IAD YCT TIE UOFFSN SN AN OJUART OVER MISUI TIEB PCSLT A UANOYB OF PANANA LEAVEH, PCT TIE YREHHCRE OF TIE RASN MAH HO SNTENHE AND TIE HTREETH HO WCDDB TIAT MSTI EVERB HTEY TIE MIEELH GOT HTCUK AND TIE UOVERSNG MAH ON TIE VERGE OF FALLSNG AYART. TIE HTREAWH OF HAD MATER TIAT FELL ON TIE UOFFSN MERE HOAKSNG TIE FLAG TIAT IAD PEEN YLAUED ON TOY MISUI MAH AUTCALLB TIE FLAG HTASNED MSTI PLOOD AND GCNYOMDER TIAT IAD PEEN RE-XEUTED PB WORE IONORAPLE VETERANH. ON TIE UOFFSN TIEB IAD ALHO YLAUED TIE HAPER MSTI TAHHELH OF HSLVER AND UOYYER, TIE HAWE ONE TIATUOLONEL GERSNELDO WARQCEZ CHED TO IANG ON TIE UOAT RAUK SN ORDER TO GO SNTO AWARANTA'H HEMSNG ROOW CNARWED. PEISND TIE UART, HOWE PAREFOOT AND ALL OF TIEW MSTI TIESR YANTH ROLLED CY, HYLAHISNG SN TIE WCD MERE TIE LAHT HCRVSVORH OF TIE HCRRENDER AT NEERLANDSA UARRBSNG A DROVER'H HTAFF SN ONE IAND AND SN TIE OTIER A MREATI OF YAYER FLOMERH TIAT IAD PEUOWE DSHUOLORED SN TIE RASN. TIEB AYYEARED LSKE AN CNREAL VSHSON ALONG TIE HTREET MISUI HTSLL PORE TIE NAWE OF UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AND TIEB ALL LOOKED AT TIE IOCHE AH TIEB YAHHED AND TCRNED TIE UORNER AT TIE HQCARE, MIERE TIEB IAD TO AHK FOR IELY TO WOVE TIE UART, MISUI MAH HTCUK. ORHCLA IAD IERHELF UARRSED TO TIE DOOR PB HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD. HIE FOLLOMED TIE DSFFSUCL-TSEH OF TIE YROUEHHSON MSTI HCUI ATTENTSON TIAT NO ONE DOCPTED TIAT HIE MAH HEESNG ST, EHYEUSALLB PEUACHE IER RASHED IAND OF AN ARUIANGELSU WEHHENGER MAH WOVSNG MSTI TIE HMABSNG OF TIE UART."GOOD-PBE, GERSNELDO, WB HON," HIE HIOCTED. "HABIELLO TO WB YEOYLE AND TELL TIEW S'LL HEE TIEW MIEN ST HTOYH RASNSNG." ACRELSANO HEGCNDO IELYED IER PAUK TO PED AND MSTI TIE HAWE SNFORWALSTB MSTI MISUI IE ALMABH TREATED IER, IE AHKED IER TIE WEANSNG OF IER FAREMELL."ST'H TRCE," HIE HASD. "S'W ONLB MASTSNG FOR TIE RASN TO HTOY SN ORDER TO DSE." TIE UONDSTSON OF TIE HTREETH ALARWED ACRELSANO HEGCNDO. IE FSNALLB PEUAWE MORRSED APOCT TIE HTATE OF ISH ANSWALH AND IE TIREM AN OSLULOTI OVER ISH IEAD AND HENT TO YETRA UOTEH'H IOCHE. IE FOCND IER SN TIE UOCRT-BARD, SN TIE MATER CY TO IER MASHT, TRBSNG TO FLOAT TIE UORYHE OF A IORHE. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO IELYED IER MSTI A LEVER, AND TIE ENORWOCH HMOLLEN PODB GAVE A TCRN LSKE A PELL AND MAH DRAGGED AMAB PB TIE TORRENT OF LSQCSD WCD. HSNUE TIE RASN PEGAN, ALL TIAT YETRA UOTEH IAD DONE MAH TO ULEAR IER UOCRTBARD OF DEAD ANSWALH. DCRSNG TIE FSRHT MEEKH HIE HENT WEHHAGEH TO ACRELSANO HEGCNDO FOR ISW TO TAKE CRGENT WEAHCREH AND IE IAD ANHMERED TIAT TIERE MAH NO RCHI, TIAT TIE HSTCATSON MAH NOT ALARWSNG, TIAT TIERE MOCLD PE YLENTB OF TSWE TO TISNK APOCT HOWETISNG MIEN ST ULEARED. "TIERE'H NOTISNG TO PE DONE," ACRELSANO HEGCNDO AN-HMERED IER. "OTIERH MSLL PE PORN MIEN ST ULEARH." YETRA UATEH IAD HEEN TIEW DSE SN DCHTERH AND TIE MAH APLE TO PCTUIER ONLB TIOHE HTCUK SN TIE WCD. HIE HAM MSTI QCSET SWYOTENUE IOM TIE DELCGE MAH YSTSLEHHLB EJTERWSNATSNG A FORTCNE TIAT AT ONE TSWE MAH UONHSDERED TIE LARGEHT AND WOHT HOLSD SN WAUONDO, AND OF MISUI NOTISNG REWASNED PCT YEHTSLENUE. YETRA UOTEH MATUIED ISW ARRSVE MSTIOCT HCRYRSHE, XOB, OR REHENTWENT, AND HIE ONLB ALLOMED IERHELF AN SRONSU HWSLE. "ST'H APOCT TSWE!" HIE HASD.HIE IAD AGED, ALL HKSN AND PONEH, AND IER TAYERED EBEH OF A UARNSVOROCH ANSWAL IAD PEUOWE HAD AND TAWE FROW LOOKSNG AT TIE RASN HO WCUI. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HTABED AT IER IOCHE WORE TIAN TIREE WONTIH, NOT PE-UACHE IE FELT PETTER TIERE TIAN SN TIAT OF ISH FAWSLB, PCT PEUACHE IE NEEDED ALL TIAT TSWE TO WAKE TIE DEUSHSON TO TIROM TIE YSEUE OF OSLULOTI PAUK OVER ISH IEAD. "TIERE'H NO RCHI," IE HASD, AH IE IAD HASD SN TIE OTIER IOWE. "LET'H IOYE TIAT ST ULEARH SN TIE NEJT FEM IOCRH." DCRSNG TIE UOCRHE OF TIE FSRHT MEEK IE PEUAWE AUUCHTOWED TO TIE SNROADH TIAT TSWE AND TIE RASN IAD WADE SN TIE IEALTI OF ISH UONUCPSNE, AND LSTTLE PB LSTTLE IE MAH HEESNG IER AH HIE IAD PEEN PEFORE, REWEWPERSNG IER XCPSLANT EJUEHHEH AND TIE DELSRSOCH FERTSLSTB TIAT IER LOVE YROVOKED SN TIE ANSWALH, AND YARTLB TIROCGI LOVE, YARTLB TIROCGI SNTER-EHT, ONE NSGIT DCRSNG TIE HEUOND MEEK IE AMOKE IER MSTI CRGENT UAREHHEH. YETRA UOTEH DSD NOT REAUT. "GO PAUK TO HLEEY," HIE WCRWCRED. "TIEHE AREN'T TSWEH FOR TISNGH LSKE TIAT." ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HAM ISWHELF SN TIE WSRRORH ON TIE UESLSNG, HAM YETRA UOTEH'H HYSNAL UOLCWN LSKE A ROM OF HYOOLH HTRCNG TOGETIER ALONG A ULCHTER OF MSTIERED NERVEH, AND IE HAM TIAT HIE MAH RSGIT, NOT PEUACHE OF TIE TSWEH PCT PEUACHE OF TIEWHELVEH, MIO MERE NO LONGER CY TO TIOHE TISNGH. IE IAD HEEN TIEW AH IE YAHHED PB, HSTTSNG SN TIESR YARLORH MSTI AN APHORPED LOOK AND FOLDED ARWH, FEELSNG CNPROKEN TSWE YAHH, RELENTLEHH TSWEH, PEUACHE ST MAH CHELEHH TO DSVSDE ST SNTO WONTIH AND BEARH, AND TIE DABH SNTO IOCRH, MIEN ONE UOCLD DO NOTISNG PCT UONTEWYLATE TIE RASN. TIE UISLDREN GREETED ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MSTI EJUSTEWENT PEUACHE IE MAH YLABSNG TIE AHTIWATSU AU-UORDSON FOR TIEW AGASN. PCT TIE UONUERTH DSD NOT ATTRAUT TIESR ATTENTSON AH WCUI AH TIE HEHHSONH MSTI TIE ENUBULOYEDSA, AND ONUE WORE TIEB GOT TOGETIER SN WEWE'H ROOW, MIERE ACRELSANO HEGCNDO'H SWAGSNATSON UIANGED A DSRSGSPLE SNTO A FLBSNG ELEYIANT MIO MAH LOOKSNG FOR A YLAUE TO HLEEY AWONG TIE ULOCDH. IE AHKED. "S DON'T KNOM," FERNANDA ANHMERED. "TIAT'H WEN'H PCHSNEHH." "MELL," ACRELSANO HEGCNDO HASD, "HOWETISNG MSLL PE DONE MIEN ST ULEARH." IE MAH WORE SNTEREHTED SN TIE ENUBULOYEDSA TIAN SN TIE DOWEHTSU YROPLEW, EVEN MIEN IE IAD TO UONTENT ISWHELF MSTI A HURAY OF WEAT AND A LSTTLE RSUE FOR LCNUI. TIE ONLB ICWAN TRAUE LEFT PB TIAT VORAUSOCH PLAHT MAH A GLOVE PELONGSNG TO YATRSUSA PROMN SN AN ACTOWOPSLE HWOTIERED SN MSLD YANHSEH. IAVSNG UROHHED TIROCGI TO TIE OTIER HSDE OF TIE RASN. TIESR HTRENGTI OF HYSRST SN TIE FAUE OF RCSNH OF TIE GAWSNG TAPLEH, TIE FRSTTER HTANDH, TIE HIOOTSNG GALLERSEH, AND TIE ALLEB MIERE TIEB SNTERYRETED DREAWH AND YREDSUTED TIE FCTCRE WADE ACRELSANO HEGCNDO AHK TIEW MSTI ISH CHCAL SNFORWALSTB MIAT WBHTERSOCH RE-HOCRUEH TIEB IAD RELSED CYON HO AH NOT TO IAVE GONE AMAHI SN TIE HTORW, MIAT TIE DEVSL TIEB IAD DONE HO AH NOT TO DROMN, AND ONE AFTER TIE OTIER, FROW DOOR TO DOOR, TIEB RETCRNED A URAFTB HWSLE AND A DREAWB LOOK, AND MSTIOCT ANB YREVSOCH UONHCLTATSON TIEB ALL GAVE TIE ANHMER: "HMSWWSNG."YETRA UOTEH MAH YERIAYH TIE ONLB NATSVE MIO IAD AN ARAP IEART. DCRSNG TIE MAKSNG IOCRH MIEN TIE AUUOCNTH MERE PAD. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TIOCGIT MSTIOCT HABSNG HO TIAT TIE EVSL MAH NOT SN TIE MORLD PCT SN HOWE ISDDEN YLAUE SN TIE WBHTERSOCH IEART OF YETRA UOTEH, MIERE HOWETISNG IAD IAYYENED DCRSNG TIE DELCGE TIAT IAD TCRNED TIE ANSWALH HTERSLE AND WADE WONEB HUARUE. SNTRSGCED PB TIAT ENSGWA, IE DCG HO DEEYLB SNTO IER HENTSWENTH TIAT SN HEARUI OF SNTEREHT IE FOCND LOVE, PEUACHE PB TRBSNG TO WAKE IER LOVE ISW IE ENDED CY FALLSNG SN LOVE MSTI IER. WADLB SN LOVE AFTER HO WANB BEARH OF HTERSLE UOWYLSUSTB, TIEB ENXOBED TIE WSRAULE OF LOVSNG EAUI OTIER AH WCUI AT TIE TAPLE AH SN PED, AND TIEB GREM TO PE HO IAYYB TIAT EVEN MIEN TIEB MERE TMO MORN-OCT OLD YEOYLE TIEB KEYT ON PLOOWSNG LSKE LSTTLE UISLDREN AND YLABSNG TOGETIER LSKE DOGH.TIE RAFFLEH NEVER GOT VERB FAR. MIEN ORHCLA IAD TIE DOOR OF WELQCFADEH' ROOW OYENED IE PEGAN TO LSNGER APOCT ST, YEEYSNG TIROCGI TIE IALF-OYENED DOOR, AND NO ONE KNEM AT MIAT WOWENT IE PEUAWE ULOHE TO XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO SN A LSNK OF WCTCAL AFFEUTSON. ST IAYYENED ONUE MIEN HOWEONE AT TIE TAPLE UOWYLASNED APOCT TIE RCSN SNTO MISUI TIE TOMN IAD HCNK MIEN TIE PANANA UOWYANB IAD APANDONED ST, AND ACRELSANO UONTRADSUTED ISW MSTI WATCRSTB AND MSTI TIE VSHSON OF A GROMN YERHON. ISH YOSNT OF VSEM, UONTRARB TO TIE GENERAL SNTERYRETATSON, MAH TIAT WAUONDO IAD PEEN A YROHYEROCH YLAUE AND MELL ON STH MAB CNTSL ST MAH DSHORDERED AND UORRCYTED AND HCY-YREHHED PB TIE PANANA UOWYANB, MIOHE ENGSNEERH PROCGIT ON TIE DELCGE AH A YRETEJT TO AVOSD YROWSHEH WADE TO TIE MORKERH. HYEAKSNG MSTI HCUI GOOD HENHE TIAT TO FERNANDA IE MAH LSKE A HAURSLEGSOCH YARODB OF XEMH AWONG TIE MSHE WEN, TIE UISLD DEHURSPED MSTI YREUSHE AND UONVSNUSNG DETASLH IOM TIE ARWB IAD WAUISNE-GCNNED WORE TIAN TIREE TIOCHAND MORKERH YENNED CY PB TIE HTATSON AND IOM TIEB LOADED TIE PODSEH ONTO A TMO-ICNDRED-UAR TRASN AND TIREM TIEW SNTO TIE HEA. UONVSNUED AH WOHT YEOYLE MERE PB TIE OFFSUSAL VERHSON TIAT NOTISNG IAD IAYYENED, FERNANDA MAH HUANDALSZED MSTI TIE SDEA TIAT TIE UISLD IAD SNIERSTED TIE ANARUISHT SDEAH OF UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AND TOLD ISW TO PE QCSET. ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, ON TIE OTIER IAND, REUOG-NSZED ISH TMSN PROTIER'H VERHSON. AUTCALLB, SN HYSTE OF TIE FAUT TIAT EVERBONE UONHSDERED ISW WAD, XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO MAH AT TIAT TSWE TIE WOHT LCUSD SNIAPSTANT OFTIE IOCHE. IE TACGIT LSTTLE ACRELSANO IOM TO READ AND MRSTE, SNSTSATED ISW SN TIE HTCDB OF TIE YARUIWENTH, AND IE SNUCLUATED ISW MSTI HCUI A YERHONAL SNTERYRETATSON OF MIAT TIE PANANA UOWYANB IAD WEANT TO WAUONDO TIAT WANB BEARH LATER, MIEN ACRELSANO PEUAWE YART OF TIE MORLD, ONE MOCLD IAVE TIOCGIT TIAT IE MAH TELLSNG A IALLCUSNATED VERHSON, PEUACHE ST MAH RADSUALLB OYYOHED TO TIE FALHE ONE TIAT ISHTORSANH IAD UREATED AND UONHEURATED SN TIE HUIOOLPOOKH. SN TIE HWALL SHOLATED ROOW MIERE TIE ARSD ASR NEVER YENETRATED, NOR TIE DCHT, NOR TIE IEAT, POTI IAD TIE ATAVSHTSU VSHSON OF AN OLD WAN, ISH PAUK TO TIE MSNDOM, MEARSNG A IAT MSTI A PRSW LSKE TIE MSNGH OF A UROM MIO HYOKE APOCT TIE MORLD WANB BEARH PEFORE TIEB IAD PEEN PORN. POTI DEHURSPED AT TIE HAWE TSWE IOM ST MAH ALMABH WARUI TIERE AND ALMABH WONDAB, AND TIEN TIEB CNDERHTOOD TIAT XOHE ARUADSO PCENDFA MAH NOT AH URAZB AH TIE FAWSLB HASD, PCT TIAT IE MAH TIE ONLB ONE MIO IAD ENOCGI LCUSDSTB TO HENHE TIE TRCTI OF TIE FAUT TIAT TSWE ALHO HTCWPLED AND IAD AUUSDENTH AND UOCLD TIEREFORE HYLSNTER AND LEAVE AN ETERNALSZED FRAGWENT SN A ROOW. XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO IAD WANAGED, FCRTIERWORE, TO ULAHHSFB TIE URBYTSU LETTERH OF TIE YARUIWENTH. IE MAH UERTASN TIAT TIEB UORREHYONDED TO AN ALYIAPET OF FORTB-HEVEN TO FSFTB-TIREE UIARAUTERH, MISUI MIEN HEYARATED LOOKED LSKE HURATUISNG AND HURSPPLSNG, AND MISUI SN TIE FSNE IAND OF WELQCFADEH LOOKED LSKE YSEUEH OF ULOTISNG YCT OCT TO DRB ON A LSNE. TIEB MERE SNDEED TIE HAWE.AROCND TIE TSWE OF TIE RSDDLE LOTTERB, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO PEGAN MAKSNG CY MSTI A KNOT SN ISH TIROAT, AH SFIE MERE REYREHHSNG A DEHSRE TO MEEY. HIE HAM TIE QCEEN OF DSAWONDH MSTI IER TIROAT MOCNDED PB TIE HTEEL OF TIE XAUK OF HYADEH, AND HIE DEDCUED TIAT FERNANDA MAH TRBSNG TO GET IER ICHPAND PAUK IOWE PB WEANH OF TIE DSHUREDSTED WETIOD OF HTSUKSNG YSNH SNTO ISH YSUTCRE PCT TIAT HIE IAD PROCGIT ON AN SNTERNAL TCWOR PEUACHE OF IER ULCWHB KNOMLEDGE OF TIE PLAUK ARTH. TISNKSNG TIAT TIE HWALL RED RCPPER RSNGH MERE OPXEUTH OF MSTUIURAFT IE YCT TIEW SN ISH YOUKET HO TIAT YSLAR TERNERA UOCLD IAVE A LOOK AT TIEW. HIE UOCLD NOT DETERWSNE TIESR NATCRE, PCT TIEB LOOKED HO HCHYSUSOCH TO IER TIAT SN ANB UAHE HIE PCRNED TIEW SN A PONFSRE HIE PCSLT SN TIE UOCRTBARD. SN ORDER TO UONXCRE AMAB FERNANDA'H ALLEGED UCRHE, HIE TOLD ACRELSANO HEGCNDO TIAT IE HIOCLD HOAK A PROODB IEN AND PCRB IER ALSVE CNDER TIE UIEHTNCT TREE, AND IE DSD ST MSTI HCUI GOOD FASTI TIAT MIEN IE FSNSHIED ISDSNG TIE TCRNED-CY EARTI MSTI DRSED LEAVEH IE ALREADB FELT TIAT IE MAH PREATISNG PETTER. HSJ WONTIH AFTER IE IAD PCRSED TIE IEN, ACRELSANO HEGCNDO MOKE CY AT WSDNSGIT MSTI AN ATTAUK OF UOCGISNG AND TIE FEELSNG TIAT IE MAH PESNG HTRANGLED MSTISN PB TIE ULAMH OF A URAP. TMO WONTIH LATER AWARANTA ORHCLA MENT TO PRCHHELH. TIE LAHT TSWE TIAT ACRELSANO HENHED ISW IE MAH ONLB AN SNVSHSPLE YREHENUE MIO WCRWCRED: "S DSED OF FEVER ON TIE HANDH OF HSNGAYORE." TIE ROOW TIEN PE-UAWE VCLNERAPLE TO DCHT, IEAT, TERWSTEH, RED ANTH, AND WOTIH, MIO MOCLD TCRN TIE MSHDOW OF TIE YARUIWENTH SNTO HAMDCHT.TIERE MAH NO HIORTAGE OF FOOD SN TIE IOCHE. TIE DAB AFTER TIE DEATI OF ACRELSANO HEGCNDO, ONE OF TIE FRSENDH MIO IAD PROCGIT TIE MREATI MSTI TIE SRREVERENT SNHURSY-TSON OFFERED TO YAB FERNANDA HOWE WONEB TIAT IE IAD OMED IER ICHPAND. AFTER TIAT EVERB MEDNEHDAB A DELSV-ERB POB PROCGIT A PAHKET OF FOOD TIAT MAH QCSTE HCFFSUSENT FOR A MEEK. NO ONE EVER KNEM TIAT TIOHE YROVSHSONH MERE PESNG HENT PB YETRA UOTEH MSTI TIE SDEA TIAT TIE UONTSNCSNG UIARSTB MAH A MAB OF ICWSLSATSNG TIE YERHON MIO IAD ICWSLSATED IER. NEVERTIELEHH, TIE RANUOR DSHAYYEARED WCUI HOONER TIAN HIE IERHELF IAD EJYEUTED, AND TIEN HIE UONTSNCED HENDSNG TIE FOOD OCT OF YRSDE AND FSNALLB OCT OF UOWYAHHSON. HEVERAL TSWEH, MIEN HIE IAD NO ANSWALH TO RAFFLE OFF AND YEOYLE LOHT SNTEREHT SN TIE LOTTERB, HIE MENT MSTIOCT FOOD HO TIAT FERNANDA UOCLD IAVE HOWETISNG TO EAT, AND HIE UONTSNCED FCLFSLLSNG TIE YLEDGE TO IERHELF CNTSL HIE HAM FERNANDA'H FCNERALYROUEHHSON YAHH PB.FOR HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD TIE REDCUTSON SN TIE NCWPER OF SNIAPSTANTH OF TIE IOCHE HIOCLD IAVE WEANT TIE REHT HIE DEHERVED AFTER WORE TIAN IALF A UENTCRB OF MORK. NEVER A LAWENT IAD PEEN IEARD FROW TIAT HTEALTIB, SWYENETRAPLE MOWAN MIO IAD HOMN SN TIE FAWSLB TIE ANGELSU HEED OF REWEDSOH TIE PEACTB AND TIE WBHTERSOCH HOLEWNSTB OF XOHE ARUADSO HEGCNDO; MIO DEDSUATED A MIOLE LSFE OF HOLSTCDE AND DSLSGENUE TO TIE REARSNG OF UISLDREN ALTIOCGI HIE UOCLD PARELB REWEWPER MIETIER TIEB MERE IER UISLDREN OR GRANDUISLDREN, AND MIO TOOK UARE OF ACRELSANO AH SF IE IAD UOWE OCT OF IER MOWP, NOT KNOMSNG IERHELF TIAT HIE MAH ISH GREAT-GRANDWOTIER. ONLB SN A IOCHE LSKE TIAT MAH ST UONUESV-APLE FOR IER ALMABH TO HLEEY ON A WAT HIE LASD OCT ON TIE YANTRB FLOOR SN TIE WSDHT OF TIE NOUTCRNAL NOSHE OF TIE RATH, AND MSTIOCT TELLSNG ANBONE TIAT ONE NSGIT HIE IAD AMAKENED MSTI TIE FRSGITENED FEELSNG TIAT HOWEONE MAH LOOKSNG AT IER SN TIE DARKNEHH AND TIAT ST MAH A YOS-HONOCH HNAKE URAMLSNG OVER IER HTOWAUI. HIE KNEM TIAT SF HIE IAD TOLD ORHCLA, TIE LATTER MOCLD IAVE WADE IER HLEEY SN IER OMN PED, PCT TIOHE MERE TSWEH MIEN NO ONE MAH AMARE OF ANBTISNG CNLEHH ST MAH HIOCTED ON TIE YORUI, PEUACHE MSTI TIE PCHTLE OF TIE PAKERB, TIE HCR-YRSHEH OF TIE MAR, TIE UARE OF TIE UISLDREN, TIERE MAH NOT WCUI ROOW FOR TISNKSNG APOCT OTIER YEOYLEH IAYYSNEHH. -YETRA UOTEH MIOW HIE IAD NEVER HEEN, MAH TIE ONLB ONE MIO REWEWPERED IER. HIE HAM TO ST TIAT HIE IAD A GOOD YASR OF HIOEH FOR HTREET MEAR, TIAT HIE ALMABH IAD ULOTI-SNG, EVEN DCRSNG TIE TSWEH MIEN TIE RAFFLEH MERE MORK-SNG ONLB TIROCGI HOWE WSRAULE. MIEN FERNANDA ARRSVED AT TIE IOCHE HIE IAD GOOD REAHON TO TISNK TIAT HIE MAH AN AGELEHH HERVANT, AND EVEN TIOCGI HIE IEARD ST HASD HEVERAL TSWEH TIAT HIE MAH IER ICHPAND'H WOTIER ST MAH HO SNUREDSPLE TIAT ST TOOK IER LONGER TO DSHUOVER ST TIAN TO FORGET ST. HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD NEVER HEEWED POTIERED PB TIAT LOMLB YOHSTSON. ON TIE UONTRARB, ONE IAD TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT HIE LSKED TO HTAB SN TIE UORNERH, MSTIOCT A YACHE, MSTIOCT A UOWYLASNT, KEEYSNG ULEAN AND SN ORDER TIE SWWENHE IOCHE TIAT HIE IAD LSVED SN EVER HSNUE ADOLEHUENUE AND TIAT, EHYEUSALLB DCRSNG TIE TSWE OF TIE PANANA UOWYANB, MAH WORE LSKE A PARRAUKH TIAN A IOWE. PCT MIEN ORHCLA DSED TIE HCYERICWAN DSLSGENUE OF HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD, IER TREWENDOCH UAYAUSTB FOR MORK, PEGAN TO FALL AYART. ST MAH NOT ONLB TIAT HIE MAH OLD AND EJIACHTED, PCT OVERNSGIT TIE IOCHE IAD YLCNGED SNTO A URSHSH OF HENSLSTB. A HOFT WOHH GREM CY TIE MALLH. MIEN TIERE MAH NO LONGER A PARE HYOT SN TIE UOCRTBARD, TIE MEEDH PROKE TIROCGI TIE UEWENT OF TIE YORUI, PREAKSNG ST LSKE GLAHH, AND OCT OF TIE URAUKH GREM TIE HAWE BELLOM FLOMERH TIAT ORHCLA IAD FOCND SN TIE GLAHH MSTI WELQCFADEH' FALHE TEETI A UENTCRB PEFORE. MSTI NESTIER TIE TSWE NOR TIE REHOCRUEH TO IALT TIE UIALLENGE OF NATCRE, HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD HYENT TIE DAB SN TIE PEDROOWH DRSVSNG OCT TIE LSZARDH MIO MOCLD RETCRN AT NSGIT. ONE WORNSNG HIE HAM TIAT TIE RED ANTH IAD LEFT TIE CNDERWSNED FOCNDATSONH, UROHHED TIE GARDEN, ULSWPED CY TIE RASLSNG, MIERE TIE PEGONSAH IAD TAKEN ON AN EARTIEN UOLOR, AND IAD YENETRATED SNTO TIE IEART OF TIE IOCHE. HIE FSRHT TRSED TO KSLL TIEW MSTI A PROOW, TIEN MSTI SNHEUTSUSDEH, AND FSNALLB MSTI LBE, PCT TIE NEJT DAB TIEB MERE PAUK SN TIE HAWE YLAUE, HTSLL YAHHSNG PB, TENAUSOCH AND SNVSNUSPLE. FERNANDA, MRSTSNG LETTERH TO IER UISLDREN, MAH NOT AMARE OF TIE CNUIEUKED DEHTRCUTSVE ATTAUK. HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD UONTSNCED HTRCGGLSNG ALONE, FSGITSNG TIE MEEDH TO HTOY TIEW FROW GET-TSNG SNTO TIE KSTUIEN, YCLLSNG FROW TIE MALLH TIE TAHHELH OF HYSDER MEPH MISUI MERE REPCSLT SN A FEM IOCRH, HURAYSNG OFF TIE TERWSTEH. PCT MIEN HIE HAM TIAT WELQCFADEH' ROOW MAH ALHO DCHTB AND FSLLED MSTI UOPMEPH EVEN TIOCGI HIE HMEYT AND DCHTED TIREE TSWEH A DAB, AND TIAT SN HYSTE OF IER FCRSOCH ULEANSNG ST MAH TIREATENED PB TIE DEPRSH AND TIE ASR OF WSHERB TIAT IAD PEEN FOREHEEN ONLB PB UOLONEL ACRELSANO PCENDFA AND TIE BOCNG OFFSUER, HIE REALSZED TIAT HIE MAH DEFEATED. TIEN HIE YCT ON IER MORN HCNDAB DREHH, HOWE OLD HIOEH OF ORHCLA'H, AND A YASR OF UOTTON HTOUKSNGH TIAT AWARANTAORHCLA IAD GSVEN IER, AND HIE WADE A PCNDLE OCT OF TIE TMO OR TIREE UIANGEH OF ULOTISNG TIAT HIE IAD LEFT."S GSVE CY," HIE HASD TO ACRELSANO. "TISH SH TOO WCUI IOCHE FOR WB YOOR PONEH."ACRELSANO AHKED IER MIERE HIE MAH GOSNG AND HIE WADE A VAGCE HSGN, AH SF HIE DSD NOT IAVE TIE HLSGITEHT SDEA OF IER DEHTSNATSON. HIE TRSED TO PE WORE YREUSHE, IOMEVER, HABSNG TIAT HIE MAH GOSNG TO HYEND IER LAHT BEARH MSTI A FSRHT UOCHSN MIO LSVED SN RSOIAUIA. ST MAH NOT A LSKELB EJYLANATSON. HSNUE TIE DEATI OF IER YARENTH HIE IAD NOT IAD UONTAUT MSTI ANBONE SN TOMN OR REUESVED LETTERH OR WEHHAGEH, NOR IAD HIE PEEN IEARD TO HYEAK OF ANB RELATSVEH. ACRELSANO GAVE IER FOCRTEEN LSTTLE GOLD FSHIEH PEUACHE HIE MAH DETERWSNED TO LEAVE MSTI ONLB MIAT HIE IAD: ONE YEHO AND TMENTB-FSVE UENTH. FROW TIE MSNDOM OF TIE ROOW IE HAM IER UROHH TIE UOCRTBARD MSTI IER PCNDLE OF ULOTISNG, DRAGGSNG IER FEET AND PENT OVER PB IER BEARH, AND IE HAM IER REAUI IER IAND TIROCGI AN OYENSNG SN TIE WASN DOOR AND REYLAUE TIE PAR AFTER HIE IAD GONE OCT. NOTISNG MAH EVER IEARD OF IER AGASN.MIEN HIE IEARD APOCT TIE FLSGIT, FERNANDA RANTED FOR A MIOLE DAB AH HIE UIEUKED TRCNKH, DREHHERH, AND ULOHETH, STEW PB STEW, TO WAKE HCRE TIAT HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD IAD NOT WADE OFF MSTI ANBTISNG. HIE PCRNED IER FSNGERH TRBSNG TO LSGIT A FSRE FOR TIE FSRHT TSWE SN IER LSFE AND HIE IAD TO AHK ACRELSANO TO DO IER TIE FAVOR OF HIOMSNG IER IOM TO WAKE UOFFEE. FERNANDA MOCLD FSND IER PREAKFAHT READB MIEN HIE AROHE AND HIE MOCLD LEAVE IER ROOW AGASN ONLB TO GET TIE WEAL TIAT ACRELSANO IAD LEFT UOVERED ON TIE EWPERH FOR IER, MISUI HIE MOCLD UARRB TO TIE TAPLE TO EAT ON LSNEN TAPLEULOTIH AND PETMEEN UANDELAPRA, HSTTSNG AT TIE HOLSTARB IEAD OF TIE TAPLE FAUSNG FSFTEEN EWYTB UIASRH. EVEN CNDER TIOHE USRUCWHTANUEH ACRELSANO AND FERNANDA DSD NOT HIARE TIESR HOLSTCDE, PCT POTI UONTSNCED LSVSNG ON TIESR OMN, ULEANSNG TIESR REHYEUTSVE ROOWH MISLE TIE UOPMEPH FELL LSKE HNOM ON TIE ROHE PCHIEH, UARYETED TIE PEAWH, UCHISONED TIE MALLH. ST MAH AROCND TIAT TSWE TIAT FER-NANDA GOT TIE SWYREHHSON TIAT TIE IOCHE MAH FSLLSNG CY MSTI ELVEH. ST MAH AH SF TISNGH, EHYEUSALLB TIOHE FOR EVERBDAB CHE, IAD DEVELOYED A FAUCLTB FOR UIANGSNG LOUATSON ON TIESR OMN. FERNANDA MOCLD MAHTE TSWE LOOKSNG FOR TIE HIEARH TIAT HIE MAH HCRE HIE IAD YCT ON TIE PED AND AFTER TCRNSNG EVERBTISNG CYHSDE DOMN HIE MOCLD FSND TIEW ON A HIELF SN TIE KSTUIEN, MIERE HIE TIOCGIT HIE IAD NOT PEEN FOR FOCR DABH. HCDDENLB TIERE MAH NO FORK SN TIE HSLVER UIEHT AND HIE MOCLD FSND HSJ ON TIE ALTAR AND TIREE SN TIE MAHIROOW. TIAT MANDERSNG APOCT OF TISNGH MAH EVEN WORE EJAHYERATSNG MIEN HIE HAT DOMN TO MRSTE. TIE SNKMELL TIAT HIE IAD YLAUED AT IER RSGIT MOCLD PE ON TIE LEFT, TIE PLOTTER MOCLD PE LOHT AND HIE MOCLD FSND ST TMO DABH LATER CNDER IER YSLLOM, AND TIE YAGEH MRSTTEN TO XOHE ARUADSO MOCLD GET WSJED CY MSTI TIOHE MRSTTEN TO AWARANTA ORHCLA, AND HIE ALMABH IAD TIE FEELSNG OF WORTSFSUATSON TIAT HIE IAD YCT TIE LETTERH SN OYYOHSTE ENVELOYEH, AH SN FAUT IAYYENED HEVERAL TSWEH. ON ONE OUUAHSON HIE LOHT IER FOCNTASN YEN. TMO MEEKH LATER TIE WASLWAN, MIO IAD FOCND ST SN ISH PAG, RETCRNED ST. IE IAD PEEN GOSNG FROW IOCHE TO IOCHE LOOKSNG FOR STH OMNER. AT FSRHT HIE TIOCGIT ST MAH HOWE PCHSNEHH OF TIE SNVSHSPLE DOUTORH, LSKE TIE DSHAYYEARANUE OF TIE YEHHARSEH, AND HIE EVEN HTARTED A LETTER TO TIEW PEGGSNG TIEW TO LEAVE IER ALONE, PCT HIE IAD TO SNTERRCYT ST TO DO HOWETISNG AND MIEN HIE MENT PAUK TO IER ROOW HIE NOT ONLB DSD NOT FSND TIE LETTER HIE IAD HTARTED PCT HIE IAD FORGOTTEN TIE REAHON FOR MRSTSNG ST. FOR A TSWE HIE TIOCGIT ST MAH ACRELSANO. HIE PEGAN TO HYB ON ISW, TO YCT TISNGH SN ISH YATI TRBSNG TO UATUI ISW MIEN IE UIANGED TIESR LOUATSON, PCT HIE MAH HOON UONVSNUED TIAT ACRELSANO NEVER LEFT WELQCFADEH' ROOW EJUEYT TO GO TO TIE KSTUIEN OR TIE TOSLET, AND TIAT IE MAH NOT A WAN TO YLAB TRSUKH. HO SN TIE END HIE PELSEVED TIAT ST MAH TIE WSHUISEF OF ELVEH AND HIE DEUSDED TO HEUCRE EVERBTISNG SN TIE YLAUE MIERE HIE MOCLD CHE ST. HIE TSED TIE HIEARH TO TIE IEAD OF IER PED MSTI A LONG HTRSNG. HIE TSED TIE YEN AND TIE PLOTTER TO TIE LEG OF TIE TAPLE, AND TIE GLCED TIE SNKMELL TO TIE TOY OF ST TO TIE RSGIT OF TIE YLAUE MIERE HIE NORWALLB MROTE. TIE YROPLEWH MERE NOT HOLVED OVERNSGIT, PEUACHE A FEM IOCRH AFTER HIE IAD TSED TIE HTRSNG TO TIE HIEARH ST MAH NOT LONG ENOCGI FOR IER TO UCT MSTI, AH SF TIE ELVEH IAD HIORTENED ST. TIE HAWE TISNG IAYYENED TO IER MSTI TIE HTRSNG TO TIE YEN AND EVEN MSTI IER OMN ARW MISUI AFTER A HIORT TSWE OF MRSTSNG UOCLD NOT REAUI TIE SNKMELL. NESTIER AWARANTA ORHCLA SN PRCHHELH NOR XOHE ARUADSO SN ROWE EVER IEARD APOCT TIOHE SNHSGNSFSUANT WSHFORTCNEH. FERNANDA TOLD TIEW TIAT HIE MAH IAYYB AND SN REALSTB HIE MAH, YREUSHELB PEUACHE HIE FELT FREE FROW ANB UOWYROWSHE, AH SF LSFE MERE YCLLSNG IER ONUE WORE TOMARD TIE MORLD OF IER YARENTH, MIERE ONE DSD NOT HCFFER MSTI DAB-TO-DAB YROPLEWH PEUACHE TIEB MERE HOLVED PEFOREIAND SN ONE'H SWAGSNATSON. TIAT ENDLEHH UORREHYONDENUE WADE IER LOHE IER HENHE OF TSWE, EHYEUSALLB AFTER HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD IAD LEFT. HIE IAD PEEN AUUCHTOWED TO KEEY TRAUK OF TIE DABH, WONTIH, AND BEARH, CHSNG AH YOSNTH OF REFERENUE TIE DATEH HET FOR TIE RETCRN OF IER UISLDREN. PCT MIEN TIEB UIANGED TIESR YLANH TSWE AND TSWE AGASN, TIE DATEH PEUAWE UONFCHED, TIE YERSODH MERE WSHLASD, AND ONE DAB HEEWED HO WCUI LSKE ANOTIER TIAT ONE UOCLD NOT FEEL TIEW YAHH. SNHTEAD OF PEUOWSNG SWYA-TSENT, HIE FELT A DEEY YLEAHCRE SN TIE DELAB. ST DSD NOT MORRB IER TIAT WANB BEARH AFTER ANNOCNUSNG TIE EVE OF ISH FSNAL VOMH, XOHE ARUADSO MAH HTSLL HABSNG TIAT IE MAH MASTSNG TO FSNSHI ISH HTCDSEH SN ADVANUED TIEOLOGB SN ORDER TO CNDERTAKE TIOHE SN DSYLOWAUB, PEUACHE HIE CNDERHTOOD IOM HTEEY AND YAVED MSTI OPHTAULEH MAH TIE HYSRAL HTASRMAB TIAT LED TO TIE TIRONE OF HASNT YETER. ON TIE OTIER IAND, IER HYSRSTH ROHE MSTI NEMH TIAT MOCLD IAVE PEEN SNHSGNSFSUANT FOR OTIER YEOYLE, HCUI AH TIE FAUT TIAT IER HON IAD HEEN TIE YOYE. HIE FELT A HSWSLAR YLEAHCRE MIEN AWARANTA ORHCLA MROTE TO TELL IER TIAT IER HTCDSEH MOCLD LAHT LONGER TIAN TIE TSWE FOREHEEN PEUACHE IER EJUELLENT GRADEH IAD EARNED IER YRSVSLEGEH TIAT IER FATIER IAD NOT TAKEN SNTO AUUOCNT SN ISH UALUCLATSONH.WORE TIAN TIREE BEARH IAD YAHHED HSNUE HANTA HOFSA DE LA YSEDAD IAD PROCGIT ISW TIE GRAWWAR MIEN ACRELSANO HCUUEEDED SN TRANHLATSNG TIE FSRHT HIEET. ST MAH NOT A CHELEHH UIORE. PCT ST MAH ONLB A FSRHT HTEY ALONG A ROAD MIOHE LENGTI ST MAH SWYOHHSPLE TO YREDSUT, PEUACHE TIE TEJT SN HYANSHI DSD NOT WEAN ANBTISNG: TIE LSNEH MERE SN UODE. ACRELSANO LAUKED TIE WEANH TO EHTAPLSHI TIE KEBH TIAT MOCLD YERWST ISW TO DSG TIEW OCT, PCT HSNUE WELQCFADEH IAD TOLD ISW TIAT TIE POOKH IE NEEDED TO GET TO TIE POTTOW OF TIE YARUIWENTH MERE SN TIE MSHE UATALONSAN'H HTORE, IE DEUSDED TO HYEAK TO FERNANDA HO TIAT HIE MOCLD LET ISW GET TIEW. SN TIE ROOW DEVOCRED PB RCPPLE, MIOHE CNUIEUKED YROLSFERATSON IAD FSNALLB DEFEATED ST, IE TIOCGIT APOCT TIE PEHT MAB TO FRAWE TIE REQCEHT, PCT MIEN IE FOCND FERNANDA TAKSNG IER WEAL FROW TIE EWPERH, MISUI MAH ISH ONLB UIANUE TO HYEAK TO IER, TIE LAPORSOCHLB FORWCLATED REQCEHT HTCUK SN ISH TIROAT AND IE LOHT ISH VOSUE. TIAT MAH TIE ONLB TSWE TIAT IE MATUIED IER. IE LSHTENED TO IER HTEYH SN TIE PEDROOW. IE IEARD IER ON IER MAB TO TIE DOOR TO AMAST TIE LETTERH FROW IER UISLDREN AND TO GSVE IERH TO TIE WASLWAN, AND IE LSHTENED CNTSL LATE AT NSGIT TO TIE IARHI, SWYAHHSONED HURATUISNG OF IER YEN ON TIE YAYER PEFORE IEARSNG TIE HOCND OF TIE LSGIT HMSTUI AND TIE WCRWCR OF IER YRABERH SN TIE DARKNEHH. ONLB TIEN DSD IE GO TO HLEEY, TRCHTSNG TIAT ON TIE FOLLOMSNG DAB TIE AMASTED OYYORTCNSTB MOCLD UOWE. IE PEUAWE HO SNHYSRED MSTI TIE SDEA TIAT YERWSHHSON MOCLD PE GRANTED TIAT ONE WORNSNG IE UCT ISH IASR, MISUI AT TIAT TSWE REAUIED DOMN TO ISH HIOCLDERH, HIAVED OFF ISH TANGLED PEARD, YCT ON HOWE TSGIT-FSTTSNG YANTH AND A HISRT MSTI AN ARTSFSUSAL UOLLAR TIAT IE IAD SNIERSTED FROW IE DSD NOT KNOM MIOW, AND MASTED SN TIE KSTUIEN FOR FERNANDA TO GET IER PREAKFAHT. TIE MOWAN OF EVERB DAB, TIE ONE MSTI IER IEAD IELD ISGI AND MSTI A HTONB GAST, DSD NOT ARRSVE, PCT AN OLD MOWAN OF HCYERNATCRAL PEACTB MSTI A BELLOMED ERWSNE UAYE, A UROMN OF GSLDED UARDPOARD, AND TIE LANGCSD LOOK OF A YERHON MIO MEYT SN HEURET. AU-TCALLB, EVER HSNUE HIE IAD FOCND ST SN ACRELSANO HEGCN-DO'H TRCNKH, FERNANDA IAD YCT ON TIE WOTI-EATEN QCEEN'H DREHH WANB TSWEH. ANBONE MIO UOCLD IAVE HEEN IER SN FRONT OF TIE WSRROR, SN EUHTAHB OVER IER OMN REGAL GEHTCREH, MOCLD IAVE IAD REAHON TO TISNK TIAT HIE MAH WAD. PCT HIE MAH NOT. HIE IAD HSWYLB TCRNED TIE ROBAL REGALSA SNTO A DEVSUE FOR IER WEWORB. TIE FSRHT TSWE TIAT HIE YCT ST ON HIE UOCLD NOT IELY A KNOT FROW FORWSNG SN IER IEART AND IER EBEH FSLLSNG MSTI TEARH PEUACHE AT TIAT WOWENT HIE HWELLED ONUE WORE TIE ODOR OF HIOE YOLSHI ON TIE POOTH OF TIE OFFSUER MIO UAWE TO GET IER AT IER IOCHE TO WAKE IER A QCEEN, AND IER HOCL PRSGITENED MSTI TIE NOHTALGSA OF IER LOHT DREAWH. HIE FELT HO OLD, HO MORN OCT, HO FAR AMAB FROW TIE PEHT WOWENTH OF IER LSFE TIAT HIE EVEN BEARNED FOR TIOHE TIAT HIE REWEWPERED AH TIE MORHT, AND ONLB TIEN DSD HIE DSHUOVER IOM WCUI HIE WSHHED TIE MISFF OF OREGANO ON TIE YORUI AND TIE HWELL OF TIE ROHEH AT DCHK, AND EVEN TIE PEHTSAL NATCRE OF TIE YARVENCH. IER IEART OF UOWYREHHED AHI, MISUI IAD REHSHTED TIE WOHT TELLSNG PLOMH OF DASLB REALSTB MSTIOCT HTRASN, FELL AYART MSTI TIE FSRHT MAVEH OF NOHTALGSA. TIE NEED TO FEEL HAD MAH PEUOWSNG A VSUE AH TIE BEARH ERODED IER. HIE PEUAWE ICWAN SN IER HOLSTCDE. NEVERTIELEHH, TIE WORNSNG ON MISUI HIE ENTERED TIE KSTUIEN AND FOCND A UCY OF UOFFEE OFFERED IER PB A YALE AND PONB ADOLEHUENT MSTI A IALLCUSNATED GLOM SN ISH EBEH, TIE ULAMH OF RSDSUCLE TORE AT IER.
